  Okukuqala nje ngithanda ukubonga uMvelingqangi ngokungipha unandla okwenza 10 msebenzi. Ngibonga ozakwethu abangisizile befunda 10 nsebenzi izahluko nezahluko, uSolwazi PJ Zungu, uGugulethu Mazibuko, IGugulethu Mkhize, uSfiso Gumede. Ngiphinde ngidlulise ukubonga cozakwethu bonke Esikoleni Sezifundo ZesiZulu eThusini, eMgungundlovu laseWestville ngokungeseka ngibhala 10 msebenzi. Ngibonga kakhulu ,bafundi ebesibambisene nabo ababambe iqhaza elilthulu kulo msebenzi, 
abo ngoWiseman Nzama, Zethembe Mpungose noZinWe Nkosi. Ngibonga "Ikhulu kuStaff Shabalala ngokungifundela wonke 10 msebenzi eqinisekisa ll<:uthi awunamaphutha. 
  Ukubonga kwami okukhulu kuya kubafundi ababefunda ukuWelwa kolimi myakeni wesithathu, kwaHonours kanjalo nakwabeMasters. Laba bafundi Tibona ababambe iqhaza elikhulu ekutheni kuphume 10 msebenzi njengoba 
Jese sisebenze nabo iminyaka eyisishiyagalolunye edlule. Baningi-ke abafundi lbafunde ukuWelwa kolimi, angeke ngibagagule ngamagama. Muningi kakhulu rmsebenzi ebese siwenzile nabo ongavelile kule ncwadi oyovela emqulwini llandelayo. 
  Ngibonga kakhulu kuDokotela Nkosinathi Hlongwa, umyeni wami 19okungisingatha abuye awufunde 10 msebenzi ngesilthathi ngiwubhala. \lgibonga amadodakazi ami uNomfundo noS'ne, abaEma bami uBongani lOSbonelo ngokwamukela futhi bangelekelele kulo msebenzi. 


lSANDULELO 
Uthando lokufunda ngezilimi kanye nemithetho elawula ukusebenza 
kolimi lwaqala ngonyaka we-l 999 ngesilthathi kuvakashela uDokotela NonWanWa Mkhulisi esilthungweni semfundo iWestville emhlanganweni okwakungowokucobelelana ngolwazi. Ngaleso sikhathi wabe enguMqondisi Wezilimi Kuzwelonke. Wethula inkulumo eyangithinta kakhulu lapho ayegcizela khona ukuthi ulimi luyisilthali ongakwazi ukuthi ngaso unike umuntu amandla noma umamuke amandla. Inkulumo yakhe yayigxile eqhazeni leMinyango yezilimi ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme kanye nasekwakhiweni kwamathuba emisebenzi. Wagcizela iphuzu lokuthi asingagcini nje ngokufundisa uWelo lolimi (insebenwzakhi, inguqukomsindo, uWelomisho njll) kuphela kodwa kumele uWdo siluWanganise nemilthakha emisha engathuthukisa futhi iqeqeshe abafundi emakhonweni amaningi njengokuba ngotolika, ababumushi, abahleli bolimi, abakhiqizi bobuchwepheshe bolimi. 
Le nkulumo yalandelwa unIWangano wesibili owabe ungukhukhulelangoqo owawubanjelwe eThekwini owawubizwa nge-Language Indaba ngonyaka wezi-2000. Ngaqala lapho-ke ukuzibandakanya nasekufundeni ngokuWelwa kolimi. Imihlangano eminye eminingi esasibuye siyethamele yayibuye iWelwe yiBhodi Yezilimi Zonke ZaseNingizimu Afrika eyayiba se Tshwane (ePitoli) ngaleso silthathi. Emva kokufunda imibiko eminingi yoMnyango Wewbuciko Namasiko mayelana nokuWelwa kolimi eNingizimu Afrika, ikakhulukazi umbiko owenziwa ikomidi i-LANGTAG (1996) elaliholwa nguDokotela uNeville Alexander, ngasungula isifundo sokuWelwa kolimi. Ngenyanga kaAgasti 2001 ithimba elifundisa isayensi yolimi lomphakathi Esikoleni Sezilimi esilthungweni iDurban- Westville saba nenkuthazakwenza ngokulIlelwa 
kolimi. Sasimeme ozakwethu ezikhungweni ezahlukene zemfundo ephakeme esifundazweni saKwaZulu-Natali kubandakanya namaTechnikon. Kuzwelonke sasimeme umqondisi wokuWelwa kolimi u-Anne-Mari~ Beukes. Ikomidi lolimi lesifundazwe saKwaZulu-Natali nalo lalinyingxenye yale nkuthazakwenza. Ababemele izikhungo zemfundo ephakeme bavuma ngo 'E1ethu' ekutheni kwenziwe imizamo yokuthuthukisa ubuliminingi ezikhungweni zethu. Ngenyanga kaSepthemba 2002 saba nenkuthazakwenza yesibili eyabe iWola ukuthi sekulIanjwe indlela engakanani. Umbiko ngale nkuthazakwenza sawushicilela ngonyaka wezi-2003 (Ndimande, Desai and Ramsay-Brijball 2003). 
Ngizibandakanye emakomidini ahIukene abebhekele ukuWelwa kolimi

kwaba nesidingo sokumi kube nekomidi elalihlela ulimi bese liqhamuka nenqubomgomo yolimi. Ngaba ngomunye owaba kulelo komidi elasebenza kanzima iminyaka emithamu. 

   Kunezihloko eziningi engizishiyile engingabhalanga ngazo ngoba ngikholelwa ukumi zingaba yizincwadi ngokwazo njengepolitiki yolimi, izilimi wmdabu zase-Afrika nomnomo. Umsebenzi omningi olapha kule ncwadi bewungucwaningo ebengilwenza eminyakeni edlule nengisalwenza namanje. 

   Inhloso yale ncwadi ukuveza indima eseyihanjiwe ekumumukiseni ubuliminingi eNingizimu Afrika nguhulumeni, izifundazwe, iminyango eyahlukene kanjalo naseNyuvesi yaKwaZulu7Natali njengesikhungo seMfundo ephakeme. Incwadi ibhalelwe abafundi abafunda ngokuhielwa kolimi kanjalo nalabo abasebenza ngolimi noma ngokuhlelwa kolimi ezikhungweni zabo. Iwbasiza kakhulu labo abasahlongoza ukuqhamuka nenqubomgomo yolimi ..

   Ziningi izazi zilimi okuyizona ezibambe iqhaza eJikhulu ekufundweni kolimi. Lezi zazi ziJimi ngoNkabinde, Nyembezi, Nkosi, CeJe, Doke, Cope, Finnegan kanye nabanye abaningi esingeke sabaqeda. Ngengqikithi yenkulumo yona kusuke kuqondiswe esimweni lapho umuntu eyaye asebenzise noma aphimise amagama, amabinzana nemisho. 

   Ulimi JuyindleJa abantu abakwaziyo ukuthi baxhumane ngayo. Lokhu akusho ukuthi abantu baxhuman~ ngoJimi kupheJa, kodwa bayakwazi ukuxhumana ngokusebenzisa izimpawu benga,zange bakhulume. Ulimi namanje lusabambe iqhaza eJikhulu ekutheni abantu baphile ngendJeJa abaphila ngayo manje. 

   NgokwencazeJo enikezwa nguRadebe noMchunu (I989: 6) ulimi Jungachazwa njengempimiso yemisindo ezwakalayo nebonakalayo, equkethe imicabango nokusebenza kwengqondo yomuntu. Kungabe kuyini ukuhlelwa kolimif 
   Ukuhlelwa kolimi kuchazwa njengemizamo egunyaziwe kahulumeni ethatha isikhathi eside yokushintsha ukusebenza kwezilimi emphakathini ngesizathu sokusombulula izinkinga zokuxhumana (Weinstein, 1980: 
56). Ngokwe-Eric Digest ku: http://www.ericftcility.net/tktabases/ERICDigestled303051.html. Ukuhlelwa kolimi ngumsebenzi kahulumeni osemthethweni ophathelene nokuqokwa kanye nokuthuthukiswa kolimi noma izilimi zokuphatha. Ukuhlelwa kolimi kungurilkhakha osathuthuka obuka ulimi njengensizakusebenza emphakathini. Kukhombisa iqhaza elibanjwa ngabantu abathize noma izinhlangano ezinamandla okuthuthukisa nokusebenzisa ulimi. 
  Ukuhlelwa kolimi kanye nemithetho yolimi emazingeni a1ingene kubheka kakhulu izinto ezincine eziqondene nolimi njengokuthi imithombo yolwazi kufanele igcine hlobo luni lwezincwadi futhi ngaluphi ulimi. Kungagcinwa maphi amaphephandaba, ezikoleni kufanele kufundiswe ziphi izilimi. Yiziphi izilimi okufanele zisetshenziswe ukudayisa imikhiqizo ethile. Ziningi izincazelo ababhali abaqhamuka nazo zokuhlelwa kolimi. Nazi izin=lo ezitholakele: Ngokujwayelekile ukuhlelwa kolimi kwahlukene kabili, kodwa uCooper (1989) ukwahlukanise kathathu. 
N gaphambi kokuveza lezi zindlela kuhle ukuthi kuchazwe ukuthi

4. Kwabezombusazwe (Abezepolitiki) 
5. Ezemfundo 
6. Ezomnotho (Ukuhwebelana) 
7. Ezenhlalo yabantu kanye neziphathi-mandla zolimi

uhulumeni (inqubomgomo kazwelonke) maqondana nokusetshenziswa kolimi njengokuthi yiluphi ulimi oluzosetshenziselwa ukufunda nokufundisa. Yiziphi izilimi ezizosebenza esifundazweni njl!. UCrawford (2000: 1) naye uyahambisana nale ncazelo ngoba uthi inqubomgomo yolimi yilokho uhulumeni akwenzayo ngokusemthethweni ngokukhipha umthetho, izinqumo zenkantolo noma nje ngezinye izindlela ukuthatha isinqumo sokuthi izilimi zizosetshenziswa kanjani emphakathini, kuhlolwe amakhono olimi adingekayo bese kutholwa amalungelo abanru okufunda, basebenzise futhi balonde ulimi. 
Ulimi [wesigodi 
  Ulimi lwesigodi luwulimi olususelwa olimini olulodwa olusemthethweni kodwa lona olukhulunywa rigokwehlukile kulolo olusemthethweni 
kuye ngesifunda leso abakhulumi asebehlala kuso. Ukwehlukana kwalo kubonakala ekuphinyisweni kwezinhlamvu zamagama, ngephimbo, ngamagama asetshenziswa ngaliakhulumi, ngefonoloji, ngemofoloji, ngangokulandelana kwamagama emishweni. Ulimi lwesigodi luqala lapho ulimi oselukhulunywa luqhekeka kabili noma ngaphezulu okudalwa ngabakhulumi. 
Ukuphungula izi[imi 
  Lapha umkhulumi uqala enekhono lokukhuluma izilimi ezingaphezu kolulodwa kodwa aye ngokuya eziyeka lezi ezinye izilimi aze agcine esekhuluma ulimi olulodwa kuphela. Lezi ezinye izilimi ugcina esezikhohliwe esazi ulimi olulodwa kuphela. 
Ukwandisa izilimi 
  Ukwandisa izilimi kuchazwa nguLuckett (1995:'''75) njengokuthasisela inani lezilimi kulezo umkhulumi asuke esezazi. Uma umkhulumi wolimi kade azi izilimi ezintathu uyaye aphokophelele ukufunda nezinye izilimi ukuze akhulise ulwazi lwakhe. Phela akuwukhulisi umqondo womkhulumi wolimi ukwazi ulimi olulodwa kuphela. Indlela abakhulumi bezilimi ngezilimi abacabanga ngayo ayefani. Yilabo nalabo banikazi bolimi bafunda lukhulu kubakhulumi bolunye ulimi. 






Ikuze akwazi ukukhuluma ijagoni, kufanele abe nesitiflketi esihlonza okho. Iwulimi oluqondwa yilabo bantu abathile bodwa (njengodokot<;1a lamakhambi nje) olubenza bezwane bodwa kodwa abaseceleni bangezwa IOkuthi bathini. 
Ikriyoli 
  NgokukaNhlumayo (1999: 9) ikriyoli ivela lapho kukhona imiphakathi :xubile esebenzisa iphijini njengolimi lokuxhumana. Abantwana abazalwa apha bakhula bekhuluma lolu limi kube sengathi ulimi lwabo. Iphijini isuke siwulimi lwabantu bendawo leyo isifana nolimi lokuqala izingane eziluncela :beleni. 
Iphijini 
Iphijini ngokubhala kukaNhlumayo (1999: 9) wulimi olusetshenziswa 
* izinhlanga ezahlukene ukuze zikwazi ukuxhumana njengasezimayini. Iba ndlela abantu abaxhumana ngayo ngoba lungekho ulimi olujwayelekile okuxhumana. Ulimi lwesiFanakaIo lwaqhamuka kanjalo. 
Abahleli bolimi 
  Ngesizathu sokuthi ukuhIelwa kolimi kubheka kakhulu izinkinga :ziphathelene nomphakathi nokuphathwa kwezwe, abahlaziyi bezombusazwe =ye nabahlaziyi benhlalo yomphakathi bayaye bahlole ukuthi kukhona yini lkungenziwa. lzazi zilimi rona zingabamba iqhaza lapho sekuhlolwa isidingo okuhlelwa kolimi. Izinqumo zokuhlelwa kolimi ziyadingeka lapho kunezilimi :ziningi ezahlukene ezingatholi amalungelo nokusetshenziswa ngendlela :linganayo. Ulimi lungahlelwa ngabalandelayo: Uhulumeni, abasezikhundleni :ziphezulu, abezemfundo, izinhlangano ezizimele kanye nabathile abanegalelo :kuhIelweni kolimi. Emazweni ase-Mrika ukuhlelwa kolimi yinto endala :yaqala ngesikhathi lawa mazwe ethola uzimele geqe emva konyaka we-I960. 
  Bathathu abantu abaqhamuke nezindlela eziyisisekelo ekuhlelweni mlimi, labo ngoHaugen (1983), Haarman (1990) kanye noCooper (1989). Jkuhlelwa kolimi kungahlukaniswa kathathu: Ukuhlela izinga lolimi 
Status planning) Ukuhlela ikhophasi (Corpus planning). Ukuhlela ukufunda IOkwamukelwa kolimi (Acquisition planning). 


ngayo. Uma kuhlelwa izinga lolimi kuthathwa izinqumo ezinqala ngolimi okumele lube semthethweni emikhakheni eyehlukene yempilo. Kurochazwa kabanzi ngalesi sigaba esahlukweni sesishiyagalombili. 
Ukuhlela ikhophasi 
   Lesi sigaba sokuhlelwa kolimi sigxile esakhiweni sangaphakathi solimi uqobo lwalo. Uma kukhulunywa ngokuhlelwa kwekhophasi, kusuke kuqondiswe ikakhulukazi emizamweni yokwakha ulimi njengomsebenzi wokwakha amagama amasha ukuze kugcine kuvele izichazimagama, umkhankaso wokubhalwa kwezincwadi robucikomazwi. Akugcini 
lapho kuphela kodwa kubhekwa nokuthi ulimi luphuculwa kanjani bese Iuvanyiswa emphakathini, (Cooper 1989). UBraam (2004: 14) yena uthi ukuhlela ikhophasi kubandaIcinya ukwenza busha nokucubungulisisa isakhiwo solimi ukuze sihambisane nokuthuthuka kwesayensi nobuchwepheshe . 
Ukuhlela ukufundwa nokwamukelwa kolimi 
  UCooper (1989) uthi lapha kulolu hlobo lokuhlela kusuke kukhulunywa ngemizamo ehlelekile yokuthuthukisa ukufundwa kolimi. Lokhu kufunda kungenzeka ezikoleni, emaNyuvesi noma ezikhungweni ezizimele nezikahulumeni. 
Uma kuhlelwa ulimi miningi imiburo eyaye ibuzwe njengalena: 
1. Lungahlelwa kanjani ulimi? 
2. Ngubani okufanele aluhlele? 
   UCooper (1989: 182) uthi ukuhlela ulimi kuyefana nokuhlela umphakathi. Izinqumo ezithathwayo ngolimi, ukusebenza kwalo, izinga kanye nokuthuthuka kolimi kufanele kube ezibalulekile: 
* Ngokwenhlalo yabantu 	,', 
* Ngokomnotho 
* Ngokwemfundo 
* Nangokwerombusazwe

isempini yokulwela inkululeko lapha eNingizimu Mrika umunru lsebenzisa noma yiluphi uhlobo lwesikhali esikhona. Inkinga yolimi , lyihambi yodwa kodwa kunemixhanrela eminingi ekhona esingabala kuyo:

Uma kuhlelwa ulimi aluhlelelwa umphakathi noma izwe futhi 
Juhlelelwa emazingeni kazwelonke kuphela kodwa nasemazingeni 
phansi luyahlelwa, okungaba ngokwenkolo noma ezikhungweni nje zizimele. Uma senza ukuhlelwa kolimi kube yinto kahulumeni sivalela bantu abaningi amathuba okubamba iqhaza. Abahleli bolimi abafuni lkubandakanya izikhungo ezincane ezifana nezikole, amakhaya kanye lamasonto ekuhlelweni kolimi yize noma ukuhlelwa kolimi kwenzeka kulezi indawo. * Owokuchaza

   INingizimu Mrika yona iqoke ukuthi iphume yodwa eceleni isebenzise izilimi eziyishumi nanye njengezilimi ezisemrhethweni. Kunokwenzeka-ke ukuthi akukho ezinhlelweni zikahulumeni ngempela ukuzithuthukisa lezi zilimi noma azame ukuthi azirhuthukise kodwa ehluleke. lmindeni yezilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika 
   Udaba lomndeni wezilimi zase-Mrika ludala ngoba lususelwa esikhathini lapho sekuqaliwe ukusetshenzwa kwamatshe (Stone Age). Imindeni yezilimi zase-Mrika yahlukaniswa ka.f1e, ngale ndlela: Umndeni wokuqala i-MroAsiatic noma i-Mrasian, owesibili umndeni omkhulu obizwa ngokurhi iNiger-Kordofanian. Ngaphansi kwalo mndeni kukhona umndeni wezilimi iNiger-Congo kanye neKodorfanian. Umndeni wesithathu iNiio-Saharan kanti umndeni wesine owezilimi zabaThwa (Ndimande 200l). 
Umndeni weNiger-Kordofanian 
   NgokukaGregerson (1977: 112) Izilimi zeNiger-Kordofanian zikhulunywa ngabantu ababalelwa kulOO 000000. Ngonyaka wezi-2009 i-ACALAN iveza ukurhi lesi sibalo sesiphilldekile njengoba sebebalelwa ku200 000000. Izilimi ezikhulunywa ngaphansi kwalo mndeni zingaphezu kwenkulungwane. IKordofanian ithatha abantu abangu 200 000. INiger-Congo itharha sonke isamba esisele. Isigaba sabantu sinezilimi ezingamalrhulu amane (400) okungabantu ababalelwa ku 60, 000 000. Izilimi ezirholakala lapha ziyizilimi ezihlanganisayo kanti ezaseNtshonaianga neSudani ziyahlukanisa. Izilimi zomndeni wabantu zonke zinephimbo. Kulezo ezikhulunywa eNingizimu Mrika imvamisa,zinongwaqa-baThwa abathekelwe ezilimini zaba Thwa. Ezilimini ezingamashumi amatharhu nesikhombisa, isigidi, I 000 000 sazo sakhiwa ngabantu abatholakala e-Mrika.

   Ngokubhala kukaGregersen (1977: 116) i-Mro-Asiatic yinto eyodwa neSemitic noma iHamito-Semitic. Izilimi ezingena kumaHamitic yilezi: 
Berber, ezaseGibhithe, neKushitic. Inani labantu abalrhuluma lezi zilimi

ana inani lingu 10 000 000, inani elingu 9 000 000 likhuluma iHausa. nani labanru abakhuluma IKhushiric lingu 6 000 000. Erhiopia bangu 
, 500 000. Ezigabeni ezinhlanu ze-Afro-Asiatic, zimbili kuphela izilimi zisebenzisa iphimbo uma kukhulunywa. Lezo zilimi iChadic neKushitic.

Inani labanru seliphelele ngu II 000000. Izilimi ezitholakala lapha zibalelwa ku-I40, ezinye zazo ibandakanya lezi ezilandelayo:

2. iLuo

Ulimi olusemthethweni 
   Umunru angeze athembela kakhulu ezilimini zezigodi ngoba kakade zithathwa ngokuthi azikakabi semmethweni noma azikemukeleki. Kunohlobo lolimi okuyilona olukhulunywa ngokuvelele kulelo nalelo qembu labakhulumi bolimi. Lugqama kangangoba yilona olugcina seluthathwa njengolimi olusemthethweni. Lolu limi luhlonis~wa. kakhul~. Lokhu kuhlonishwa kwalo kuyivelakancane ngoba akuhamblsam nokuthl umkhulumi ukhuluma luphi ulimi uma esekhaya. Ulimi olusemthethweni luba nezimpawu ezithathwa ngokuthi ezekhethelo ezethekelwe kuzo zonke izinhlobo zokukhuluma ezikhona ezilimini zezigodi ezahlukahlukene. Yingako kuyiphutha elikhulu ukubukela phansi izilimi .zezigodi ngoba yizo ezizala ulimi olusemthethweni. Ulimi olusemthethwem lubonakala ngokuba nobhalojikelele lwalo, inguqukomsindo, insebenzozakhi noma imofoloji, uhlelomisho, isemantiksi, nokufana komqondo wamagama atholakala kuzo zonke izilimi zezigodi ngezigodi zolimi olulodwa uma sez~didiyelwe. Yo~k~ Ie ndidiyela ihlelwa kahle ilandele imithetho ethize. ~emlbhalo yalolu hml iyoqukatha loko okumayelana nesiko laleso sizwe, inkolo nezinkolelo zaso, imilando yaleso sizwe, naleyo yawoyise mkhulu. 
Ubnbi bolimi olnthathwa ngoknthi olusemthethweni 
   Noma sebephoqwe kangakanani abantu ukuthi balukhulume lolu limi kodwa abanru bayoqhubeka nokukhuluma izilimi zabo zezigodi ngoba abanru abayi nganxanye bengemanzi. Kunezizathu eziningi ezingenza abantu balushaye indiva ulimi olusemthethweni. Uma bebona u.kuthi 




e/~ma ukuyisho. Kuyenzeka futhi umkhulumi athande ukusebenzisa igama ehngekho uma ebona ukuthi lelo elisemthethweni seliyisidala uzohlekwa ngabamlalele uma elisebenzisa. Phela umuncu uthanda ukuhambisana nezikhathi ngoba nolimi nalo aluzithambisi luhambisana nesikhathi. Abalthulumi abasebasha abathandi ukubizwa ngokuthi bayisidala. Kwesinye isikhathi ulimi olusemthethweni luyaye (uncule amagama ahlaba esikhonkosini kuze kudingeke ukuthi kusetshenziswe amagama ethekelwe ~ilimin.i ze~ig.odi; ukwenza izibonelo (iginsa, umpi, njalonjalo) kwesinye lSlkhathl uhml olusemthethweni luthatha kade kanci olwesigodi lusuke selunawo amagama ayihlaba esikhonkosini. Yingakho nje abakhulumi bewancamela amagama amafushane ashaya khona noma ngabe ethekelwe kwezinye izilimi zezigodi nakwezinye-ke nje izilimi inqobo nie uma igama Iiyihlaba esikhonkosini kuleyo nco okusuke kukhulunywa ngay'; 
kilimi ezisemthethweni eNingizimu Afrika 
  Ngokomthethosisekelo wezwe laseNingizimu Mrika ziyishumi nanye izilimi ezisemthethweni esingabala kuzo: IsiZulu, isePedi, isiXhosa, isiTsonga, isiSwati, isiVenda, isiN debele, isiTswana, isiSuthu, isiN gisi nesisiBhunu. Izilimi zaBathwa kanye nolimi Lwezimpawu zingezinye ,ezilimi ezihlonishwayo eNingizimu Mrika. 
kinqubomgomo zokuqala zolimi ezabekwa eNingizimu Afrika Ucwaningo ngomlando wenqubomgomo yolimi eNingizimu Mrika l'Ienziwa ngabacwaningi abaningi esingabala kubo uReagan (1995), ~-A1exande~ (1997, 2000), Kamwangamalu (2001), Webb (2002), Heugh .2003), Ndlmande (2004), Ndimande-Hlongwa (200S), Kaschula (2004) 1Madiba (2004) nabanye abaningi. 
  Ngokubhala kuka-Extra noMaartens (1998: 25) ngonyaka we-1652 ,bancu ababehlala eKapa kwakungaBathwa kanye namaLawu. Ayekhuluma IIimi lwawo. Kwakukhona nabanye ababeyizivakashi ababeqhamuka :Yurophu imvamisa okwakungamaPutukezi namaFrench. Ngalesi sikhathi lmthetho owakhiswa ngowokusebenzisana kwezilimi ngokukhululeka ,hakathi kwaBathwa namaDutch. Kwathi ngesikhathi sekuqala ,kuhwebelana okwalandelwa ukufundiswa kwezenkolo kwaqala kwatolikwa. Alkhu kwenzeka ngonyaka gonyaka we-1657 sekuphele iminyaka emihlanu 'Jan Van Riebeek ethole isiteshi sezidlo. Abancu abaningi ababengamaDutch  	. 
emazweni ahIukene abantu baqala balthuluma ilingua franca (Zungu 1995). N gokubona ukuthi yayanda ngokushesha eKapa ilingua franca, kwalthishwa umthetho wokuqala wolimi owawuthi zonke izigqila mazifunde isiDutch. Lana kwaba ngumthetho wokuqala wolimi eNingizimu Mrika. lzikole zokuqala ezafundisa ezenkolo zazisebenzisa isiDutch njengolimi lokufundisa nokuxhumana. IsiBhunu ngalesi sikhathi sabe sesiqalile naso ukukhulunywa. 
Ukukhula kolimi IwesiNgisi 
  Ulimi IwesiNgisi lwaqala ngesikhathi amaNgisi efika eKapa ngonyaka we-1795. Ngonyaka we-1806 amaNgisi aqala ukufaka umthetho wawo wokusetshenziswa kwesiNgisi. Abantu baseNingizimu Mrika kwafuneka ukuba badele izilimi zabo bafunde isiNgisi. IsiBhunu sona sasaziwa njengesiDutch sasemalthishini: Ezikoleni zikaHulumeni isiBhunu. savalwa. . Lokhu akwenzekanga ezindlini zokufundela kuphela kodwa nasezmkundlem zemidJalo. Ukusukela ngonyaka we-1814 kuya kowe-1826 uLord Charles Somerset, okunguyena owayephethe eKapa nguye futhi owayengamele ukuqondiswa kolimi eNingizimu Mrika. UReagan (1986) uthi uLord Somerset wazama ukushincsha isiDutch ngesiNgisi. Lokhu wakwenza ngokubeka isiNgisi sibe ulimi oluhamba phambili nolusemthethweni. 
  IsiNgisi saqala ngokuthi siphoqwe ezikoleni zikahulumeni. Le mpoqo yaqhubeka yadJulela ezinkantolo ngonyaka we 1820. Ngonyaka we-1853 isiN gisi senziwa saba yilona lodwa u1imi olwalu~sershenziswa .ephal~en~e. Ngonyaka we-1875 amaBhunu altha inWangano yawo okwathl ekugcmem avumelana ngokuthi isiBhunu kuzokuba ngulimi lwawo kunesiDutch. 
Ulimi LwesiZulu nokukhula kwalo 
  Ngesikhathi seminyaka yowe-1700 eNatali kwakul'hethe inkosi uMalandela. Ngeminyaka yowe-1820 kuya onyakew we-1850 kwakuyisikhathi seMfecane lapho abantu abaningi babebalekela izimpi basabalala e-Mrika yonkana. Baningi abaya eZimbabwe nakwamanye amazwe ase-Mrika. UShintsho lwaqala eNyakatho noThukela kubeNguni abaseNyakatho. Emva kweMfecane iNyakatho yeNatali yayinamalthosi ahlukahlukene. Ngaleso sikhathi inkosi uDingiswayo waba inkosi yesizwe sakwaMthethwa. Inkosi UZwide yena ephethe isizwe sakwaNdwandwe. Ukuhlasela kwenkosi uDingiswayo ehlasela inkosi uZwide kwakukhombisa amandla. Inkosi uShaka yaqeqeshwa emabuthweni enkosi uDingiswayo    Napr;;:ikh::lthi 




maphakathi neNingizimu Mrika. Ngonyaka we-1819 inkosi uShaka yayiphethe umbuso omkhulu eNingizimu Mrika ukusukela emfuleni u:hongola oseNyakatho kuze kuyofika oThukeia (Ndimande 1998). Ukukhula kolimi IwesiBhunu 
.- 
Ngonyaka we-1910 kwasayinwa isivumelwano esungunombolo-137 
kumthethosisekelo wezwe laseNingizimu Mrika esasinikeza ulimi lwesiOutch amalungelo afanayo nesiNgisi, njengezilimi ezisemthethweni. INingizimu Afrika yaba ilizwe elinezilimi ezimbili ezisemthethweni. Ngonyaka we-l 925 isivumelwano salungiswa ukuze kufakwe nolimi lwesiBhunu. Ngowe-1933 ukufundiswa kwesiBhunu ezikoleni kwase ~uqalile sekufinyelele naseNatali. Ngonyaka we-1948 uMalan owayephethe Iqembu leNational Party wathatha izintambo zombuso. Umthetho awukhipha wavumela isiBhunu ezikoleni zabamhlophe. IsiBhunu senziwa saba ulimi oluphoqelekile kwamatekuletsheni. 
Ngonyaka we-1949 isiNgisi nesiBhunu sasiphoqelekile ezikoleni 
umthetho wemfundo yabansundu owawubizwa ngokuthi i-Bantu Education Act. Ngeminyakayama 60's nama70's amabhodi ezikole kanye namabhodi ayengabeluleki bemfundo yabansundu kanye nenhlangano yothisha yabansundu yaseNingizimu Mtika bazama ukuxoxisana nohulumeni ngomthetho wolimi. N gonyaka we-1961 iNingizimu Afrika yaphathwa nguOokoteia HF Verwoed. N gesikhathi sokubusa kuka Verwoed izilimi zomdabu zazingaziwa noma zikhona yini. Lokhu kwenza ukuthi isiBhunu singathandeki kodwa kuthandwe isiNgisi. IsiBhunu sasaziwa njengolimi lwencindezelo kanti isiNgisi sona sathathwa njengolimi IweNkululeko. 
Umthetho Wohlelo LwemfUndo Yabantu (Bantu Education Act 1953) Lona umthetho wemfundo yabantu wama-47 we-1953. 
NgokukaNdimande (2004: 65) 10 mthetho wachibiyelwa ngonyaka we1954,1956, 1959 no 1961. Kwakhiwa uMnyango Wemfundo yabantu abansundu ngaphansi koMnyango owawubizwa ngokuthi: "Native Affiirs" owawuphethwe nguOkt. Hendiik Verwoerd. Lo Mnyango yiwo owakha uhlelo lwemfundo abathi uma beluchaza bathi olwaluhambisana nezidingo zomuntu onsundu. Umthetho wabhalwa ngu Okt. Hendrik Verwoerd. Inhloso yalo mthetho kwabe kungukuvimbela abantu abansundu ukuthi bathole imfundo ezobenza babe sezikhundleni abangeke bavunyelwa

lomdabu. Into engasenzeki kakhulu manje ngoba abantu bajahe isiNgisi. Kwaba khona amakomidi abhekele ubhalomagama (orthography) Iwezilimi zomdabu. Ngonyaka we-1988 kuya kowe-1993, imfundo yonke yabe seyiphethwe nguMnyango Wezemfundo, ngaleyo ndlela yiwo owashicilela ubhalomagarna. Okwaba inkinga enkulu ngomthetho wemfundo yabantu ukuthi ubhalomagama Iwalwenziwa ngababephethe okwenza ukuthi kungabi yilolo olufimele izilimi zomdabu. lwabo ukusukela ebangeni lokuqala kuze kuyofika kwelesine kuphela emva kwaloko abafundi abansundu base bezothola imfundo ngesiNgisi. Ngonyaka we-1982 uMnyango wezemfundo nokuqeqeshwa wenza umbiko kwethulwa iziphakamiso ezilandelayo: 
* Umfundi makafunde ngolimi Iwakhe uma esangena esikoleni bese elandelisa ngesiNgisi noma isiBhunu. 
* Umfundi makafundiswe ngesiNgisi noma ngesiBhunu eqala nje ukungena esikoleni. 
* Umfundi makafundiswe ngolimi Iwakhe aze ayophothula imfundo yakhe. 
Iminyaka ephakathi konyaka we-1990 nowe-1993 yaba ngeyokuxoxisana.

3. INQUBOMGOMO YOLIMI 
   Kulesi sahluko kuwkhulunywa ngenqubomgomo yolimi kazwelonke eNingizimu Afrika, ekuMasipala waseThekwini, eyeNyuvesi yaKwaZuluNatali kanye nomthethosivivinywa wezilimi zaseNingizimu Aftika 
Inqubomgomo yolimi kazweumke eNingizimu-Afrika 
Inqubomgomo yobuliminingi yiyona esebenzayo eNingizimu 
Aftika. Ngokomthethosisekelo wezwe ziyishumi nanye izilimi ezisemthethweni eNingizimu Afrika. Phezu kwaloko uhulumeni 
uthi makuhlonishwe ezinye izilimi ezikhulunywayo kuleli lizwe. INingizimu Afrika yizwe loku,qala emhlabeni ukuthi libe nezilimi eziyishumi nanye ezisemthethweni. Ngaleyo ndlela inqubomgomo yobuliminingi ayejwayelekile. Amazwe amaningi aba nezilimi ezimbili eziba semthethweni. UHulumeni ubeke iBhodi Yezilimi Zonke ZaseNingizimu Afrika (iPanSALB) ukuthi yenze umsebenzi wokuthi ubuliminingi bube yimpumelelo kuleli lizwe iphinde ithuthukise izilimi ebezicindezelwe phambilini. INingizimu Aftika yizwe elinabantu abazi izilimi ezahlukene. Ezilimini ezisemthethweni kuleli kukhona izilimi ezikhulunywa nakwamanye amazwe ase-Afrika.

Isidingo senqubomgomo yolimi 
   Le nqubomgomo yolimi ihlose ukusiza ekutheni kuthuthukiswe izilimi ezahlukene eNingizimu Mrika. Ikhuthaza ukuhlonishwa kwamalungelo olimi ngenhloso yokwakha isizwe esibumbene nesikhululekile saseNingizimu Mrika. Le nqubomgomo yolimi kufanele ihlelwe ngendlela yokuthi ihambisane nobuliminingi kanye nomthethosisekelo futhi. Konke kufanele kuhambisane nemizamo yokuhlela umphakathi neyoshintsho eNingizimu Mrika. UMnyango Wezobuciko, Amasiko, Isayensi Nobuchwepheshe wawuqokelwe ukuthi kube nguwo owengamele ukuthi Ie nqubomgomo yolimi yenziwe futhi isebenze. Le nqubomgomo yolimi yavela esikhathini lapho izikhungo ezizimele nezomphakathi zithatha izinqumo zolimi ezingashintsha noma yinini, ezivama futhi ukungahambisani nezidingo zomthethosisekelo ngokolimi. Lokhu kuhambisana nemibono eyahlukene ngokusetshenziswa kobuliminingi eNingizimu Mrika. 
   UHulumeni uzinikele ekutheni ahambisane nomthethosisekelo ngasohlangothini lolimi. Inqubomgomo yolimi kuphoqelekile ukuthi ibe khona. Yiyo ezokwenza ukuthi uHulumeni akhe ubumbano nokubuseka ngokwentando yabantu eNingizimu Mrika. Le nqubomgomo yolimi yiyona okufanele ibe ngumhlahlandlela. 
   Yize uHulumeni eneqhaza elikhulu okufanele alibambe ekutheni inqubomgomo yolimi isebenze, 10 mbiko ubheka umsebenzi kahulumeni of ana nendlela okufanele yakhiwe yokulawula Iyokubhekela inqubo kanye nokwabiwa kwezinsizakusebenza kuzwelonke nasezifundazweni. 
Umthethosisekelo wezwe usiphatheleni? 
Ukulingana (isigaba 9 (3), ikhasi lesi-7. 
Ulimi kwezemfundo isigaba 29 (2), ikhasi le-16. Ulimi namasiko isigaba 30, ikhasi le-16. Amasiko, inkolo isigaba 31, ikhasi le-16-17. 
   Isigaba sesithupha somthethosisekelo sinikeza izi1imi ezisemthethweni ilungelo lokuba zisetshenziswe nokuthi kuhlonishwe ubukhona bezilimi ezahlukene. Izilimi ezisemthethweni kumele zisetshenziswe ngokulinganayo kukhushulwe izinga nokusetshenziswa kwezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika. Uhulumeni kanye nabanikazi bolimi uqobo kufanele benze imizamo yokulawula ukuthi izilimi ezisemthethweni ziyasetshenziswa ezindaweni eziningi. 
Imigomo ye DACST ekuthuthukiseni !tbuliminingi Umthetho sisekelo kufanele wenze lokhu: 
. a) Ukunikeza abantu amandla ngokuthuthukiswa, ukusetshenziswa kwezilimi ezisemthethweni ngokulinganayo. Kufanele kuqinisekiswe ukuthi abantu baseNingizimu Mrika bayayithola inkululeko yokusebenzisa am.alungelo abo olimi ngokusebenzisa izilimi ezisemthethweni eziqokwe yibo. 
b) Ukuthuthukiswa kwezilimi ezisemthethweni eNingizimu Mrika. IsiPedi, isiSuthu; isiTswana, isiSwati, isiVenda, isiTsonga, isiBhunu, 
	isiNdebele, IsiXhosa nesiZulu. 	. 
c) Ukusetshenziswa kwezilimi ezisemthethweni ezindaweni zikaHulumeni. 
d) Ukuxhasa ukusimama komnotho ngokuthuthukiswa kobuliminingi. 
e) Ukwenza abahlali baseNingizimu Mrika. bakwazi ukufunda izilimi zakhona bathuthukise ubumbano ~okuxubana kwamasiko. 
Izidingo zenqubomgomo yolimi 
Zinhlanu izidingo zenqubomgomo yolimi: 
a) Ukuthuthukiswa nokwelekelelwa kwabasebenzi ngenhloso yokufaka umthetho wobuliminingi 
b) Ukwenza umsebenzi wabasebenzi bolimi uhlonishwe 



d) Izilimi ebezicindezelwe zibhelekelwe kakhulu, okuyizilimi zomdabu kubalwa zamaKhoe, amaSan nolimi lweZimpawu, e) Ukuxhaswa kokufundwa nokufundiswa kwezilimi zaseNingizimu Afrika.

lsiphakamiso sokuqala 
   Ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukusetshenziswa ngokulingana kwezilimi ezisemthethweni, umthetho wokusebenzisa izigaba ezine zezilimi ngokushintshana kufunele usebenze eMinyangweni kahulumeni ngaphandle uma: 
i) Zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni zizosetshenziswa 
ii) Kukhona umqulu ngolunye ulimi olungenza kusebenzeke kahle kuhulumeni kunoma yiliphi izinga, lapho-ke imiqulu kufanele ihunyushelwe ezilimini ezifunekayo.

olusetshenziswayo. 	,. 
  Inqubomgomo yolimi kwezangaphandle ngokuxhumana ngomlomo ezikhungweni zikahulumeni 
   Ukuxhumana konke kukahulumeni okusemtheth,,;,eni nomphaltathi kufanele kwenziwe ngezilimi umphakathi ozaziyo. Lokhu futhi kufanele kwenziwe nangosizo lotolika kanye nezinye izindlelanjengokwenza kanye kanye uma kudingekile. 
   lnqubomgomo yolimi kwezangaphandle ngokuxhumana ngokubhala ezikhungweni zikahulumeni 
   Ngasohlangothini lokuxhumana ngokubhala phansi phaltathi kweMinyango kahulumeni nabahlali baseNingizimu Afrika, ulimi oluqokwe ngabahlali luzosetshenziswa. Uma kunguhulumeni oqaIise ukuxhumana 




nabaphesheya kwezilwandJe okufanele kwenziwe ngokohlelo lukahulumeni kuyoba ngesiNgisi noma ngolimi olufunwa yilelo lizwe. 
Isishayamthetho sikazwelonke nesezijimdazwe 
  Ngonyaka wezi-2005, noma yiluphi ulimi olusemthethweni luyosetshenziswa kuzona zonke izinto ezenziwa yisishayamthetho kubandakanya nokushicilelwa kwe"Hansard' njengelungelo. 
Kuzishayam thetho zezifundazwe izimo zezifunda eziyoveza ulimi okufanele lusetshenziswe. Yileso naleso sifundazwe kudingeka ukuthi siziqokele ulimi lwaso esifuna ukuthi sisebenze ngalo. Kubhekwe ukuthi ngonyaka wezi2005 isifundazwe ngasinye sibe sesimweni sokurhi singasebenzisa noma yiluphi ulimi kwezisemthethweni ikakhulukazi kulezo ezintarhu eziqokwe isifundazwe. 
Inqubomgomo yolimi kohulumeni basekhaya 
Nalthona lapha futhi ohulumeni basekhaya yibona okufanele 
baqoke ulimi okufanele lusebenze emphakathini ngoba yibona abawazi kahle umphakathi ukurhi unabalthulumi abasebenzisa luphi ulimi ngokuhambisana nenqubomgomo yolimi. Uma sekubhekisiswe ukusebenza kolimi nokurhi umphakathi ukhetha luphi, ohulumeni basekhaya ngokubambisana nemiphakathi yabo mabalthe, basabalalise futhi benze inqubomgomo yolimi isebenze. 
Inqubomgomo yolimi kwezemjUndo: UkujUndd nokujUndisa Inqubomgomo yolimi kwezemfundo kunoma iliphi ilizwe ayikaze yanelise. Imbangela yaloko: Inkolo, ezombusazwe, umphakathi kanye nesimo somnotho. ENingizimu Mrika uhulumeni wengcindezelo usebenzise ulimi njengesikhali sokuphatha kwezombusazwe. Imfundo yaseNingizimu Afrika yayiphethwe ngesiNgisi nangesiBhunu. Isidingo sokufunda ngolimi lomdabu sasibukelwa phansi engekho amalungelo olimi. Inqubomgomo yolimi kwezenfundo ikhishwe kahle ngonyaka wezi-2005. Lona ngumbiko 
oqhamuka noMnyango Wezemfundo. 	. 
Inqubomgomo yolimi ezinkantolo 
Kufanele ukurhi ummangalelwa aziqokele yena ulimi afuna    
ngokuthi ukhona urolika ozorolikela kulolo limi. Ulimi lokubhala phansi kuyoba ulimi okuhanjiswa ngalo icala enkantolo, kanti kungahunyushelwa kolunye uma kudingekile. 
Ukutolika 
   Ngonyaka wezi-20IO noma yimuphi umuntu onecala, ekurhethweni kwalo, kanjalo futhi nofakazi kunoma iyiphi inkantolo, uyoba nelungelo lokuba norolika oyingcweti futhi owaziwayo uMnyango Wezomthetho omele abahumushi norolika uma kudingekile. Kuzokwenzeka into efanayo, naseMnyangweni Wezokuvikela nokulondoloza. 
Amaphephanddba nemisakt;zo 
   Zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni eNingizi~u Mrika kufanele zisetshenziswe emisakazweni, kumaphephandaba nakumabonisakude. Umabonisakude kufanele ubonelele kalthulu izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika ebezicindezelwe phambilini kanjalo nolimi lwezimpawu kuze kube zonke izilimi zithola ukusetshenziswa ngendJela elinganayo. IMinyango yolimi kahulumeni iyokwalthiwa nguhulumeni kuzona zonke izifundazwe. 
Lo msebenzi uqedwe ngonyaka wezi-2005. Uhulumeni wagqugquzela iMinyango ezimele ukuthi nayo yalthe imithetho yolimi. 
Inqubomgomo yolimi kaMasipala waseThek~ini 1. Isingeniso 
   UMthethosisekelo waseRiphabhliki yaseNingizimu Mrika uhlinzekela izilimi ezilishumi nanye ezisemthethweni futhi uyawuqonda umlando wokuya ngokwehla kokusetshenziswa kwezilimi zendabuko zabantu baseNingizimu-Mrika nokwehla kwesithunzi sazo (lsl!;. 6). 
   Uhlinzekela ukuba noma ngubani unelungelo lok~sebenzisa ulimi lwalthe nokuzimbandakanya empilweni yesiko azikhethele lona (lsig. 30). 
   OMasipala bacindezelekile ngokoMthethosisekelo nomthetho iMunicipal Systems Act ukuba babhekelele lokhu kusetshenziswa kolimi nokuzikhethela kwabantu abalthe ngaphansi kwabo lapho bexhumana nabantu, kubalwa nezidingo ezikhethekile zalabo bantu abangakwazi ukufunda nokubhala. 
   Uhlaka Lwezwe LweNqubomgomo Yolimi luhlinzekela ukuthi lapho uMasipala eqoka izilimi eziz~set~~enziswa .?~m~ ~zi~eth.,,:e yimi~hakathi,

ezikhulunywa KwaZulu-Nataii ngokulandelana kwazo yisiZulu (80,9%), isiNgisi (13,6%), isiXhosa (2,3%) nesiBhunu (1,5%). Izibalo zesifun,da saseThekwini kazehlukene neze nezesifundazwe. 
  Yikho nje-ke uMasipaia waseThekwini ephasise Ie nqubomgomo yokusetshenziswa kwezilimi. 
2. Izinhloso 
Izinhloso zale nqubomgomo zifaka lokhu okulandelayo: 
1.1) Ukukhuthaza ukusetshenziswa ngokunobulungiswa kwazo zombili izilimi ezisemthethweni ezikhulunywa yiningi eThekwini, 
	okuyisiZulu nesiNgisi. 	_ 
1.2) Ukwenza lula ukurholakala kolwazi kanye nemisebenzi eyenziwa nguhulumeni. 
1.3) Ukuqinisekisa ukulungiswa kokungalingani ekusetshenzisweni kwezilimi kwangesikhathi esedlule. 
1.4) Ukukhurhaza nokweseka izakhamuzi ukuba zifunde izilimi ezisemthethweni ngaphezu kolimi lwebele okuyosiza ekwakheni nasekugcineni ubunye njengesizwe nasekuqikeleleni ukungashababali kwarnasiko esizwe ahlukahlukene. 
1.5) Ukuqinisekisa ukusetshenziswa ngokunobulungiswa kwezilimi ezinokusetshenziswa ngokukhurhaza ukuphathwa ngendlela efanele kwezilimi. 
1.6) Ukusebenzisa nokulandela imiyalelo yeSigaba sesi-6 soMthethosisekeio kanjalo nemigomo yeBatho Pele neminye 
	imibandela yokusebenza efuze Ie. 	. ... , 
3. Izinjongo 
Izinjongo zale nqubomgomo zifaka lokhu okulandelayo: 
1.1) Ukuhlahla izilimi ezinokusetshenziswa nguMasipala wase Thekwini, okungukuthi ezisetshenziswa lapho kuxoxwa ngokusemthethweni. 1.2) Ukukhetha zona lezo-ke ezinokusetshenziswa nguMasipaia. 
1.3) Ukugudluza zonke izithiyo ekusetshenzisweni kolimi ngaleyo ndlela kukhuthazwe ukutholakala ngokulingana kwezinhlelo nemisebenzi eyenziwa nguMasipaia.  _ 
1.5) Ukunika isiZulu nesiNgisi isithunzi nokuphathwa okulinganayo. 
4. lzosebenza kuphi Ie nqubomgomo 
   Imibandela yale nqubomgomo izosebenza kuzo zonke izinhlaka zikaMasipaia. 
5.1 Imibandela yokusetshenziswa kwezilimi ezisemthethweni: 
Imihlangano . 1.1) Kungasetshenziswa noma yiluphi ulimi kulezi ezimbili 
ezinokusetshenziswa nguMasipaia kunoma iyiphi inkulumo-mpikiswano nanoma yimuphi umhlangano woMkhandlu noma wamaKomidi awo. 
1.2) Emihlanganweni y6Mkhandiu neyamaKomidi awo, 
kumele kube nabazohumushela kolunye lwalezi zilimi ezinokusetshenziswa. Uma kwenzeka noma yiliphi ilungu lifisa ukuba okwenzekayo kuhunyushelwe kolunye ulimi okungelona olunokusetshenziswa, ilungu lelo kumele lazise usihlalo woMkhandlu noma walelo Komidi kusenesikhathi esanele ukurhi liyodinga'kutolikwe. 
1.3) Ulimi lokusayina ngezimpawu zezandla nalo kumele lutholakale uma kunesidingo. 
1.4) Noma yimiphi imihlangano nomphakathi noma imicimbi enomphakathi kumele iqhutshwe ngolunye lwezilimi ezinokusetshenziswa kuye ngokukhetha kwalabo abayizethameli. Uma phakathi kwezethameli kuba khona abangaluzwa ulimi olukhethiwe, kumele kurolikwe. 
5.2 Imigomo kanye nemithetho kaMasipala Yonke imigomo, imithetho kaMasipala kanye nezinqumo zoMkhandlu nezamaKomidi kumele kubhalwe ngazo zombili izilimi ezinokusetshenziswa zikaMasipaia. 
5.3 Izaziso nezikhangiso 
Zonke izaziso nezikhangiso ezisemthethweni ezikhishelwa ukwazisa 
5.4 Ukuxhumana ngezincwadi 
1.1) IsiZulu noma is iN gisi kungasetshenziswa ngenhloso yokuxhumana ngezincwadi ngaphakathi. Uma lowo obhalelwe engaluzwa ulimi olusetshenzisiwe, angacela ukuba abhalelwe ngolimi aluzwayo. 
1.2) Amasekhula kumele akhishwe ngazo zombili izilimi ezisetshenziswayo. 
1.3) Ukuxhumana ngomlomo kwangaphakathi kungaba ngesiNgisi noma ngesiZulu kuye ngalabo abaxoxayo. 
1.4) Ukubhalelana nabantu bangaphandle kumele kube ngolunye lwezilimi ezinokusetshenziswa, kubhekelwe ukuthi obhalelwayo ukhetha luphi ulimi. Uma kuphendulwa incwadi eya ngaphandle impendulo kufanele ibe ngalolo limi ebibhalwe ngaToieyo ncwadi ephendulwayo. 
1.5) Izincwadi eziphumayo kumele zikuveze ukuthi uma obhalelwayo elisa ukuba abhalelwe ngolunye ulimi kwezinokusetshenziswa okungelona okubhalwe ngalo, kuyokwenzeka lokho uma ecela. 
1.6) Izakhamuzi zinelungelo lokusebenzisa ulimi ezizikhethele lona. 
5.5 Izimpawu zokukhomba 
  Izimpawu wkukhombisa izikhungo noma amahhovisi kaMasipala kumele zibe ngazo zombili izilimi ezinokusetshenziswa. 
5.6 Ukunakekela amakhasimende 
  Wonke amakhasimende kumele asizwe ngolimi aIiikhethayo, ngosizo lotolika, uma kunesidingo. 
6. Indlela yokuqikelela ukuthi Ie nqubomgomo iyalandelwa 6.1 Amasu 
1.1) UMasipala kumele uqinisekise ukuthi amakhansela nabasebenzi bayakuqonda ukubaluleka kwezilimi ezahlukahlukene futhi bakhuthazwe ukuba bakwamukele ukusetshenziswa kwezilimi ezikhethwa yizakhamuzi/amakhasimende, amanye amakhansela nabasebenzi. 


1.3) UMasipala kumele ugqugquzele futhi ulekelele ukuthuthukis~a kwamaIthono ezilimi zabasebenzi nawamaIthanseia. 
1.4) Abasebenzi namakhansela kuf.mele bagqugquzelwe ukuba bafunde ezinye izilimi okungezona ezabo ngalokho kuyobe kuqinisekiswa ubugugu bezilimi ezahlukahlukene, ukuhlonishwa kwamasiko ahlukahlukene nokwenza ngcono ukuhlinzekwa kwabantu ngezidingo. 
1.5) Uma iminyango kamasipala ihlungela uku'qasha abasebenzi abasha kumele ibeke emqondweni Ie nqubomgomo yokusetshenziswa kwezilimi. 
6.2 Isikhathi esibekelwe ukuqala ukusebenza kwale nqubomgomo 2.1) Ngaphandle uma kushiwo kule nqubomgomo noma kusho isinqumo soMkhandlu, Ie nqubomgomo izoqala ukusebenza kusukela ngosuku eyophasiswa ngalo uMkhandlu. 
2.2) Kufanele kuthi zingakapheli izinyanga eziyisithupha iphasisiwe Ie nqubomgomo, iMenenja yeDolobha ibeke izikhathi okuzoqala ukulandelwa ngazo imibandela yale nqubomgomo. 
7. Umthelela kwezezimali 
   IMinyango eyahlukahlukene kaMasipala w3:seThekwini kumele ikuhlinzekele esabelweni sezimali ukulandelwa kwale nqubomgomo yokusetshenziswa kwezilimi isib. Ukuthuthukisa amakhono ezilimi abasebenzi nawamakhansela, ukuthenga imishini yokwelekelela ekutolikeni, nokunye. Okuphawulekayo ngale nqubomgomo ukuthi izobuyekezwa ngonyaka wezi-2009 ngoba kunamaphuzu abalulekiie ahambisana nokwenza inqubomgomo yolimi isebenze angafakiVie kuyona. Ukwenza 
nje isibonelo, Ie nqubomgomo ayinawo unyaka ohlonza ukuthi iqala nini ukusebenza. 
Inqubomgomo Yolimi YeNyuvesi YaKwaZulu-Natali: 
Isingeniso 
   Umthetho Wezemfundo Ephakeme we-1997 uchaza ngenqubomgomo yolimi kwezemfundo ephakeme. Imiqulu "Ulimi Kwezemfundo 



uNgqongoshe Wezemfundo Kuzwelonke, yileso naleso sikhungo semfundo ephakeme kufanele sikhethe inqubomgomo yolimi yaleso sikhungo b.ese leyo nqubomgomo iyashicilelwa. 
   INyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali ihambisana nezinhloso zenqubomgomo yobuliminingi yaseNingizimu Mrika fumi ifuna ukubamba iqhaza ekutheni ibe yimpumelelo. Kunesidingo sokuthuthukisa nokuqhubekisa impumelelo ezilimini ezisemthethweni, ikakhulukazi isiNgisi nesiZulu. Izinzuzo kubafundi zokuphumelela esiNgisini, ulimi lokuxhumana kwezemfundo, ekuhwebeni, ezimbonini, emazweni omhlaba, i-lingua franca ezikhungweni zikahulumeni nasezikhungweni zaseNingizimu Mrika zicacile. Ukwazi isiZulu kuzoba nomthelela ekwakheni izwe nasekusizeni umfundi ukuthi akwazi ukuxhumana nenani labantu abaningi KwaZulu-Natali.,Le nqubomgomo izama ukucacisa imivuzo yokwazi izilimi ezimbili eNingizimu Mrika. 
Inqubomgomo yeNyuvesi icacisa: 
* isidingo sokuqhubekisa ukuhlonishwa, ukuphumeleliswa kwezilimi ezibalwe kumthemosisekelo nezinye izilimi, kubandakanya izilimi ezingamagugu, ezenza kube nesidingo sokuxhumana ngamasiko, isayensi kanye nezomnotho; 
* ukumuthukisa ukuqonda ngobuliminingi ngokuvumela zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni KwaZulu-Natali, okuyisiZulu, isiNgisi kanye nesiBhunu; 
* isidingo sokuthuthukisa isiZulu sibe sezingeni elifanayo nesiN gisi ezikhungweni zemfundo; 
* ukunikezwa kwezinsizakwenza ukud'isiZulu sisetshenziswe njengolimi lokufunda, ukufundisa nokiiphatha; kanye 
* nesidingo sokukhulisa ucwaningo ekuthuthukiseni nasekuhlelweni kolimi. 
   INyuvesi izoqhubeka nokusebenzisa isiNgisi njengolimi oluhamba phambili kwezemfundo, kodwa izoqalisa ukuthu~hukisa isiZul~ 
bese sisetshenziswa njengolimi lwesibili lokufundlsa kuhlanganlswa nezinsizakusebenza (zemfundo ephakeme kanye nokuhlalisana kwabantu) ezizokwenza ukusetshenziswa kwezilimi kube yinto exhumanisa wonke amalungu eNyuvesi. 
1. Isisekelo 
1.1) Umsebenzi weNyuvesi ukuthi ikhiqize ulwazi bese iludiuliseia ngokwamazinga aphezulu omhlaba, nokwengeza enqolobaneni yolwazi ngocwaningo nokubambisana kwabacwaningi kuzwelonke nasemazweni omhlaba. 
1.2) ENyuvesi yemu yaKwaZuIu-Natali, abafundi abanolimi lwesiZulu njengolimi lwebele bakha iqembu elikhulayo nelibalulekile lolimi, lokhu kutshengisa ukumi baningi abafundi abakhuluma isiZulu eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali. Ngakho-ke iNyuvesi inomsebenzi wokunikezela isimo sezilimi kanye namasiko esivuna bonke abafundi. 
1.3) Ukukwazi kweNyuvesi ukukhiqiza ulwazi bese ilusabalalisa ocwaningweni nase~usebenzeni nomphakathi kuyahlangana namandia okuvivisa isiZulu ngokugcwele. 
1.4) IsiZulu singolunye Iwezilimi zendabuko ezisemthethweni ngokomthemosisekelo, izinga nokusetshenziswa kwaso okwancishiswa ngokomlando. INyuvesi ngokulandela umthemosisekelo iphoqelekile ukuthi ithathe izinyathelo ezibonakalayo neziya phambili ukwenyusa izinga nokukhulisa ukusetshenziswa kolimi lwesiZulu. INyuvesi iphoqelekile futhi ukumumukisa ubuliminingi, okusho ukuthi zonke izilimi ezisemthemweni ~zaseNingizimu Mrika ziphathwe ngokulingana. 
1.5) Inqubomgomo yolimi yeNyuvesi yakha ingxenye yesu elibanzi ezingeni likazwelonke yokumuthukiswa kobuliminingi esifundazweni ukukhulisa ulimi lwesiZulu . 
2. Imithetho ehow inqubomgomo yolimi yeNyuvesi 
2.1) Ukufunda, ukufundisa nokucwaninga kweNyuvesi kufanele kuqhubeke kube sezingeni eliphezulu futhi'kwaziwe kuzwelonke nasemazweni omhlaba. 
2.2) Inqubomgomo yolimi yeNyuvesi ichazwa yizidingo zenqubomgomo yesifundazwe nezikazwelonke. 
2.3) Inqubomgomo yolimi ihambisana nesitatimende nombonongqangi kanye nempokophelo yeNyuvesi ebandakanya umyalezo wokumumukiswa nokubekezelelana kanye nokuhlonishwa kwamasiko ehlukene namagugu omphakathi. 




2.5) INyuvesi ngokulinganayo iyakubona ukubaluleka kolimi IwesiZulu njengolimi olulondoloza amasiko, amagugu nolungulimi lokuxhumana. 
2.6) INyuvesi iyakubona ukubaluleka kolimi IwesiBhunu njengolimi Iwamasiko kanye nokubaluleka kwaso njengolimi lokuxhumana. 2.7) INyuvesi iyabona ukuthi izilimi namasiko nenani elithile labangabokudabuka eNdiya, eNingizimu Mrika kuqinisa ukunotha kwesifundazwe. 
2.8) INyuvesi ihlose ukuthuthukisa ukusershenziswa kwesiZulu njengolimi lokufundisa nokuxhumana, futhi kungumsebenzi wamaFakhalthi noma imikhakha, ngokubambisana neBhodi Lezilimi leNyuvesi ukuhlonza umthelela wokwenziwayo. 
2.9) Inqubomgomo yobuliminingi ifuna kube khona ukuhlonishwa kokwahlukana ngokwezilimi namasiko. 
2.10) Inqubomgomo yolimi yeNyuvesi iwholwa ngokuyisibonelo. 
3. Ukuthuthukiswa kwezilimi zokufimdisa eNyuvesi. 
3. I) INyuvesi iyasiqonda isikhundla sesiNgisi njengolimi oluhamba phambili lokufundisa futhi ikholelwa ekuthini kudingekile ukugcina isiNgisi njengolimi olusetshenziswayo kepha nakuba kunjalo ngenkathi isiNgisi sisetshenziswa kufanele kuthuthukiswe isiZulu ukuze sisetshenziswe ezikhungweni eziphakeme zemfundo. 
3.2) INyuvesi iwthuthukisa ulimi lwesiZulu njengolimi lokufundisa njengengxenye yesu lesikhashana kuya kwelesikhathi eside kuthuthukiswa ubulimimbili. Ngale nhloso iNyuvesi iwkhipha uhlelo lolimi olunikeza imininingwane ngokWenza Ie nqubomgomo isebenze njengezikhathi nokuthi kuwbiza imali engakanani. 
3.3) Ukuthuthukiswa kolimi IwesiZulu njengolimi lokufundisa kuwdinga kwakhiwe izichazimagama nezinye izinsiza kufundisa nezinsizakufunda. Ukuze lokhu kube yimpumelelo, iNyuvesi iwsebenzisana neBhodi Yezilimi Zonke ZaseNingizimu Mrika (PanSALB), kanye noMnyango Wezamasiko noBuciko kanye neHhovisi likaNgqongqoshe Wezemfundo. 
3.4) Ukuphumelela kokwenza inqubomgomo yolimi isebenze kuyoncika ekufakweni kwezinsizamali ezinkulu eziqhamuka kuHulumeni, isikhathi eside njengoba kwenziwa kunqubomgomo 
wlimi wkuthuthukisa ukufunda isiNgisi kanye nesiZulu. 
4. Ukuthuthukiswa kolimi IwesiZulu nesiNgisi njengezilimi zokufimda nokucwaninga. 
4. I) INyuvesi kuzomele igxile ekuthuthukisweni kohlelo lokufunda 
	isiNgisi kanye nesiZulu. 	- 
4.2) INyuvesi izosebenzisana neNyuvesi yaseZululand ukwakha isigungu esifundazweni sokuthuthukiswa nokufundwa kwesiZulu. 
  5. Ukuthuthukiswa kobuliminingi ezinqubweni kanye nakulokho okwenziwa isikhungo 
5. I) INyuvesi izosebenzisa indlela efanayo naleyo ephakanyisiwe yokufundwa kwesiZulu nesiNgisi esahlukweni sesine ngenhla ukugqugquzela uk~thuthukiswa nokufundwa kwezinye izilimi, ikakhulukazi lew ezikhulunywa ezwenikazi i-Mrika nezibalulekile ekuthuthukisweni ezokuhwebelana nokuvakasha ngokwamazwe omhlaba, kanjalo nezokufunda kanye nokuxhumana ngamasiko. 
5.2) INyuvesi iyalazi iqhaza .layo ekuthuthukisweni kobuliminingi ngokwezenhlalo yomphakathi, amasiko nasekuthuthukiseni ingqondo nomno.tho. Lokhu kubandakanya ezinye izilimi wmdabu nezinye izilimi zamagugu nezangaphandle. 
5.3) Ukwenza konke lokhu; iqophasikhungo leNyuvesi, izimpawu zikawonkewonke, imicimbi kawonkewonke njengokuthweswa iziqu, izinkulumo zokugcotshwa neminye imicimbi yomphakathi ezophathwa ngolimi IwesiNgisi nesiZulu. 
5.4) Izilimi zokuphatha kuzokuba isiNgisi kanye nesiZulu. 
5.5) Ukwengezelela ulwazi kubasebenzi abafundisayo nabaphethe, iNyuvesi izoba nezifundo zolimi lapho izofUndisa abasebenzi beNyuvesi abangenawo amakhono okuxhuinana ngesiN gisi nangesiZulu. 
5.6) Abantu abafuna umsebenzi kwezokuphatha noma kwezokufundisa kuzolindeleka ukuba babe nolwazi IwesiNgisi nesiZulu. Lapho ulwazi Iwanoma yiluphi ulimi lunganele mayelana nomsebenzi kuzoba khona izifundo ezizonikezwa ukuze kuthuthukiswe umuntu odinga lowo msebenzi.

Umthethosivivinywa Wezilimi zaseNingizimu Afrika 
* Unikeza uhlaka lwenqubomgomo yokuthuthukisa izilimi ezablukene zaseNingizimu Mrika. 
* Ukhuthaza ukuhlonishwa kwamalungelo olimi ngenhloso yokwakha ubumbano eNingizimu Mrika. 
* Ukwakhiwa kophiko lwezilimi kuwona wonke amazinga kahulumeni. 
* lnhloso yomthethosivivinywa ukwenza isigaba sesi-6 somthethisisekelo sisebenze. 
* Ukuth uthukisa ukusetshenziswa ngokulinganayo kwezilimi eNingizimu Mrika. 
* Ukwenza umthetho wobuliminingi usebenze. 
Imigomo yomthethosivivinywa 
* Ukupheliswa kokubukelwa phansi kwezilimi zomdabu; 
* Ukulingana kwezilimi namalungelo olimi; 
* Ukufundwa kwezilimi zomdabu; 
* Uhulumeni kufanele akulandelele ukuthi imithetho 
iya,etshenziswa yini ezikhungweni ezahlukene; 
* Ukwakhiwa kophiko lwezilimi 
* Kuloyo naloyo Mnyango kahulumeni 
* Kuleso naleso sifundazwe 
* Kufanele uphiko nophiko luhambisanenokubekiwe yinqubomgomo yolimi kazwelonke 
* Ukuthuthukiswa kwezilimi zomdabu 
* Uphiko nophiko kufunele lulethe umbiko kanye ngonyaka 


4. IMIHLAHLANDLELA YOKUHLELWA KOLIMI 
  Yize noma kunokugxambukela kwamazwe omhlaba ngezinWobo ezehlukene zezilimi okumele zithathwe noma zisetshenziswe, lokho kuyinqubo esidlulelwe yisikhathi. Ucwaningo lwesayensi ngalesi simo lubuyela emuva eminyakeni yowe-1960. Omunye weminyakazo yokuhlelwa kolimi eNingizimu Mrika usibuyisela emuva lapho inkosi uShaka yakhipha isinqumo esingumnqamula-juqu sokuthi kukhulunywe isiNtungwa sodwa ukuze kubhekwane nezingqinamba zokuxhumana. Lesi sinqumo senza ukuthi isiN tungwa sithole udumo nokwathi emva kwalokho sasabalala 
saze sakhulunywa nayilabo ababekhuluma ezinye izilimi zesigodi. Ezinye zezibonelo zokuhlelwa kolimi zibandakanya inqubomgomo yolimi lwesiDutch yenkampani i-Dutch East India COII?-pany, ukuguqulwa kwazo 
zonke izinto zenziwe ngenqubo yamaNgisi okwakungumbhidlango ka-Lord Charles Somesert kanye nokudlondlobala kwesiBhunu, sisukela ezingeni, lokukhulunywa emakhishini kuya ekutheni sibe wulimi olusemthethweni . Kuxoxwe kabanzi ngalezi zibonelo esahlukweni sesibili sale ncwadi. Njengoba lezi zibonelo zibeka, ukiIhlelwa kolimi kuwumzamo wokuxazulula inkinga eqhubekayo yolimi ukuze kufinyelelwe enhlosweni-ngqangi ethile . 
   Lezi zibonelo zidinga ukuqashelisiswa kabanzi ukuze sizivikele engozini yokubheka ukuhlelwa kolimi njengemizamo nje yokuxazulula izinkinga zokuxhumana (ikakhulukazi emiphakathini emincane). Izinhloso-ngqangi ezisobala zokuhlelwa kolimi zingavezwa njengezihlobene nolimi, kodwa ezikhathini eziningi kunezinhloso-ngqangi ezinqala zepolitiki nomnotho . Lelo qeqebana labantu okuthuke kukhethwa ulimi lwalo njengolimi olusemthethweni liba nengqayizivele yethuba lokuthola imfundo kalula (Myers-Scotton, 1990). Abakhulumi bolunye ulimi olungurnxhantela bejwayele ukuxhashazwa ngenxa yolimi lwabo olungasus'indod'ebandla . Ukwenza isibonelo, isiXhosa esijwayelekile nesikhulunywa yiningi, sigxile kakhulu emixhanteleni eyaqhamuka noNgqika, uNdlambe noThembu. 
Le mixhantela ingumgogodla wesiXhosa esibhalwa phansi. UNyamende (1994: 211) ubalula ukuthi isiXhosa esejwayelekile nesikhulunywa yiningi sasetshenziswa njengethuluzi lokuhlonza abakhulumi abangafundile ngokubheka imixhantela yesiXhosa abayisebenzisayo, lokho okwadala ukuba imixhantela yesiXhosa ibukelwe phansi. Ukukhuphuka kwesiBhunu sisuka ekubeni wulimi lwasekhishini siba wulimi olusemthethweni noluthuthukile kukhombisa kahle ukuthi ukiIhlelwa kolimi kuwumshikashika othatha 

 I  


8. 
yokuhlelwa kolimi: ngokwenyusa izinga lolimi Iwebele lufinyelele ekutheni luthathwe njengolusemthethweni. Abakhulumi bolimi bangaluvum<;la ulimi njengophawu lukazwelonke, ngalokho bese beba yimbumba yomphakathi. Lo mphakathi ohlangene ungabe usaxhashazwa ngokwezepolitiki. 
  Inkulumompendulwano ejwayelekile ngokuhlelwa kolimi ethinta isimo nengomuso lezilimi ikhombisa izihloko ezithile ezejwayelekile ezidinga ucwaningo Iwazo olunzulu: 
* Ukwehla kwamandla nokufa kwezilimi ezehlukene (njengesiKhoyi-Khoyi, noma isi-Sani eNingizimu Mrika) 
* Ukugcinwa kwezilimi ezincane (njengesiTsonga noma isiVenda eNingizimu Mrika) 
* Ukugcinwa nokusabalala kwezilimi ezinkulu (iijengesiSwahili e-eTanzania, eKenya naseUganda) 
* Ukusabalala kwezilimi ezisezingeni lomhlaba (njengesiNgisi nesiFulentshi e-Mrika) 
   Ucwaningo ngalezi zihlokwana lukhomba uhlelo oluthile lokucabanga nezinkolelo eziwumshoshaphansi ezinomthelela omkhulu endleleni esetshenziswayo nemiphumela etholakalayo. URuiz (1984) ubuka ulimi ngokwemihlahlandlela emithathu: 
* Ulimi luyinkinga 
* Ulimi luyilungelo 
* Ulimi luyinsizakusebenza 
Ulimi njengenkinga 
  Imiphakathi ethi ulimi luyinkinga yileyo eneziliml ezihlanganiswe nezinye noma ezahlukene. ENingizimu Mrika izilimi zomdabu zase- 
Mrika bezibandlululwa futhi zibukelwa phansi. Bezithathwa njengezilimi eziyinkinga nguhulumeni wobandlululo. Umqondo wokuthi izilimi zomdabu ziyinkinga usaqhubeka yize noma lezi zilimi sezisemthethweni ngokwenqubomgomo yolimi. Abantu abansundu akufanele bahlale nomcabango wokuthi ulimi luyinkinga ngoba aluyona. UCluver (I 996: 20) uthi ngokolimi, i-Mrika ihlobe ngoxhaxha Iwezilimi ezehlukene. I-Nigeria inezilimi ezingaphezu kwamakhulu amane kanti i-Zaire yona inezingamakhulu amabili. Kodwa-ke Ie nqubo yobuliminingi abayiboni kahle osopolitiki. Izizwe eziningi ezixube amasiko nezinhlanga eziningi ziye   
yokufinyelela ebunyeni besizwe. Lokhu kufakazelwa yizimpi eziningi zobuhlanga e-Mrika. Kodwa-ke, umlando wokuhlelwa kolimi eNingizimu Mrika akumele usiholele ophathe lokuthi sivume inkoleloze yokuthi 
inqubo yobuliminingi yiyona ewumnyombo wezimpi nezinxushunxushu zobuhlanga. Ukuthi u1imi Iwaba yimbangela yokubumba isizwe samaBhunu akusho ukuthi ulimi, ubuhlanga kanye nobuzwe kuyaxhumana. Isibonelo, ama-Irish alahlekelwa wulimi lwawo kodwa hhayi ubuwona. Umbono wobuliminingi njengenkinga ubuye uncike futhi kwezomnotho: Alikho 
izwe elingakwazi ukuthuthukisa izilimi ezingaphezu kwezimbili noma ezintathu, kanti amazwe amaningi ase-Mrika anezilimi ezingaphezu kwamashumi amathathu. Lokhu kusho ukuthi emazweni amaningi e-Attika, izingane eziqhamuka ezizweni ezincane zifundiswa ngolimi lwesifunda ezingaluqondi. Uma zikwazi ukufunda 1010 !imi, zibe sezishintshwa futhi zisebenzise ulimi lwesibili um~'sezifika emabangeni asethe thuthu emfundo, njengesiNgisi, isiFulentshi, isiPutukezi. Lezi zilimi zisebenza njengezilimi zokufunda nokufundisa. 
  Izinqubomgomo zolimi zase-France naseBotswana zingabonakala njengezibonelo zokuhlelwa kolimi okuncike emqondweni wokuthi inqubomgomo yobuliminingi iyinkinga. Womabili lawa mazwe asabalalisa inkoleloze yokuthi angamazwe aqhuba ngomthetho wolimi-lunye, kanti lokho kwenza ukuthi la mazwe acindezele ezinye izilimi, futhi aqhalrambise u1imi olusetshenziswa kakh.ulu ukucindezela abantu abayingcosana . ETanzania isiSwahili siqhalranjiswa njengalo lodwa uIimi Iwase-Mrika, 
kube kungabhekelelwa ezinye izilimi eziyikhulu namashumi amabili ezikhulunywa kuleliya lizwe. Indlela i-France neBotswana eyathatha ngayo inqubomgomo yobuliminingi yayincike embonweni wokuthi Ie nqubo 
idala uqhekeko emphakathini, ngakho-ke kumele kusetshenziswe u1imi olulodwa ukuhlanganisa abantu abehlukene ngokwamasiko nobuhIanga. Izinqubomgomo zolimi ezincike kule nkoleloze zizam,a ukuxazulula inkinga yobuliminingi, ngokuphoqelela ulimi olulodwa ezweni. Elinye lamathuluzi abalulekile asershenziswayo ukucindezela izilimi ezisakhasayo kanye nokusabalalisa ulimi olulodwa ohlelweni lwezemfundo. 
Ulimi njengethuluzi: 
  Lo mbono uncike emfuniselweni yokuthi u1imi alumele izinqubo nje kuphela emphakathini kodwa luyakwazi futhi ukuqondisa izinqubo emphakathini. Imibutho yezilimi ngokujwayelekile isebenzisa u1imi 




UScaglione (1984) ubhekisisa ubuhlobo phakathi kolimi kanye nezinhloso ezicashile zenhlalo nepolitiki. Ulimi olulodwa lungasetshenziswa ukuqipisa nokuqondisa imizwa engabonakali yobuzwe, hhayi ukuyidala. Leli phuzu lifakazelwa ngokucacile yimizamo eminingi engaphumelelanga yokusebenzisa isiBhunu ukudala imibutho ehlukene yezepolitiki (Isibonelo, Impumalanga Kapa eWukene ekuqaleni kweminyaka khulu edlule. Le mizamo (noma imibutho yezilimi) yaphumelela ngenxa yokungabikho kwezidingo zepolitiki wkuWanganisa amaBhunu. Yingalesi sikhathi uMilnet eseqala imizamo ecacile yokubulala ulimi lapho amaBhunu abumbana ndawonye evikela ulimi nolwaphenduka inkundla yokudonsisana kuphikiswana nombuso wamaNgisi. 
   ENingizimu Aftika, izilimi zezigodi ezehlukene zase-Afrika zahlanganiswa zaphakanyiselwa ekutheni zibe yizilimi ezikhlAlu..nywa yiningi njengengxenye yenqubomgomo ejwayelekile yokuqhakambisa ubuzwe obuthile. Ngakho ulimi lwasetshenziswa njengengxenye yamathuluzi ekuqaliseni inqubomgomo kaHulumeni wobandlululo. Imithelela eyengeziwe emincane yalolu hlelo ayikahlonzwa ngokwazi kwami: Akusikho nje kuphela ukuthi lezi zilimi zathuthukiswa ngokwenqubo okungeyona eyase-Afrika, kodwa kwakhula umuzwa wokuthi amaqoqo amagama azo "awathuthukile". Ngaleyo ndlela, wnke izingxenyana zamaqoqo amagama ebelokhu enganakiwe kanti futhi awabhaliwe ngisho kuzichazimazwi. 
Lokhu kukhombisa luvivi imiphumela ewubungozi yokuphoqelela umbono waseNtshonalanga (wesiNgisi) emphakathini okhuluma ulimi Iwase-Afrika. 
Kunobufakazi bokuthi Ie nqubomgomo ayiphumelelanga ndawo. 
Isibonelo, ukuthuthukiswa okuhleliwe kwesiNdebele akuphumelelanga ekwakheni isizwe saMaNdebele kubantu abahlalangaphandle kwesizwe esidala. Ukuphakanyiswa okuhleliwe kwesiSwazi ukuba sibe wulimi olusemthethweni eNingizimu Afrika kwehlisa umuZW" phakathi kwabamu ababephila eMpumalanga yeNtiiasifali wokuthi bangamaZulu.

Lezi zibonelo zikhombisa ukuthi ulimi lungabonakala ngengomfantu. 
Ezimweni lapho kuhlangana khona abantu abakhuluma izilimi ezehlukene ulimi lungaba wumgoqo ohlukanisa imiphakathi emibili eyehlukene. Umehluko ngokwamasiko kanye nolimi phakathi kwamaZulu kanye namaSwati mncane kakhulu, kodwa noma kunjalo abanye abantu basebenzisa lokhu kwahlukana ukuzihlonza ngokuthi bangamaSwazi 
noma amaZulu. Abakhulumi abaningi besiBhunu basemadolobheni

(Cluver, 1992). Yikho lokhu okufaka amanzi emadolweni ekutheni ulimi lwehliswe ngenxa yovalo lokuthi luzoqeda umngcele okhona. Lo mfantu ungasetshenziselwa ukufeza izinhloso zepolitiki. 
Ulimi njengelungelo 
   URuiz (1984) yena ubeka umqondo wokuthi ulimi luyilungelo eliqhamuka nemiphakathi ehambisana nomthetho wokulingana kwabantu. Ngokomthethosisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika ulimi luyilungelo., Umthethosisekelo ugunyaza ukuthi ulimi Iwakho kanye nobuzwe bolimi lwakho buhlonishwe. Umumu unelungelo lokuthi afundiswe ngolimi alukhethile yena. Okwenzekayo eNingizimu Afrika ukuthi isiNgisi 
sisalokhu siwulimi olusethenziswa kakhulu ezikoleni, emaphalamende, kwewmnotho njl!. Umbono Wokuthi ukwahlukana kuyingxenye yokuba ngumumu, nokuthi ukwahluka ngezilimi ngokufanayo kuyimo esibonakala ngayo thina njengabantu, uholela_ekutheni kuvikelwe lokhu kwahlukana ngokusemthethweni. Yingakho amazwe amaningi esikhathini samanje eseka izizwana ezincane ukuthi zisebenzise futhi zigcine ulimi namasiko aw. Umbuw obalulekile oqondene riezinqubomgomo wlimi ezigxile olimini njengelungelo ngowokuthi kungabe kwanele uma uhulumeni ewhlonza izilimi ezincane noma uHulumeni unengwadla yokuthuthukisa lezi zilimi? Kungabe kuyilungelo yini kubakhulumi besiCele esiwurnxhantela wesiZulu ukucela ukuthi ulimi Iwabo luthuthukiswe luze lufinyelele ekutheni luzimele njengolimi? Kungabe amaNdebele anelungelo lokuhlukanisa ulimi Iwabo izigaba ezimbili? Ngokungangabazi banalo ilungelo, kodwa angicabangi ukuthi leli lungelo lisho ukuthi uHulumeni kumele abe nomthwalo wokuxhasa ngezezimali izinhloso zalesi sinqumo ngoba akusiyena oqhamuke nalezi ziphakamiso. Ngesikhathi kuqhubeka umkhankaso wokuthuthukisa izilimi eziningi, inqubomgomo yolimi njengelungelo ilengela egebeni lokuthi ifadalale ize ivumele ubuliminingi obusho ukuthi izilimi ezincane azizukucindezelwa ngokucacileyo kodwa futhi ngeke zithuthukiswe ngokucacileyo. Lokhu kusho ukuthi izilimi ezincane zivumelekile ukuthi zife ngokuthula. Kodwa-ke ziningi izibonelo lapho imiphakathi emincane iphumelela ukugcina izilimi zawo kanye namasiko ekubeni zigutshuzelwa noma zizungezwe yimiphakathi nezilimi ezinkulu nezinamandla. 
Ulimi njengensizakusebenza 
1 Jmnnndn wnknthi nlimi luvinsizakusebenza ulethwa inkolelo vokuthi 




uwsebenza umsebenzi wokuhumusha, kubalulekile ukuthi wazi izilimi ezimbili ngokulinganayo. Lokhu kusiza lapho umkhulumi esethi yena, ufuna ukukhuluma ngolimi lwakhe aluncela ebeleni, akakwazi ukukhuluma isiLungu, noma-ke nje olunye ulimi. Uma utolika engakwazi ukutolika inkulumo yalowo mkhulumi eyisusa esiZulwini eyisa esiNgisini kuba nenkinga enkulu. Eminye imisebenzi ephoqayo ukuthi wazi izilimi ezimbili yileyo efana nokusebenza eMnyangweni Wezabavakashi. N gesikhathi uhamba ubonisa abavakashi izindawo, uyaphoqeka ukuthi wazi izilimi ezimbili noma ngaphezulu. Kodwa futhi abavakashi banetshisekelo 
enkulu yokufunda ulimi lwaleyo ndawo. Ubuntatheli noma ukusebenza ezikhungweni wkwazisa kudinga umuntu olimimbili noma oliminingi. 
   UHulumeni waseNingizimu Mrika ubeke Ibhodi Yezilimi2':onke zaseNingizimu Mrika ukuthi mayithuthukise ubuliminingi ezili-;nini eziyishumi nanye ezisemthethweni. Ukubekile uhulumeni ukuthi makubhekelwe kakhulu izilimi wmdabu eziyisishiyagalolunye ebezikade zinganakiwe phambilini okuyizilimi zabomdabu base-Mrika. Ucwaningo lukhombisa ukuthi izinga lokungafundi eNingizimu Mrika liphakeme kakhulu. Njengoba iNingizimu Mrika ishintsha nje abasebenzi basezimbonini badinga ukuthi bathole ukuqeqeshwa kwanoma yiluphi uhlobo ngolimi lwabo abalwaziyo 1010 limi okungulimi lomdabu. Uma lokhu kungenzeka, nabo abanikazi bezimboni bangathola inzuzo engcono okungenza umphumela ongcono kwezomnotho. Ngaleyo ndlela izilimi zabomdabu zase-Aftika, eNingizimu Mrika zingaba nomthelela noma igalelo elikhulu ekuthuthukiseni isimo senhlalo, sezemfundo kanye nezomnotho kubantu. UCluver (1996: 23) uthi umqondo wokuthi amazwe ahlukene ngobuhlanga angahlanganiswa abe yisizwe ngokwezepolitiki (kunesizwe esibumbene) lapho izinjongo zepolitiki zihlanganisa abantu futhi zibavumele ukuthi bathola ilungelo ngokwamasiko nolimi ukhonjiswa ngokucacileyo ezizweni ezinjenge-Switzerland lapho kwabelwana ngokwahlukana ngokwamasiko kanye nezilimi. Kulo mqondo kwenziwa umzamo wokuthi kugcizelelwe ubuhle bokuba buliminingi. Inqubo yobuliminingi ayivumeli kuphela umuntu ukuba afinyelele emasikweni ehlukene nemibhalo kodwa futhi ivumela ukuba umuntu ancintisane nabanye ezimakethe eziwuchungechunge ezibanzi. Izwe lase-Australia cishe yilona lizwe eselikhombise inqubekela phambili uma kuziwa kulo mqondo uma kuqhathaniswa namanye amazwe aqhuba ngomthetho wobuliminingi. ngoba 10 mqondo uzivumela ukuba zithole umsebenzi. Ukuba khona kwemiphakathi yaseYurophu eyehlukene e-Australia njengamaNtaliyane, amaJalimane kanye namaDashi kuvumela i-Australia ukuba inikezele ngezinsiza ezijulile zokutolika ezingqungqutheleni ezisezingeni lomhlaba. I-Australia isiphenduke isikole sezilimi zase-Yurophu, saseMpumaianga kanye nesikole sezilimi zaseMpumaianga saseNtshonaianga. Izinkampani ezigcwele izwe lonke manje sezikhetha ukuvula ezinye izikhungo e-Australia kunakwamanye amazwe angomakhelwane ngenxa yokuba khona kwezinsiza zokutolika ezingaqondakali kulawo mazwe. Yize kunjalo, angiyizwa imibono ebhekiswe ezilimini zendabuko zabantu base-Australia njengemicebo. AmaNyuvesi afana ne-Melbourne, analesi sikhala emakethe anokukhula okuqinile kwezitshudeni ezikoleni zazo zezilimi .. 
   Ingxenyana ebalulekile yalo;mbono umqondo wokuthi abantu ezweni lenqubo yobuliminingi kudinga bakhulutne ulimi olulodwa ukuze bakhe isizwe esisodwa. Ulimi olujwayelekile ngokungangabazeki luyadingeka ukulawula izwe elinenqubo yobuliminingi. Lolu limi akumele lugcwalise izikhala zezinye izilimi kodwa lungengezwa ezilimini eziphindaphindekile ezifundwa ngabakhulumi. Uhulumeni ophumelelayo kanye nezinjongo ezijwayelekile zepolitiki nomnotho unezinto ezinamandla kakhulu ukuhlanganisa imiphakathi 'yamanje kunolimi olulodwa oluphoqelelwayo. Kodwa-ke ukwakhiwa kwalezi zinhlosongqangi kuthwesa uHulumeni umthwalo omkhulu emahlombe, ngakho 10 mqondo bawuchitha ngazo zonke izindlela osopolitiki. Ingxoxo emfushane yezindlela ezejwayelekile zokubhekana nezinqubomgomo zolimi iholela ekudingidweni kafushane kwezibonelo zangempela zokuhlelwa kolimi. Le mihlahlandlela ibonakala kahle ezindleleni noma kumamodeli amane aziyizibonelo zokuhlelwa kolimi. 
I-Assimilationist model - Indlela yokubhaciswa kolimi 
   Umbono wokuthi ubuliminingi buyinkinga uholela kunqubomgomo yokuhlelwa kolimi ebhacisa imiphakathi emincane ngaphansi kwaleyo emikhulu. Izinqubomgomo zokuhlelwa kolimi e-France, Engilandi naseMelika zingathathwa njengezibonelo lapho kwenziwa khona imizamo yokuthi imiphakathi emincane igwinywe yileyo emikhulu. Izinkulumo ezifana nokuthi "Ibhodwe lengxubevange yamaMelikana" "American Melting Pot" zifihla ukucindezelwa kwezilimi ezincane okwenzeka kuleli "bhodwe" u-Ovando noWiley (2003). Ukucindezelwa kwezilimi ezincane 




njengeyokugwinya nokubhacisa njengoba inhlangano yazama ukugwinya imiphakathi ekhuluma isiBhunu eyayibandlululiwe phambilini enhlanganweni. 
I-Integrationist model - Indlela yokuhlanganisa 
  Le ndlela isondele kakhulu kulena engenhla kodwa yona ivumela imiphakathi emincane kanye nezilimi ezincane ukuthi ziqhubeke 
zibe khona kodwa ezindaweni ezibaliwe. Inqubomgomo yolimi yaseFrance, e-Afrika iyisibonelo esihle salokhu. Ulimi olubhula amaphiko isiFulentshi, luyilo kuphela ulimi lokufunda nokufundisa kuzo zonke izikhungo zemfundo, yilo kuphela ulimi olusetshenziswa wuHulumeni, abemithombo yezindaba kanye namasonto. Ngokujwayelekile-kuba nezinqubomgomo ezingandile lapho izilimi zebele ziba nemisebenzi emincane. Ulimi olusetshenziswa kakhulu yilona oluba yithuluzi lokwakha isizwe esisodwa emphakathini onamasiko nezilimi ezahlukahlukene. Iqiniso lokuthi okungaphansi kwamaphesenti ayishumi komphakathi wamazwe amaningi e-Afrika kwazi lolu limi kahle ukuze kwaziwe njengabalwazi kahle ulimi, akusho ukuthi kungubufakazi bokuthi lezi zindlela eziyizibonelo ezisetshenziswayo uma kuhlelwa ulimi zihlulekile emazweni amaningi ase-Afrika. Isibonelo esingasinika senqubomgomo yolimi lapho kusetshenziswe Ie ndlela ye-Integrationist e-Afrika 
kungaba yiseNamibia lapho isiNgisi sodwa siwulimi olusemthethweni. Izilimi zikazwelonke (njengesiNdonga, isiKwanyama nesiHerero) zisetshenziswa kancane njengokuba kuqalwe ngazo ezikoleni njengezilimi zokufunda nokufundisa, kanye nezilimi zemisakazo, kodwa isiNgisi 
yilona lodwa ulimi olusetshenziswa emabangeni ap.h~keme emfundo, kuHulumeni kazwelonke, enqubweni yezobuIungiswa nezinkantolo 
kanye nakomabonisakude. IsiNgisi kumele sibe wulimi olungachemile olungahlanganisa umphakathi (UNIN, 1981). 
  1- Vernacularisation model- Indlela yokudlondlobalisa ulimi lwebele lube ulimi olusemthethweni 
   Ukubuka ulimi njengethuluzi kuholela kunqubomgomo yolimi lapho izilimi zebele ziphakanyiswa zifinyelele ekutheni zibe yizilimi ezisetshenziswa ezinhlakeni ezehlukene, nokungagcina kuzenze zifinyelele ekubeni yizilimi ezisemthethweni. Ukuphakanyiswa

ukuba sibe wulimi olusemthethweni eTanzania yizibonelo ezinhle zale nqubomgomo. Inqubomgomo yolimi yaseNingizimu Afrika ngaphambi konyaka we-1994 ikucacisile futhi ukuthi Ie ndlela ingaguqulwa 
kanjani ukuze ihambisane nombono ngeso lezepolitiki. Lesi sibonelo siphinde sichaze ubuthakathaka noma ububi bale ndlela: Ibiza kakhulu kanti ikhombisa ukuphumelela kakhulu uma isetshenziswaolimini olulodwa. Izilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika eNingizimu Afrika zamenyezelwa ngokomthethosisekelo njengezilimi ezisemthethweni, kodwa azizange zithuthukiswe ngokugculisayo njengezilimi ezisemthethweni. Le ndlela kumele ibe nezinhlosonqangi ezikholekayo uma sekubhekiswe ekutheni yiluphi ulimi okumele luthuthukiswe. 
I-Pluralist model- Izilimi :ionke zinikwa ilungelo elifanayo 
  Umbono wolimi njengelungelo uholela kunqubomgomo enika zonke izilimi zezwe izinga elifanayo. I-S'Yitzerland ivamise ukucashunwa njengesibonelo, De Preez no Du Plessis (2004). Eqinisweni iyisibonelo esingezwakali kahle ngoba i-Switzerland ayizange ithuthukise izilimi 
zayo ezinkulu nezisemqoka, njengesijalimane, isiNtaliyane nesiFulentshi, kodwa yavumela omakhelwane bayo ukuba benze 10 msebenzi. Ngaphezu kwalokho, ulimi Iwesine i-Swiss, ne-Rhaeto-Romanic zithathwa njengezilimi zikazwelonke kodwa hhayi njengezilimi ezisemthethweni, lokho okusho ukuthi amalungu alo mphakathi okhuluma lezi zilimi ngeke akwazi ukuxhumana noHulumeni kazwelonke wase-Switzerland ngolimi Iwawo. 
   E-Afrika izindlela ze-pluralist model ezibona amalungelo alinganayo ezilimi njengentuthuko elinganayo elethwa nguHulumeni kazwelonke wazo zonke izilimi zivamise ukubonakal~ ngokungaphumeleli kwazo. Amazwe anjenge-Benin azama ukuthuthukisa izinhlelo zemibhalo ezilimini eziyishumi nesikhombisa zalezo ezingamashumi amahlanu nambili. Uhlelo Iwafadalala ngenxa yokuswelakala kwezazi kanye 
nezimali (Igue & N'Oueni, 1994). Isimo esifanayo senzeka eZaire kanye nakwamanye amazwe ase-Afrika. Inqubomgomo efanayo lapha ingamba eqolo ngoba kuyomele sithuthukise izilimi eziningi ngaphambi kokutolika imibhalo ejulile siyise kuzo. Eminye yemiqondo ebalulekile yokuhlelwa kolimi evelayo ukuthi ngeke ukwenze ukuhlelwa kolimi ukwenzelwa omunye. Igxathu kumele lithathwe ngabantu uqobo lwabo futhi kumele bawenze bona umsebenzi. 5. IZINjULALWAZI ZESAYENSI YEZILIMI ZOMPHAKATHI 
  Kunezinjulalwazi ezibalulekile ekusombululeni izinkinga wlimi. Ziningi izinjulalwazi okuroxoxwa ngaro lapha, kodwa ngaphambi kokwenza njalo kubalulekile ukuehaza ukuthi iyini injulalwazi. NgokukaNdimande (1998: 
17) injulalwazi ngumhlanhlandlela ohlahlwa ngosonjulalwazi ngokubona ukwenzeka kwezinto emhlabeni. Ingabuye iehazwe futhi njengombono womuntu ongawuthatha uwusebenzise ocwaningweni'ukuze wesekele ubuqiniso nolwazi olwethuliwe ngocwaningo. Ziningi izinzululwaii eziyibekile induku ebandla ukuze izizukulwane ngezizukulwane zisale zisizakale. Izinjulalwazi okuwkhulunywa ngaro zibandakanya lezi ezilandelayo:

laba abakade becindezelwe, bathole imfundo kube khona ukuthuthuka komnotho, kube khona ukuxolelana phakathi kwezizwe ezahlukene nezingazwani. 40) alubiza ngokuthi "Uhlaka lokuhlela ngecebo" (Strategic Planning. Framework). Lapha kubhekwa ukuthuthukiswa kwenqubomgomo 

yolimi kazwelonke eNingizimu Mrika. Inqubomgomo yolimi kufanele ihambisane nenhlosonqgangi yezwe ebekiwe. Lapha eNingizimu Mrika umthethosisekelo uvuna inkululeko yawo wonke umuntu. Impokophelo yezwe ukuthuthukisa izilimi eziyishumi nanye ezisemthethweni eNingizimu Mrika. Kunezihibe ezikhona ekuphumeleliseni inhlosonqangi yezwe okuyintando yabantu. Abahleli bolimi kufanele bakhe izinhloso noma izinjongo ezihambisana nezinhlosonqangi zezwe futhi ezizodala izisombululo zezinkinga ezikhona. Izinhloso zenqubomgomo yolimi yizona ezakha inqubomgomo yolimi kahulumeni kanti kufuneka i~e umbhalo 
osemthethweni. 	-. 
Elinye iphuzu elibalulekile uhlaka lokwenza inqubomgomo isebenze. 

Lolu uhlelo olubanzi oluzohlangabezana nezinhloso zenqubomgomo. Uma kuhlelwa ulimi kumele kwazeke ukuthi ubani wenzani, kuphi kanjani ngaziphi izinsizakusebenza, furhi kufanele acacise ngezidingo zokupharha kanye namasu okwenza inqubomgomo isebenze, izinsizakusebenza ezidingekayo zibandakanya abantu okumele benze umsebenzi, izimali, ubuchwepheshe kanye nomphakathi ozokwelekelela nokuthi izikhalazo zizoxazululwa kanjani. 

   Uhlelo lokwenza inqubomgomo yolimi isebenze kufanele lube nezinkomba zokusebenza, ukuze luvumele abeluleki bakwazi ukuhlola ukuthi inqubomgomo yolimi iyasebenza ngempela yini. Inqubomgomo yolimi ibandakanya ukulawulwa kanye nokuhlolwa. Okokugcina- 

ke kule njulalwazi yokuhlelwa kolimi ubudlelwano phakathi kolimi nenqubomgomo yolimi kanye nempilo yomphakath[ Lona umkhakha uWebb (2002) awubiza ngokuthi "Ipolitiki yolimi". Alukho ulwazi olwanele ngalesi sifundo ngoba abacwaningi bolimi lomphakathi bayehluleka ukuqagela ukuthi sinjani isimo sezilimi ngokwepolitiki nangokwenhlalo yomphakathi, isib. Yinini lapho ulimi lufa khona? Azikabi khona izinsiza zokwenza ukuthi ulimi lufundwe kahle ngokwepolitiki. 

   Izimpikiswano zolimi ziyaye zihluthule abantu kugcine sekwenze isimo sokuthi inqubomgomo igcine ingathuthukiswanga. Ukwakha inqubomgomo yolimi kudinga ukuthi kuthathwe isinqumo ngezilimi ezizosetshenziswa ezinhlelweni ezisemthethweni, kufanele kutholakale kuqala ukurhi yiziphi lezo zinhlelo ezisemthethweni. ezisetshenziswa kuleyo ndawo. Abahleli bolimi kufanele babe nolwazi locwaningo oseluke lwenziwa phambilini, bazi ngemigomo yokuhlela kanye nobudlelwano phakathi kolimi nomphakarhi.

ungenazwi ekuhlelweni kolimi leyo nqubo ehlongozwayo ayiphumeleli. Okudingekayo ukuthi umphakathi nawo ubambe iqhaza ngokurhi kutholakale izidingo zawo, imibono yawo. Umbuw obuziwe ukuthi kungabe ukuhlelwa kolimi kungawenza yini umahluko ezinguqukweni ezihlongozwayo eNingizimu Africa? Incazelo etholakele 
. . ~ . ' .... ' - . - 
* Kwakuhlelwa izilimi eziwdwa. 
* Kwakubonakala njengento yezazi zilimi kuphela. 
* Yayibhekele kakhulu uhulumeni kazwelonke nolimi olusemthethweni. 
   Ukuhlela ulimi kungawenza umehluko eNingizimu Afrika uma kungenziwa ngendlela yokuthi umphakathi ubandakanywe urshelwe amaqiniso ngolimi kungafihlwa lutho, ukuze nawo uzibone uyingxenye yoshintsho noma abalethi boshintsho. Kungaba nomthelela emnothweni wezwe, uma ulimi lwenziwa lube yigugu ngokomnotho. Uma ukuhlelwa kolimi kungatholi ukuxhaswa ngabaholi bomphakathi nawo umphakathi uqobo lwawo akukho okuyoshintsha. Ukuhlelwa kolimi kungabamba iqhaza elikhulu ekwakheni kabusha iNingizimu Afrika. 
  Ukuhlelwa kolimi kumele k~bukwe ngeso elibanzi kubhekwa izimo zepolitiki kanye nomnotho ezingeni lomhlaba wonke jikelele. lsikhathi esiphila kuso isikhathi solwazi, uma ungenalo ulwazi usenkingeni. Umbiko we Khomishana LikaZwelonke Ezikhungweni Zemfundo ephakemel National Commission on Higher Education (NCHE) uyakufakazela lokhu lapho lichaza ukuthi izindawo wkusebenza ziya ngokuya zilawulwa 
ulwazi. Imfundo kufanele ikhiqize abafundi abanamakhono okusombulula izinkinga ngisho nalew abangakaze bahlangabezane naw. Ukusetshenziswa kwamakhompyutha njll.
