   Uma sibuka ngeso lentando yabantu, inqubomgomo yolimi ekhethiwe ingcono kakhulu kunaleyo kahulumeni wangaphambilini wobandlululo. Sekuphele iminyaka elishumi nane singenile kuhulumeni wentando yabantu. Ulimi kufanele ukuthi ngabe yilona oluholt'phambili ubumbano eNingizimu Afrika, LANGTAG (I996). Ubuliminingi eNingizimu Afrika bubonakala bamukeleka njengoba uhulumeni ezibophezele ekutheni athuthukise izilimi eziningi. Ukuze abantu bakwazi ukuthi bakhululeke kufanelekile ukuthi bathole ulwazi, amalungelo namakhono ngezilimi zabo. 
Injulalwazi yokuthambekela inkulumo - Speech Accommodation Theory 
â¢â¢â¢ 




nenhloso ngalabo bantu. Le njulalwazi ibeka ukuthi abantu bashintsha indlela abakhuluma ngayo ifane noma yehluke kweyalabo abaxoxa nabo ukuyeza ukuthi bayavumelana noma abavumelani. Uma ushintsha indlela okhuluma ngayo lokho kubizwa ngokuthi ukusondelana (convergence) 
kanti kukhombisa ukuhlangana nobumbano. Uma umkhulumi ebaleka engakhulumi ngendlela efanayo nomuntu axoxa naye lokho kubizwa ngokuthi ukwahlukana (divergence) Ndimande (2004: 63). Kufanele kuyele ukuthi abantu balusebenzisa kanjani ulimi ukuyeza ubuzwe babo noma ubuqotho babo. Ukufunda ngale njulalwazi ngakolunye uhlangothi kuyeza ukuthi ulimi lunamandla angakanani ezimpilweni zethu, okuyaye kugcine kubulale ubuhlobo. Ngakolunye uhlangothi kusinikeza isithombe esigcwele ngomkhuba wokuthanda ukushintshashintsha ulimi nokudala lokho. 
   Sonke siyazi ukuthi indlela esikhuluma ngayo iyashintsha ~gokuphazima kweso kuye ngezimbangela ezahlukene zalolo shintsho okungaba ukuhlelwa, isihloko okukhulunywa ngaso, umuntu esixoxa naye, injongo yengxoxo njll. Ukwenza isibonelo, siyaye sikhulume ngokungasheshi uma sixoxa nabantu bakwamanye amazwe, noma sisebenzise ulimi oluthambile nabantwana noma izingane (baby talk) ngenye indlela siyaye sithambekele olimini Iwabantu esixoxa nabo noma siqondise indlela esixhumana ngayo siye endimeni entulekile yalaba bantu esisuke sixoxa nabo. UGiles noCoupland, (1995) yibona abaqhamuke nayo Ie njulalwazi. 
   UHolmes (1992: 255) uthi ngesikhathi abantu bekhulumisana, inkulumo yabo iyaye ifane. Lokhu kuqonda ukuthi yilowo nalowo ozibandakanyayo inkulumo yakhe iqondana neyalowo akhuluma naye. 
Le njulalwazi yasetshenziswa nguZungu (1995) Japho ebhale khona kabanzi ngolimi olusetshenziswa yiziboshwa. Uthi kuneziboshwa ezizibiza nge-27 ngesikhathi zibingelelana zithi hhomu kwe~lnye eziyi-27 nazo ziqondanisa nayo indlela yokubingelela. Iziboshwa ezizibiza nge-28 zithi samani uma zibingelelana nenye i-28. Uma ophendulayo engaqondanisi nokwenzakalayo, olalele usezokwazi ukuthi akasiyena owalelo qembu. Injulalwazi efanayo ingasetshenziswa ezindaweni ezahlukene. 
   UHolmes (1992: 255) uthi injulalwazi yokuthambekela inkulumo yenzeka ngesikhathi izikhulumi zithandana. Ziyathanda ukuxoxa ngezinkinga zazo, zihlanganyele futhi zifune izixazululo ziphinde zinikezane ithemba. Ukwenzelana phakathi kwabantu, ikakhulukazi emaswini okukhuluma, angeke asebenze ngale kokwazi umyalezo walowo owuthumele ozolinganisa futhi ubale imiphumela ecacile yamagama kumlaleli. 
	. 	.. 	. ... 	.. I.. 	.... 	. 
ethile, singaphawulanga noma siqagele ukuthi umuntu lowo uyalwazi yini ulimi, izinga umuntu akulona, imfundo, isigaba noma nje ubuhlakani. Isibonelo abafundi abakhuluma IsiZulu abangaxubi nolunye ulimi (isiNgisi nesiBhunu) bathathwa njengabantu abangalwazi ulimi lwesiNgisi. Lokho kwenza babukelwe phansi. Ulimi luyashintshashintsha kuya ngomuntu olukhulumayo. Kuyiqiniso ukuthi abantu bayalusebenzisa ulimi bazi noma bengazi ukuthi kuyeza ubuzwe babo. 
   Okusobala ukuthi ngesikhathi sithambekela olimini lwalowo okhulumayo lokho kungaba nenzuzo noma kube yingozi ekugcineni. Isibonelo: abantu abangabokufika abangasazi kahle isiNgisi noma olunye ulimi bayaye bazithole bebandlululeka emphakathini nakothisha, okudala umthwalo emahlombe abo kwezemfundo nakwezemisebenzi. Ngaphezu kwalokho ukulinganisela inqlela esikhuluma ngayo (ukuphimisa, 
ukushesha kwenkulumo) kulabo esixoxa nabo kungaba umthwalo 
omkhulu emahlombe abo. Ukungathambekeli olimini lomuntu okhuluma naye kususelwa ekutheni abakhiilumi akubona nje kuphela abantu abafanelekile emisebenzini abanikwa yona umphakathi. Kodwa bafana nabantu ababuzayo, abazama ukuziqonda bona nabanye. Le njulalwazi yokuthambekela noma yokungathambekeli olimini igxile kakhulu olimini olukhulunywayo uma kwcl,unywana, iqhakambisa kakhulu izingxoxo noma okuxoxwayo. Ukwenza ubuqiniso kule njulalwazi kufanele kubhekisiswe izinjulalwazi eziqondene .nokusebenza kwengqondo ezakha zibuye zimelele imikhuba eyenziwa ngabantu yokuthambekela kolunye ulimi noma yokungathambekeli kolunye ulimi. [I-Similarity attraction, i-social exchange, nenjulalwazi kaTafjel ye-intergroup distinctiveness]. 
   Umkhulumi uyathambekela olimini lwalowo muntu akhuluma naye ngendlela yokuthi ulimi lufane nalowo axoxa naye. Ukungathambekeli olimini lomuntu okhuluma naye kuchaza isimo lapho abakhulumi beshintsha indlela abakhuluma ngayo ukuze labo wakhuluma nabo bangezwa noma ukuzehlukanisa kwabanye abantu. Lo mkhuba wokuthanda ukufanana ngokolimi, ukuphimisa, ukuphumula noma ukukhuluma 
njll. Ukuthambekela olimini lomuntu okhuluma naye kwenyusa 
imizamo yokuthi labo abakhulumayo babukeke befana bengabangani, kungahambisana nokulahlekelwa ubuqotho kanye nobuzwe. 
   Injulalwazi yeSocial Exchange (ukwabelana ngolimi) ithi abakhulumi kanye nabalaleli babelana ngezindlela ezifanayo zokuqonda ezivumela izinjongo zomkhulumi zokuba aziwe umkhulumi bese zihunyushwa kaWe   




uthi uma sithambekela olimini Iwabantu esixoxa nabo kungaba nenzuzo kunokulahlekelwa. Isibonelo, abaholi bezepolitiki bayathambekela olimini Iwabantu bakhulume ulimi Iwabo noma kungaselona ulimi Iwabo kodwa bathembise izinto ezithile kubantu ukuze babavotele. N gamhla ziyi-11 enyangeni kaNhlolanja onyakeni wezi-2009 umholi weDA okuyiqembu lezepolitiki wabonakala kumabonisakude ekhuluma ulimi IwesiZulu ngesikhathi ekhuluma nabalandeli bakhe. Lokhu wakwenza ukuze akwazi ukuthi azisondeze kubantu abakhuluma lolu limi abangabanikazi bolimi, ngaleyo ndlela ubethambekela olimini Iwabo ngoba kukhona afuna ukukuzuza. 
   UHawkes (1982: 83) uthola ukuthi konke ukuxhumana kubandakanya umyalezo oqalwe ngumethuli omiselwe ukuba awethulele i:>;i.~enywa. Umyalezo udinga ukuthintana phakathi komethuli nalowo omenyiwe okungaba ukukhuluma noma ukubona. Inkulumo ingenziwa ngokwamakhowudi, izinombolo, ukubhala, ukwenziwa kwemisindo 
njll. Umyalezo futhi kumele ubhekise engqikithini eqonde kulowo 
olalele. Yingakho kubalulekile ezinhlanganweni zombili ukuba zihlaziye izimpendulo zomunye nomunye ukuze ukwenzelana kuqhubeke. Uma izimpendulo zingekho noma zingakhethi bala, lokhu kusho ukuthi 
loyo ozibandakanya ezingxoxweni angeke awuhlaziye umyalezo noma imiphumela ephikisanayo. 
Injulalwazi ye - Causal Attribution 
   Le njulalwazi ithi uma sixhumana nabanye, siyaye sibe sesimweni sokUhumusha inkulumo, sihlole umuntu ngezinjongo ezithile esizibona ngesikhathi ekhuluma. Isibonelo, siyaye sibone nje indoda enothile 
isiza umuntukazana bese ngaleso sikhathi sithathwe umusa nobubele. Siyaye sibheke injongo yakhe yokwenza lokho. Kulokhu uma sibeka 
isici sokuthi uzozuza yini yena ngalokhu, ngaleyo ndlela kufanele sibuke sijule, singamehluleli ngokungeyikho ngokuthathela izinto phezulu. Ukuthambekela olimini lomunye umuntu kungangemukeleka kahle uma izici esizibeka enkulumeni zinezinjongo ezingezinhle. 
   Le njulalwazi ibuza umbuzo wokuthi kungani abantu beziphatha ngendlela engamukelekile. Leli siko lokufuna ukuthi uzimele usemncane lijwayelekile entsheni ehlala emadolobheni. lkakhulukazi laba abashiya izikole bengaqedile. Yileli siko lokufuna ukuba nezinto okungezona ezabo okwenza sisebenzise Ie njulalwazi. UMarx kuHataiambos (1987: 
,. , 
kwezinto ezithandwayo nezikhona emhlabeni ezakhiwe ngabantu. Le njulalwazi ivamile emalokishini nasemadolobheni ikakhulukazi entsheni lena ejwayele ukuntshontsha izinto okungezona ezayo, izenze ezayo. Iyaye intshontshe izimoto, omakhal' ekhukhwini namakhompyutha ukuze izuze. Laba abantshontsha izimoto babiza izintombi zabo ngokuthi (Amathekeni), ngaleyo ndlela uma insizwa ingenayo imoto lokho kusho ukuthi ayinayo intombi. Yingakho-ke abaningi begcina sebezintshontsha. 
Injulalwazi yokuqonda umqondo wesikhulumi - Cognitive Uncertainty 
   UZungu (1995: 49) uthi Ie njulalwazi isho ukuthi ngesikhathi sihlangana, siba namacebo okwenza ukuthi abantu bacabange ngendlela yokuthi si;ikele indlela esenz!J. ngayo ngokufunelekile. Le njulalwazi isetshenziswa yiziboshwa, ezisuke zifuna ukuqinisekisa kwezinye ukuthi 
nazo zingena esigabeni esisodwa ngaphambi kokuthi zamukelwe. Umethuli wesiboshwa ngokujwayelekile uthi: Ungaphakama ngani? Ungangikhombisa kanjani ukuthi wena ungowaleli qembu i-25, 26, 27 noma i- 28. 
   Ukuqoka ikhowudi kulawulwa yimithetho yomndeni, ubudlelwano phakathi kwezingane nabazali, phakathi kwezihlobo, phakathi kwamalunga omndeni kanye nezivakashi. Okwesibili, ukukhetha kwekhowudi/iregista kuya ngomuntu osuke elalele, ngamanye amagama, ngubani owenza ingxenye yabalaleli nezithameli. Okwesithathu, ubuka ingqikithi yokuhlalisana kwabantu lapho izingxoxo zenzeka khona futhi ibheka ukuthi izingxoxo zenzeka endaweni ecashile, ngokusobala noma mathupha (Holmes, 1992: 6). 
   Le njulalwazi izama ukunciphisa ukungaqondi kahle kubantu abayizikhulumi ngokusebenzisa amasu azothuthukisa izimo ezahlukene zokuthola ubudlelwano (Berger & Calabrese 1975). Ithi ukukhethwa kwekhowudi noma uphawu kuncike phakathi kobudlelwano balabo ababambe iqhaza ezingxoxweni. Okunye okuhambisana nokukhethwa kolimi kwencike ekutheni simazi kangakanani umuntu owethula inkulumo, ngamanye amagama singobani thina nokuthi sikhuluma nobani, indawo kanye nengqikithi yengxoxo nenhlalo yabantu, kanjalo nomsebenzi nesihloko sengxoxo. 
   Umuntu angakhetha ikhowudi/iregista ethile ngoba kwenza kube lula ukuxoxa ngesihloko esithile, kungenza kube lula ukudlulisela imizwa yomunye ngokupheleleyo yize noma 1000 obambe iqhaza engakuqondi okushiwovo. ikakhulukazi ezimeni eziqukethe ukunvukubezwa kolimi 




kangakanani, uyohlala esebenzisa ulimi olwejwayelekile uma ekhuluma nomuntu owejwayelekile ukuze aqonde kangcono. 
   Uma abantu bezwana noma bazana, ingxoxo yabo iyakhululeka. Uma ukhuluma nabangane uyaye uzikhulumele ngendlela ejwayelekile. Isibonelo: abantu abansundu abanolwazi lwezilimi ezahlukene bajwayele ukuthi baxubanise izilimi lezo ukukhombisa izinga abakulona uma bexhumana nabangane. UMyers-Scotton (1988: 203) urhi: "Lokhu kuyinro ejwayelekile emphakathini wamazwe angawesithathu kubantu abafundile futhi abanezilimi ezahlukene. 
   Kuba izimo ezahlukene kwezinye izindawo uma umuntu esemsebenzini uyawacwecwa amagama uma ekhuluma nomqashi wakhe. Kanjalo noma kusenkantolo umuntu usebenzisa ulimi oluhambisana nabant\!abasuke belapho. Abantu abansundu bayathanda ukuthi bakhulume isiN gisi nalapho kungasafanele khona, ngoba umuntu efuna ukubukwa, usuke ethi uyadlisa phela ngoba siqhamuka esikhathini lapho ukukwazi ukukhuluma isiNgisi bekuyinto esemgangathweni. Le njulalwazi ithi uma sihlangana nabanye abantu siyaye sifune ukuthi siqagele ukuthi labo bantu baluhlobo luni ukuze sizigade furhi sikhulume Kahle ngokuziqoqa. 
Injulalwazi yokuzihlunga ngokwamaqembu ngokomuntu - Intergroup Distinctiveness 
   UTajfel uphakamisa ukuthi uma abantu abehlukene behlangana, kuba khona umkhuba wokuziqhathanisa ngamandla, izinto abanazo, izici, impumelelo njll. Ngokwale njulalwazi ukuqhathanisa izigaba zomphakathi kusiza abantu ukuthi bantshontshe isifanekiso sabo kanye nokwahlukana kwesigaba. Njengoba sazi ukuthi inkulumo ibonakala njengendlela yokuveza ubuwena neyenza kuphakame izinga nokuthandwa (Edwards, 1985: 152). Isibonelo: Izizwe zama-Arabhu zathatha isinqumo sokukhipha isaziso ngamafutha emhlabeni wonke jikelele ngolimi lwesi-Arabhu, lokhu kwakuyinkulumo yezepolitiki. Ngaleyo ndlela babengafuni ukuzwiwa ngabaseNtshonalanga abakhuluma isiNgisi. Into efanayo nokuthi ngithi ngikwazi ukukhuluma isiZulu kodwa ngingafuni ukusikhuluma enkantolo kodwa ngikhulume isiNgisi.

Injulalwazi yokuziveza ngobuwena ngokobuzwe - Affective Reinforcement 
   Le njulalwazi ithi indlela esibuka ngayo abanye abantu yeyeme ezinkolelweni kanye nasesinyathelweni labo bantu ababelana ngazo. Ibhekene nesimo lapho sifuna izinto ezifanayo nezingafani. Okunye okushiwo yile njulalwazi sikuthatha kuGrush, Clore noCostin 1975) njengoba uNdimande (2001: 21) ekuhumushe kanje: 
   "Ukuzwana kwabantu kuncike ekutheni yini ebaxhumanisayo, okungaba ukuhambisana kwemiqondo yabo kanye nezinkolelo zabo. Ibheka lezo zinto ezifanayo kubantu eziyobenza bezwane bese ibheka nalezo abehluke ngazo" 
   Le njulalwazi iyefana nesisho sesiZulu esithi "Ubucwibi obuhle obuhamba ngabubili" Kwesinye isikhathi umuntu okhulumayo akudingi ukuthi aze aqinisekise ukuthiimgubani ngaphambi kokwamukela umuntu angamazi.    Le njulalwazi igxile kakhulu emkhubeni abantu abanawo wokuhehwa ngabantu abafuna ukubahlonipha. Abantu bajabulela inzunzo abayithola ngokuheha abanye, kodwa uma nalowo muntu oheheke kuyena naye ekubona lokho. Le njulalwazi ingakhonjiswa uma umkhulumi efuna ukuzuza kubantu akhuluma nabo. Ngokwale njulalwazi inzuzo inomthelela omuhle ekwaziseni, ekubeni ukulahlekelwa kuba nomthelela omubi. UMyers-Scotton (1971: 110) uyicacisa kanje Ie njulalwazi:

Injulalwazi ka-Gramci ebizwa ngeHegemony amandla olimi 
	ENingizimu Afrika ziyishumi nanye izilimi ezithathwa 	. 
njengezisemthethweni ngokomthetho-sisekelo wezwe. Kodwa-ke isiNgisi sisabhula amaphiko njengolimi olusemqoka nolusershenziswa kakhulu kwezemfundo nakweminye imikhakha eyahlukene. Ngakho-ke ngeke sikubalekele ukuthi isiNgisi siseyingqungqulu eshaya amaphiko uma kuqhathaniswa nezinye izilimi ezisemthethweni. UNzuza (2006: 7) uthi phakathi konyaka we-191 0 nonyaka we-I 993, iNingizimu-Afrika yaphasisa inqubomgomo yobuliminingi, eyavuna ukusershenziswa kwezilimi ezimbili zabelumbi (isiNgisi nesiBhunu). U-Meyers-Scotton (1993: 149) Ie nqubo uyibiza ngokuthi i-'elite closure'. Lakhu kuchaza ukuthi abadla izambane likampondo bakhipha inyumbazane izindimbane zalabo abadla imbuya ngothi ukuba babambe iqhaza emikhakheni yezepolitiki nomnotho.Lokho bakwenza ngokuthi baphakamise izilimi njengezinkomba wkulungela ukucwila emafutheni omnotho nezepolitiki. La mkhuba wadala ukuthi ulimi IwesiN gisi lube ngungqo shishilizi luqonele ezinye izilimi, njengalokhu lwaluthathwa noma lusathathwa yizindimbane zabanru baseNingizimu Afrika nakwamanye amazwe omhlaba njengolimi olungcono uma luqhathaniswa nezinye izilimi zendabuko. Injulalwazi i-Hegemony ka-Gramsci (1971: 443), njengoba icashunwe nguNzuza (2006: 8) kuHainsworth (2000) injengamandla ezepolitiki aqhamuka ekukhalipheni nasekuziphatheni kwalabo abasebuholini, emagunyeni noma ekuvumelaneni njengalokhu kunomeWuko embuthweni wezokuvikela. Iqeqebana elincane eliholayo emphakathini lisungula 
futhi ligcine ukuqhoqhobala kwalo amandla, nalapho lisuke liqwaqwada amakhanda amanye amaqeqebana emphakathini. NgokukaGramsci (1971), alikho iqeqebana elilodwa eliqhoqhobele amanye kodwa umshikashika wokudonsisana ngokuqhoqhobala amandla phakathi -kweqeqeba elengamele nalelo elenganyelwe. Ngaphezu kwalokho, uGramsci (1971) uyeWukanisa phakathi kokubusa, lapho ukuqhoqhobala amandla kucacile futhi kwaziwa kanye ne-hegemony, lapho ukuqhoqhobala amandla kwehluke kakhulu ngoba kuba yisivumelwano nalabo abenganyelwe. Abanru baseNingizimu Afrika bavela kungathi sebekuvumele ukuthi basebenzise isiNgisi kuphela njengolimi olusemthethweni ezikhungweni nasesindaweni eziningi zikaHulumeni. 
Lesi sivumelwano esenziwe ngabantu abenganyelwe yizwe sekufinyelele esimweni lapho isiNgisi sinamandla abizwa nge-hegemony uma kuqhathaniswa nezinye izilimi zendabuko. UKamwangamalu (1997: 237) uyakugcizelela ukuthi abanru abakhuluma izilimi zendabuko njengezilimi zebele nabo baqoka ukusebenzisa isiNgisi kunokuba basebenzise izilimi zabo zendabuko. 
Ulimi luyithuluzi elisetshenziswa kwezokuxhumana, kauti futhi 
umuntu wonke ufunda ngokusebenzisa ulimi, ngakho-ke ulimi olukhethelwe ukufunda ludlala indima ebaluleke kabi ekutheni ukufunda kuba yimpumelelo noma chao UNzuza (2006: 8) uthi njengamanje kusenenkulumo mpikiswano eshubile emayelana nokuthi ulimi lokufunda nokufundisa kumele yini luthathwe njengolimi lwebele emntwaneni ofundayo noma qha. Kunezimvo ezehlukene ngalo muzwa. Abanye bavuna ulimi Iwebele njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa kanti abanye bavuna ngokungahlonizi isiNgisi njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa ezikoleni zaseNingizimu-Afrika. Umqondo wokweseka isiNgisi njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa kubantu bonke, ungumphumela womqondo nemicabango noma izinkolelo ezengamele ukusetshenziswa kwezilimi ezikoleni. Lezi zimpikiswano zibheka icala elilodwa lokufuna ukuqoka ulimi olulodwa

azibheki ukuthi kungafundiswa ngezilimi ezimbili noma ngaphezulu.

Ngokuka-Eagleton (1991: 18) abanye abantu basebenzisa igama elithi 'ideologyukubhekisa ezinkolelweni jikelele. Ngokwakhe, igama elithi 'ideology' alibhekisiwe kuphela ezinkolelweni jikelele, kodwa nasemibuzweni yamandla futhi. Emiphakathini kunezinhlaka ezehlukene ezikhona zamazinga omphakathi okujwayeleke ukuthi zingalingani ngokwemvelo (kukhona lezo 
ezengamele nezenganyelwe). Umphakathi wemukela izinkolelo zeqeqebana eliqhoqhobele amandla kanye noWelo Iwemicabango nezinkolelo 
zalo. izintambo. 
   Ngokomlando, isiNgisi nesiBhunu kuphela obekuyizilimi ezisemthethweni eNingizimu Afrika. Lezi zilimi bezisetshenziswa njengezilimi zokufunda nokufundisa ezikoleni, nokuyisimo esaqhubeka kwaze kwaphasiswa umthethosisekelo omusha, owavumela izilimi eziyishumi nanye ukuba zibe yizilimi ezisemthethweni. Le nqubo-mgomo eyayicwasa yaphakamisa isiNgisi yacindezela izilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika.  




ophathe ngokuthi ukholwe noma uthathe umqondo wokuthi izilimi ezazibalulekile eNingizimu Mrika kwakuyisiNgisi nesiBhunu kuphela., Lokhu kwakuyiqiniso, ngoba ngaphandle kwalezi zilimi zombili 
akekho umuntu owayethola umsebenzi futhi wawuba nyamanambana nakwezomnotho nezepolitiki. Njengoba izikole eziningi zazenganyelwe nguHulumeni, zagqugquzela izinhlelo zemicabango nezinkolelo zeqeqebana elaliqhoqhobele amandla ngaleso sikhathi, lokho okwakusho ukuthi isiNgisi sathathwa njengolimi lokufunda. N genxa yalokho izilimi zendabuko zabukelwa phansi, futhi nezinqubomgomo zazakhelwa ukuba zibhebhezele ukungalingani kwamandla ngamabomu kanye nokubukela phansi izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika eNingizimu Afrika, (Ndimande 2004). 
   U- Tollefson (1991:2 07) ubuka inqubomgomo njengen!9'~nye yamandla kaHulumeni okuqondisa izigwegwe lapho izinhlaka zakhe 'esikh;'ngweni somphakathi kungukuhlukanisa abantu ngokokuthi babe phakathi noma ngaphandle'. NgokukaKamwangamalu (2001, isiNgisi sibonwa ngabaningi njengolimi lwamandla ngenxa yokusetshenziswa kwaso kakhulu njengolimi lokuxhumana nokuhwebelana emsebenzini kanjalo nakwezinye izingxenye lapho kusershenziswa khona ulimi. UHeugh (2002: II) uyawufakazela umqondo kaKamwangamalu (200 I :327) lapho ekubeka kucace ukuthi isiNgisi sisaqhubeka ukusetshenziswa kakhulu ngabazali. 
   U-Tollefson (1995: 2) ubeka ukuthi imiphakathi ngaphansi kwezinhlaka zezikhungo zayo nangamandla ayo icwasa labo abangenamandla, kanti nabo bayakuvumela lokhu kuxhashazwa. U-Fairclough (1989: 32) ubalula ukuthi izwe lidlala indima ebalulekile ekutheni lisimamise umbuso weqeqebana elithile labantu abadla imbuya ngothi bengamele l~bo abakha iqeqebana labasebenzi. Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi uHulumeni unamandla okuphoqa abantu ukuthi bemukele izinkolelo zalo ngokolimi 10amandla. Obekukade kungumkhuba waseNingizimu-Mrika wukuthi isiNgisi sinikwe isithunzi, lokho okwenza abantu baseNingizimu Mrika bakholwe ngukuthi isiNgisi siwulimi olunamandla ngoba siwulimi olusetshenziswa ezinhlakeni zokuxhumana kuHulumeni. Ngesikhathi izwe laseNingizimu Mrika lithatha lowo mbono lacekela phansi izilimi zase-Mrika ezingabange zisasetshenziswa ezikhungweni zomphakathi. Ngenxa yalokho kwamukeleka ukuthi 
isiNgisi sasiwulimi lwamandla. Umphakathi uthatha ukuhlawumbisela okwejwayelekile kweqeqebana elengamele (uHulumeni) bese uvumela izinkolelo zalo njengeqiniso elaziwa yiwo wonke umuntu. 
UNzuza (2006) uthi ukuze izikole ziphumelele kwakumele ziqinisekise 
	_ 	â¢ 	â¢ 	â¢ 	â¢ T" I 	â¢ 
amathuba phambilini kanjalo nezilimi zendabuko ezazicindezelekile kumele zikhululwe ukuze abafundi bezothola imfundo ngolimi abazikhethele lona. "isikole kumele sizibumbe ukuze sivumele isimo sabafundi, kunokuba abafundi bangene khaxa enqubweni ebivele ikhona" (De K1erk, 2002). Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi izikole ezisagcine izinqubomgomo zokuqondisa izigwegwe ezindala zolimi, kumele ziguqule izinquborrigomo zazo ukuze zihambisane nezidingo zesikhathi samanje zabafundi. Isikole kumele sikulungele ukubhekelela bonke abafundi, akumele kube ngabafundi okumele bazifake ezicathulweni zesikole abakuso. Ngokuqaliswa . kwenqubomgomo yolimi kwezemfundo, uHulumeni wenrando yabantu ulindele ukuthi izikole zicubungule kabusha izinqubomgomo zazo ezindala zolimi. Izikole okumele zishintshe, hhayi abafundi. Uhlobo lothisha esinabo ezikoleni bangumphu~ela wenqubo yobandlululo, eyayivuna ukusetshenziswa kwesiNgisi njengolimi loktifunda nokufundisa ngenxa yoluthi sasithathwa njengolimi lwamandla. Lezi zinkolelo ezithwelwe ngothisha zingakapakela nakubafuhdi abangagcina sebamukela ukuthi isiNgisi sibhula amaphiko kanti izilimi zendabuko aziliboni elidlalayo. Lokho kuyobe kuchaza ukuthi inqubomgomo yolimi esershenziswa eNingizimu Mrika ihlulekile ukwenza isimo sokuthi izilimi zisetshenziswe ngendlela elinganayo. 
   Ziningi ezinye izinjulalwazi ezingabhekwa uma kuhlelwa ulimi njengenjulalwazi yobuzwe babantu yona engabhekile kuphela ekutheni abantu bathola inzuzo kanye nokuzethemba kodwa inhloso yayo enkulu ukubumbana. Okuyinto efunekayo eNingizimu Mrika. Le njulalwazi igxile kakhulu ekwenzeni uphando ngezimo amalungu omphakathi ayaye azame ukuveza ngayo ukuthi ehluke noma afana kanjani kwabanye abanru. Le njulalwazi ibalulekile uma sizohlela izilimi ezahlukene. Enye injulalwazi engabhekwa ngeyokuxhumana ngezimpawu, yona-ke ithatha ukucabanga komuntu, indlela aziphatha ngayo, njengezinro okuyirpna ezisemqoka. Umcabango kanye nokuziphatha kwencike ekutheni yiziphi izimpawu ezixhumanisa labo bantu. Izimpawu eziningi-ke zitholakala olimini. Abantu basebenzisa izimpawu ukuze baxhumane. Uphawu alumele nje into noma isehlakalo kodwa luchaza into nesehlakalo ngandlela thile. Izimpawu zinikeza incazelo esehlakalweni esithile noma kuleyo nto. 




6. IZINHLOSO ZOKUHLELWA KOLIMI 
  Izinhloso zokuhlelwa kolimi ziyashiyana. Eziningi zihambisana nezinhloso zemithetho kazwelonke. Ababhali asebebhalile ngezinhloso zokuhlelwa kolimi njengo Annamalia noRubin, 1980; uBentahila noDavies, 1993; u-Eastman, 1983; uJaht, 1993, uKaplan, 1990 noJahr (1993. UJanr (1931: 1) uthi ukuhlelwa kolimi kungenziwa ngenhloso yokunciphisa ukungezwani, kodwa kona futhi ukuhlelwa kolimi kungazidala izinkinga ezinzulu nokungezwani. UNahir (1984) simcaphuna kuKaplan noBaidauf (1997: 59) yena uqhamuke nombono wokuthi ziyishumi nanye izinhloso noma umsebenzi wokuhlelwa kolimi njengoba sizibale ngezanzi. 
1. Language purification - Ukungaxutshwa kolimi 
2. Language revival - Ukuvuselela ulimi 
3. Language reform - Ukushintsha ulimi 
4, Language standardisation - Ukuvanyiswa kolimi 
5. Language spread - Ukusatshalaliswa kolimi 
6. Lexical modernisation - Ukwenza amagama ahambisane 
neSlman)e 
7. Terminology unification - Ukuhlanganiswa kwamatemu 
8. Stylistic simplification - Ukwenza lula ulimi 
9. Interlingual communication -Ulimi lokuxhumana 
10. Language maintanance - Ukulondolozwa kolimi 
11. Auxiliary code standardisation - Ukuvanyiswa kwamagama

njalo ngenxa yokukhula kwesibalo sabantu abayisebenzisayo. Ukungaxutshwa kolimi (Language purification) 
   L~pha kub?ek~l:va ulimi ukuthi luhlale lumsulwa yini. Ukushintsha ulimi (Language refimn) 
   Ukushintsha kolimi kwenzeka lapho ulimi luba namandla futhi kungelula ukuthi lufe, futhi Jubalulekile kodwa lungakwazi ukuthi lumelane nezinto ezintsha emasikweni: Loku kwenzeka isikbathi eside ngoba kushintsha uhlelo lokubhala amagama, uhlelo lolimi. Loku kwenzelwa ukuthi kube lula ukusebenzisa .ulimi. Okushiwo ngababhali ukuthi 
zonke izilimi ziyashintsha ngenxa yokufika kobuchwepheshe obusha. Laphaya eTurkey, ngeminyaka yowe-lnO bazama ukushintsha iKemal Ataturk ngendlela eyayibhalwa ;igayo, Rabin (1971, 1976), Omar (1975), Kaplan & Bauldauf(1997: 65). Basusa amagama ayenomthelela wolimi IwasePessia, eShayina bashintsha iPin Yin (indlela yokubhala) iMalaysia neIndonesia yenza ushintsho lokupela amagama ngonyaka we-1972 ukwenza ubhalomagama luhambisane nesikbathi. 
Ukuvanyiswa kolimi (Language standardisation) 
   Ukuvanyiswa kolimi kuba inhlosonqangi yokuhlelwa kolimi nokukbishwa kolimi IwesiZulu. Abashicileli bezichazimagama bayazivuselela izichazimagama njalo emva kweminyaka eyishumi. Uma kushicilelwa izichazimagama ezintsha kanjalo nezincwadi zolimi'zifuna ukuthi zishintshwe nazo. Kubhalwe kabanzi ngale nhloso yokuhlelwa kolimi esahlukweni sesi-8 ngaphansi kwesigaba sokuhlela ikbophasi. 
Ukusatshalaliswa kolimi (Language spread) 
   Kujwayelekile ukuba ukwanda noma ukusabalala kolimi kube wumphumela wokuhlangana kwabantu abakbuluma izilimi ezingafani noma ezisondelene bahlale ndawonye. Umuntu angakbumbula ukwanda kwesiLathini ngesikbathi sombuso wamaRoma. ukwanda kwe.,;-Arahhll 




ukufika kwenkolo (njenge-Islam, inkolo yobuKristu, i-Buddhism), kwesinye isikhathi nezomnotho (isib. isiNgisi ngonyaka wezi- 2000). Eqinisweni singasho ukuthi izilimi ezikhulunywayo ziyashintshashintsha futhi kuyaziwa emlandweni yezilimi ukuthi ezinye izilimi ziyanda ezinye ziyancipha. Njengoba ukwanda kwezilimi kuyinto eqhubekayo, abakhandi bemigomo yolimi nabahleli bezilimi sebekwenze kwaba yinto ecacile. N gokwamatemu okuhlelwa kwezilimi ukwanda kolimi kuyindlela yokukhulisa isibalo 
sabantu abakhuluma ulimi oluthile kusetshenziswa olunye ulimi noma izilimi, okuholela ekugudlukeni kolimi (language shift) (isib. Wardhaugh, 1987). Ukwanda kolimi okuhleliwe, njengoba uNahir (1984) esho, 
kuvame ukuhlanganiswa nokufaniswa kolimi (language standardization) 
kanti izibonelo singabala isiHebheru kwa-Israeli (Dagut, 1985), isiSwahili eTanzania (Whitely, 1971), isiFrentshi eQuebec(d'Anglejan, 1984), i-Indonesian I Malay e-Indonesia (Alisjahbana, 1984) naseMalaysia 
(Omar, 1984), nePoutonghua eChina (Baldauf, 1990; Tse, 1982). 
Kodwa-ke ukwanda kolimi kungabuye kubhekwe njengokuhlelwa kolimi okungahleliwe (Baldauf, 1994). Abantu bayazihlanganela ngezindlela eziningi kungahleliwe emiphakathini. Isibonelo, lapho abantu behlangana, kuvamile ukuthi kube nolimi oluzosetshenziswa kube namagama angatholakala kuzichazamagama azo zombili izilimi kanye namagama asetshenziswayo kulezo zilimi, imvamisa uthole kunokushoda kwamagama ayizichasiso bese esikhundleni sawo kusetshenziswe amagama ange~o . . emthethweni. Ukwenza lufa ulimi (Stylistic simplification) 
  Ukukhula kolimi kungadala inkinga ezinhlotsheni zolimi olusetshenziswa emphakathini imihla ngemihla lapho abantu okulindeleke ukuba ho,phpn7i,p "Iimi bezithola benenkinga yokuzwa umbhalo owethulwa kubo 
ukugcwalisela umuntu ama income tax returns, ukufaka isicelo sezincwadi zokushayela, ukufaka isicelo sencwadi yokuvakashela emazweni angaphandle (passport), njalonjalo); kuzo zombili lezi zindawo, okubhaliwe kuvame ukuthi kubhalwe ngezindlela ezahlukene. 
   EMelika, izinkantolo zisebenzisa ulimi, ziluhumushe ngendlela yokuthi lube lula, noma ngubani akwazi ukuluzwa, ngamanye amazwi, wonke 
nje umuntu akwazi ukuqonda incazelo yakho injengoba injalo. Emabhukwini kahulumeni, nakhona ikhona Ie nkinga. Ngesikhathi uMengameli Carter ekhipha i-Executive Order ngonyaka we- I 978 wayefuna ukuba izikhungo zikahuJumeni zenze owazo umqulu ngesiNgisi esilula. Impendulo yalokhu kwaba wukusayindwa kwenkontileka nguhulumeni Wesikhungo Socwaningo saseMelika ukwakha iDocument Design Project, ngenhloso yokuthi kusetshenziswane nabasebenzi bezikhungo zikahulumeni, okwak~zosiza ukwenza lula imithetho elawula ukusebenza, amafomu, amamemo kanye namabhuku athile (brochures). (Chacrow, 1982: 173). IDocument Design Project ibala izinhlobo ezine zezingqinamba zemiqulu yezemisebenzi: 
* okuphathelene nokwenziwayo 
* okuphathelene nokwakheka kokubhaliwe (organizational issues) 
* okuphathelene nolimi noma ukwakheka kwemisho 
* okuphathelene nezincazelo zamagama. 
,. 	Ngokujwayelekile, i-stylistic simplification iwumzamo wokwenza 
okubhaliwe kufundeke kangcono, kuzwakale ngokucacile kwabalalele abazokusebenzisa. Kukhona abathi ukusebenzisa isiN gisi esilula akusiyo impendulo uma injongo kuwukwenza ukuxhumana o~ungcono. . Okwesibili ukuthi ulimi yiyona nto ekwazi ukwenza ukuxhumana okuhle nokuyimpumelelo. Okwesithathu ukuthi imigomo yesiNgisi esilula ayanele ekuxazululeni izinkinga zokuxhumana okungahambi kahle. Okwesine ukuthi okubhalwe ngesiNgisi esisilula kunganikeza umuntu isithombe sokuba yisehluleki ngenxa yokungabi bikho kobuchule bombhalo (abantu 




ukuba u~untu abheke ikakbulukazi Iokbo okuyiwona mlayezo odinga ukwedluhswa kanye nalabo abangabemukeli bomlayezo nendlela ulimi olusetshenziswa ngayo. 
Ulimi lokuxhumana (Interlingual communication) 
   UNahir (1984: 312) uthi ulimi lokuxhumana lusetshenziswa abantu abakbuluma izilimi ezahlukene ngokuthi basebenzise ulimi oluzokwelekelela 'olungumbombayi' ekutheni bezwane. Lolu wulimi olusershenziswa yiningi labantu njengolimi Iokwengeza. Lokbu kuhambisana nokushintshwa kwezinye zezakbi zamagama okuzokwenza ukuthi ukuxhumana 
kube yimpumelelo. Ulimi olusetshenziswa kanjena umhlaba wonke 
kungaba yisiNgisi sona esisebenza njenge lingua franca. IsiN"glsi wulimi oIukbulunywa nomaphi emhlabeni wonke. Ngale ndlela izilimi ezincane zibhekana nokwenyuka kwezinga loku'lhuJdana. Njengoba zingenasisekelo esitheni ekusetshenzisweni yimiphakathi, ziye zibonakale zingenakukbula. Njengoba lezi zilimi ezincane zingasetshenziswa ngokwanele nayiminyango yemfundo, kuyacaca ukuthi azinaqhaza elitheni ezilibambile ekuxhumaneni okusezingeni lomhlaba. Ngakolunye uhlangothi, isiNgisi sibonakala sidlondlobala ekukbuleni njenge lingua franca. 
  Ulimi lokuxhumana esifundazweni Iugxile emsebenzini wokukbuliswa kolimi Iwesifundazwe njengeSpanishi eLatin America noma isiSwahili eMpumaianga ye-Afrika, noma ekuthuthukiseni ukuzwana kubantu bamaqembu ezilimi ezisondelene. Lokbu kuhlanganisa namakomidi ezilimi zamaNordic, azama ukuvimbela izingqinamba ezifikayo nezingenasidingo phakathi kwezilimi zawo (Molde, 1975), nokuzwana okuphakathi kweMaiaysia ne-Indonesia esipelingini nakwezinyeizinguquko (Omar, 1984; Alisjahbana, 1984) kanye nezipelingi nezinye izinguquko ezisolimini IwesiDashi phakathi kweDashi neNetheriands neBeigium (van de Crean & Willemyns, 1988; van der Plank, 1988). Kulolo nalolo Iimi kulezi, abahleli bezilimi sebesebenze kakbulu ukuthuthukisa ukuxhumana kulezi zilimi. 
   Ukuhumusha nokutolika yiminxa ekbulayo emkbakbeni wezokuxhumana ngolimi. Lo mkbakba ubheka izinto eziningi kodwa ikakhulu inkinga yokuhumusha (Roberts, 1992). Abanye ochwepheshe bayakwehlukanisa ukuhumusha nokutolika. Babuka ukuhumusha njengokuhunyushwa kokubhaliwe, imvamisa imibhalo kanye nezinye izinhlobo zokubhaliwe njengolimi oluphathelene nezamabhizinisi (nif'nO"f'7ihnvnn. j7ivl1mf'lw~n() f"7ic,;pmrhf"rhwf'ni. i7ivllmt"lw::Inn 
ngolunye, njengoba kuye kwenzeke emihlanganweni yomhlaba yizifundiswa nabamabhizinisi. Lokbu kuyenzeka nasemiphakathini ngendlela egunyaziwe, njengasezibhedlela lapho isiguli kufanele sixhumane nodokotela ukuze sithole usizo, enkantolo kufunele kube notolika ukuze icala Iihambe kahle, ummangali noma ummangalelwa ezwe kahle ngolimi alwaziyo ukuthi kuthiwani ukuze angalahlwa yicala kungafanele ngenxa yokungalwazi ulimi. Nakwezezimboni futhi Iokbu sekuyanda. Ukuxhumana ngolimi kwamazwe omhlaba kudlondlobele kakbulu kulo nyaka wezi-2000, yingakbo kudingeka kube nolimi oIuzokwaziwa yiwo wonke umuntu. Nakuba ukutolika nokuhumusha sekuyisifundo abantu abagogodayo kuso, sekuke kwagxekwa ngenxa yokweswela injulalwazi. 
Ukuhumusha nokutolika esikbathini esiningi kwenziwa ngabantu, 
kodwa ikbona nemishini esetshenziselwa lokbu. Kusukela ngonyaka we1950 izinhlangano eziningi ezifana neBell Laboratories, IBM noma CIA zisebenzile ekuqinisekiseni ukusebenza kangcono kwemishini yokuhumusha. Ziningi izinhlelo zekbompuyurna esezenziwe ukwenza umsebenzi wokuhumusha, kodwa kuze kube namhlanje alukbo uhlobo Iomshini 
kumbe Iwezobuchwepheshe oIukwazi ukuhumusha ngobunyoninco. Kukbona ezinye izinhlobo zekbompuyutha ezinjengo (Globalink Power Translators, Microtac Assistants) esezirholakala nezinconywa ngokuthi 
izinga Iazo Iokuhumusha izilimi ezisemqoka zaseYurophu (isiNgisi nesiFrentshi; isiJalimane, isiNraliyana neSpanishi) Iiseqophelweni eliphezulu ngamaphesenti angama- 80% - 90%. Ososayensi baseJaphani basazama ukuhlanganisa uhlobo Iwekbompuyutha yesizukulwane sesihlanu abethemba ukuthi Iuzokwazi ukuhumusha okubhaliwe ngokucophelela okusezingeni eliphezulu ngamaphesenti angama-95%. 
Ukulondolozwa kolimi (Language maintenance) 
   Ukunakekelwa kolimi kwenzeka ngezindlela e:i.1inbili: ukunakekelwa kolimi ezingeni lomphakathi nokunakekelwa kolimi okugqamile. 
Uma ulimi olusetshenziswa emphakathini Iusengcupheni yokuthi lufe, kunesidingo esikbulu sokuba ulimi lunakekelwe futhi ngakolunye uhlangothi, ngisho nezilimi ezikbulunywa emhlabeni wonke nazo ziyadinga ukunakekelwa ukuze kuvikelwe ukulimala kolimi lubulawa yindlela engalungile olusetshenziswa ngayo. Imizamo yokunakekelwa kolimi esikbathini esiphambili kwakuhloswe ngakbo ukuba kuna kekelwe izilimi zomdabu ezazikbulunywa ngabantu abambalwa eNyakatho yeMelika, 




lokuvuselelwal ukugqugquzelwa kolimi. Emiphakathini yabomd~bu, kunenkolelo yokuthi abantwana banamhlanje basukile ngendlela exakile kusikompilo nasendleleni yesintu yokuphila, ngendlela yokuthi akubahmele ngisho ukulufunda ulimi lwabo lwesintu. Ukwanda kwalokhu kucabanga, kuchaza ukuthi abantu abasha bangeke bakwazi ukunakekela ulimi lwabo njengoba nalo bengasalwazi. Lo mkhuba siwubona kakhulu ezilimini wmdabu zase-Mrika eNingizimu Mrika. 
Okwesibili, noma yiluphi ulimi ludinga ukunakekelwa ukuze 
luvikelwe ukuba lungafi noma lungangenwa yimirhelela yezinye izilimi, isiNgisi sibonakala siyisibonelo solimi oluvama ukubulawa ngezinye. Kusobala ukuthi lapho isiNgisi sisershenziswa njengolimi lombuso noma lukazwelonke olusemtherhweni, izilimi wmdabu ziyabulawa,jzinhlamvu emagameni esiNgisi ziba lukhuni ukuziphimisa kulabo abakhuluma ezinye izilimi, ngale ndlela bazibize kanzima (kabi) lezo zinhlamvu. Kungabuye kubhekwe nakuwo uMnyango WeMfundo, lapho sithola abantwana abakhuluma ezinye izilimi bephoqelekile ukufunda ngesiNgisi, bayeke ukufunda ngezilimi zabo. Okuvame ukwenzeka ukuthi labo bantwana baphimise ngenye nje indlela ezinye zezinhlamvu, kanti iningi lezingane ezifunda isiNgisi zibe zisifundiswa ngothisha abangasikhulumi isiNgisi njengolimi lokuqala, ziye zibe nenkinga yokungaphimisi kahle amagama ngendlela efanele ngenxa yokurhi zifundiswe othisha nabo abaphimisa ngaleyo ndlela engeyona. Kuba nzima kakhulu lapho ingane iwqhubeka nohlobo lukathisha onjalo isikhathi eside ngoba leyo ngane ihamba nakho ibanga elide lokho kubiza amagama esiNgisi ngendlela okungeyona. 
N galeyo ndlela kuyavama ukuba kube negebe p~akathi kwengane efunde emakhaya (ezikoleni zikahulumeni) naleyo efunde edolobheni, ezikoleni ezazaziwa ngokuthi ngezabamhlophe ngenxa yoktifhi emakhaya kuvama ukuba kube nothisha abangasikhulumi isiNgisi njengolimi lokuqala, ngale ndlela abafundi balolu limi batholakale besukile kulokhu okulindelekile olimini IwesiNgisi. Kusemqoka-ke ukuba ukugcinwa kolimi ukuze kuvaleke igebe elibonakalayo ezinganeni zasemiphakathini eseduzane (emakhaya) nezisedolobheni. 
Ukuhlehlisa ukuguqu/wa ko/imi (Reversing Language Shift) 
   Kusobala ukuthi ukukwazi ukukhuluma ulimi okucishe kufane noma okucishe kulingane nokomuntu omdala okhuluma ulimi njengolimi lokuqala (lwebele) kuyisiqalo sokugqugquzelwa kolimi. Abazama 
Into esemqoka (futhi eyaye inganakwa noma ithathwe kalula) kukho konke okugqugquzela inqubekela phambili kuncike ekufakeni isizukulwane 
esisha ekugqugquzeleni ukusetshenziswa kolimi ukuze kutholakale ulimi olusondelene nalo kanye nempilo yomphakathi olimini olugqugquzelwayo. Intsha yaseNingizimu Mrika iyakudinga kakhulu lokhu njengoba 
ithanda ukubukela phansi izilimi wmdabu zase-Mrika. Ukuthuthuka kwezinhlangano zomphakathi ngokosiw lwezomnotho nokuqeqeshwa kwamakhono, ukubamba iqhaza kwezepolitiki, ukunakekelwa kwezingane nemfundo, ukuhlonipha inkolo, ukunakekela impilo yomzimba neyomqondo, ezemidlalo, konke okwakha ukusondelana nomphakathi wesimanje, konke kuyinsika yomphakathi wesimanje nokwesekela 
ikhaya nempilo yomndeni. Ngakolunye uhlangothi, kuyisisekelo 
semizamo yokubandakanya, imiphakathi nezikhungo ezisemqoka ezifana nezikole, amasonto, izikh~~go wlimi zikahulumeni ekulondolozeni 
ulimi. Ngale ndlela yokuthi imisebenzi eyenziwa yilezi zikhungo 
ezingenhla yake yakhishwa, okungenani engxenyeni kusetshenziswa ulimi olugqugquzelwayo, Ie mizamo ibizwa ngokuthi ukuhlehlisa ukuguqulwa kolimi. Ulimi luyabuyiselwa emumva emisebenzini eyayisondelene nalo nasemisebenzini okungathi noma yimuphi umphakathi osondelene nayo uyikhuthaze uma iwwuphumelelisa. UMamphele Ramphele (2009) uligcizelelile kakhulu iqhaza lamasonto nosomabhizinisi ekuhlumeleliseni izimpande eziqinile zokuthanda nokusebenzisa ulimi lomdabu emabandleni nasemabhizinisi. 
Okufanele sikuqaphele 
   Kukhona okufanele sikuqaphele okuyimizamo yokuhlela ulimi, okokuqala kunakho konke, lezi zinhloso ezibalwe ngenhla akufanele ukuba zithathwe njengezinto ezingasho lutho noma ezingabalulekile. Empeleni, ziyahambisana ukwenza nje isibonelo eNingizimu Mrika, izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika eziyisishiyagalolunye zidinga ukulondolozwa, kuyekwe 
ukuthi zixutshwe noma isidingo singekho, kuqhutshekwe nokwakhiwa kwamatemu ukuze zimelane nokukhula kobuchwepheshe. Uma lokhu kwenzeka kuqhubeka kuyobe kuhambisana nezinhloso zezwe laseNingizimu Mrika kanye neze-ACALAN e-Mrika yonkana. Imizamo yokugqugquzela ukuhlelwa kolimi kufanele icutshungulwe, ibhekwe kusukela emazingeni aphansi, kubhekisiswe wonke amagama asershenziswa olimini uma kuxhunyanwa. 7. IZIKHUNGO EZIBEKWE NGUHULUMENI WASENINGIZIMU AFRIKA UKUTHUTHUKISA UBULIMININGI 
   Umthethosisekelo wezwe laseNingizimu Afrika wavumela izilimi ezilishumi nanye ukuba zibe semthethweni. Lokhu kwalandelwa ukwakhiwa ngokusemthethweni kwezinhlaka zokuthuthukisa izilimi wmdabu zase-Afrika ezazincishwe amathuba phambilini kanjalo nezinye izilimi ezisemtherhweni. Izikhungo okuzoxo,;wa ngazo kabanzi kulesi sahluko Ibhodi Yezilimi Zonke ZaseNingizimu Afrika (Pan South African Language Board), UMnyango Wezamasiko, Ubuciko Newkuvasha (Department 
of Arts, Culture and Tourism), Uphiko Lwezilimi Kuzwelonke (National Language Services), kanye Nezikhungo Zocwaningo Nokuthuthukiswa Kwezilimi (Language Research and Development Centres). 
Ibhodi Yezilimi Zonke ZaseNingizimu Afrika (PanSALB) 
   Ibhodi Yezilimi ZaseNingizimuAfrika yasungulwa ngonyaka we-1995 kulandelwa umyalelo womthethosisekelo. Yaphinde yabuyekezwa ngonyaka we-1999 kulandelwa umthethosisekelo we-1996. Lasungulwa ukubhekana nobuliminingi eNingizimu Afrika nokuthuthukisa izilimi eziyishumi nanye ezisemthethweni ikakhulu~i izilimi zabomdabu. Omunye umsebenzi wabo ukuqinisekisa ukuhlonishwa kwezinye izilimi ezikhulunywayo eNingizimu Afrika. 
Umsebenzi wePanSALB 
* Ukuthuthukisa ubuliminingi 
* Ukusetshenziswa ngokulinganayo kwezilimi ezisemthethweni 
* Ukuhlonishwa kwezinye izilimi 
* Ukuthuthukisa izilimi zabomdabu ebezikade zicindezelwe 
* Ukuvulela amathuba ocwaningo kulezi zilimi 
* Ukwengamela nokubhekana namalungelO' ezilimi nokuqondisa labo abangazihloniphi ezinye izilimi 
* Ukusiza uhulumeni ekwakhiweni komthetho wolimi 
Isakhiwo se PanSALB 
  Ibhodi lezilimi linezinhlaka ezisiza ukuthi lifeze izinhloso zalo. Lezi zinhlaka zimi kan j e:

* Ukusekela umbono wokufunda ngolimi lwabazali/lwasekhaya kusukela ezingeni lemfundo labaqalayo kuze kuyofika ezingeni lemfundo eliphakeme; 
* Ukusekela ukuthuthukiswa kwabafundisi emsebenzini wabo nokuthuthukisa izinsizakufunda ukuze kunyuswe izinga lezilimi zasezikoleni zabaqalayo; 
* Ukukhuthaza ukusetshenziswa kwezilimi eziningi ezikoleni;

* Ukuqashelwa, ukukhuthazwa, nokuthuthukiswa kwazo zonke izilimi zaseNingizimu Mrika, ikakhulukazi lezo ezazishalazelwa ngaphambilini, ngemfundo yolimi lwasekhaya nangenkambiso yezilimi eziningi; 
* Okutholakele ocwaningweni olwenziwa kuze kube yimanje   	I:~: 
* Nokucabanga okunikeza isisekelo esiqinile emfundweni sibekwe entuthukweni enhle ephawulekayo esheshe yaqaliswa.

   Ibhodi Yezilimi Zonke ZaseNingizimu Afrika inohlelo lomxhaso wezimali kule mikhakha engenhla. 
  Iqhaza elibanjwe UMnyango "Wezobuciko, Ezamasiko Nezokuvakasha Kuzwelonke ekuthuthukiseni ulimi 
  UMnyango Wezobuciko, Ezamasiko Nezokuvakasha unoPhiko Lwezilimi Kuzwelonke okuyilona olubhekele ukubhalwa kwezilimi. Uphiko Lwezilimi Kuzwelonke luhlukene imikhakha emine kanje: 
* Ukuhumusha nokuhlela 
* Ukuhlanganisa amaremu 
* Ukuthuthukiswa kwenqubomgomo y~limi nokuyenza isebenze 
* Ubuchwepheshe bezilimi zabantu 	.... ~ 
  Umbono walolu Phiko Lwezilimi Kuzwelonke ukugqugquzela ubuliminingi ngokuqinisekisa ukuthi zonke izilimi eziyi-ll ezisemthethweni zithola ukuthuthukiswa nokuvikelwa okulinganayo. Lolu phiko lwenza lokhu okulandelayo: 
* Lugqugquzela ukusetshenziswa kwezilimi ezahlukene; 
* Luhambisana nokushiwo umthethosisekelo wezwe; 
* Ukwakha ubudlelwano kuzo zonke izilimi zabantu; 
* Ukuthuthukisa izilimi ebezicindezelwe emlandweni waseNingizimu Afrika; 
* Ukugcina izidingongqangi zomthethosisekelo ngokukhuthaza 
b.) Ukuhlela iziliini nemikhankaso yobuchwepheshe bokuqanjwa kwamatemu. 
* Iziko longoti bezilimi abayisisekelo sikahulumeni ngokuhumushela kuzo zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni imibhalo nemiqulu yakwahulumeni. 
* Uphiko lobuchwepheshe bamagama lwelekelela ngokuthuthukisa futhi lufake izilimi emgudwini ohambisanayo nesikhathi okuphilwa kuso, kwenziwa kuzona zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni. 
* Uphiko lokuhlela izilimi lweluleka uhulumeni ngezokuthuthukisa inqubomgomo kwezolimi kanye nezindlela zokwenza lokho kusebenze.

* Umsebenzi wokutolika ngokohlelo lwezingcingo: Ukunikezela ngomsebenzi wokutolika osezingeni eliphezulu kuhulumeni nasemphakathini ngazo zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni; 
* Izikhungo Zocwaningo Nokuthuthukiswa Kwezilimi: Ukususela kwabanye ukuthuthukiswa kwezilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika ngokuqinisekisa ukuthi kubandakanywa umphakathi; 
* Imifundaze yolimi: Ukucija amakhono ngokunikeza imifundaze kubafundi abafunda izilimi zomdabu emikhakheni efana nokuhumusha, ukutolika, ukuhlela, ukwakha amatemu,

* Ubuchwepheshe bezilimi zabantu;

ngazo zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni kulaba abalandelayo: * Iphalamende

  Iqhaza IoMnyango Wezobuciko, Amasiko Nezokuvakasha KwaZuluNatali ekuthuthukiseni izilimi 
   Ngaphansi koPhiko Lwezilimi olwalupherhwe nguMqondisi uMnumzane M pungose kuningi osekwenziwe ekurhurhukiseni ulimi ngokwemibhalo ikakhulukazi ekurhurhukiseni ukubhalwa kwezincwadi. Ngonyaka wezi-2006 lolu Phiko lusebenzisane nenhlangano yababhali 
uSiba bahambela amajele iWestville kanye neWarervailapho bekuqeqeshwa iziboshwa ebucikweni bokubhala. Zafundiswa ukubhala imidlalo, izindaba ezimfushane namanoveli. La msebenzi waba yimpumelelo ngoba kwaze kwafika lapho imibhalo lena ihlungwa khona ngokubhaleka nangokulandela umunxa ngamunye kwase kukhulunywa nabashicileli ukuba bayishicilele 
Ie mibhalo. Lezi zincwadi zerhulwe ngokusemrherhweni ngQnyaka wezi2008 enyangeni kaLwezi, zishicilelwe yinkampani yakwaNutr-end. Incwadi yokuqala irhi "Umunru Akalahlwa" iyiqoqo lezindaba ezimfushane, kanri ihlelwe ngu T.P Shabalala benoG.B. Mazibuko. Eyesibili irhi, "Ziyosulwa Izinyembezi" yona-ke iyiqoqo lezinkondlo kanri ihlelwe nguN.T. Majola noEH. Ngcongo. 
   La Mnyango ngonyaka wezi-2006 kuze kube ngowezi-2008 ube nomncinriswano wababhali abasafufusa koMasipaia bonke besifundazwe saKwaZulu-Naraii. UMnyango ubambisene nenhlangano yababhali 
uSiba baphuma umkhankaso kufundiswa umphakarhi indlela yokubhala. Kwakubhekiswe kakhulu ekubhaleni amanoveli, izindaba ezimfushane kanye nasemibhalweni yabanrwana. Ngaphandle kokurhurhukisa ukubhala kubanru abansundu bebhala ngolimi IwesiZulu kodwa furhi bekugxilwe kakhulu kubanru abasha nabesifazane. La msebe.nzi nawo waba impumelelo ngoba ngaphambi kokuphela konyaka wezi-2007 kwaba nomcimbi omkhulu wokubungaza abaphumelele kanye noku~nicilela imibhalo yabo. 
  . UNdunankulu wesifundazwe saKwaZulu-Narali, uMhlonishwa uNdebele wakugqugquzela ukuhlelwa kwezilimi nokuguqulwa kwamagama ezindawo. UMnyango wabe sewusungula ikomidi lesifundazwe e1izobheka ukuqanjwa kwamagama ezindawo kanye nokulungisa amagama ayengabhalekanga kahle. UZungu wenza ucwaningo olunzulu ebheka lawa magama angabhalekanga kahle. 
lzikhungo Zocwaningo Nokuthuthukiswa Kwezilimi (LRDCs) 
   Lezi yizikhungo zikazwelonke ezakhiwa uPhiko Lwezilimi Kuzwelonke n!!aohansi koMnvan!!o Wezobuciko Namasiko. Zakhiwela ukucwanin!!a 
kuNdasa. Lezi zikhungo zasungulwa ngesizarhu seziphakamiso zoMnyango Wezobuciko Namasiko ngonyaka we-l 997 ukuze kugcwaliswe furhi kwenziwe uhIaka Iwenqubomgomo yolimi lukazwelonke isebenze. Lakhu kusungulwa kwalezi zikhungo yigxarhu likahulumeni ukuqinisekisa inrurhuko kanye nokusershenziswa kwezilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika njengezilimi zomnorho, zepolitiki, zemfundo, zesayensi, zomrherho njll. Uphiko Lwezilimi kuZwelonke lwabe selurharha isinqumo sokurhi lixoxisane nezikhungo zemfundo ephakeme. Kwaba khona izivumelwano zokusebenzisana. 
   Injongo enkulu yezikhungo zocwaningo nokurhurhukiswa kolimi ukuqinisekisa ukurhi izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika ziyasershenziswa njengezilimi zamabhizinisi, zocwaningo, nezikahulumeni eNingizimu Mrika yonkana. Enye injongo yezikhungo zocwaningo nokurhurhukiswa kolimi ukushinrsha imibonongqangi"yabanru ngezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika nokwenza zibukeleke phansi furhi zibonakale zingenanzunzo kwezomnorho. Lezi zikhungo zingaphonsa irshe esivivaneni ngokuqala ama-projects angarhurhukisa imiphakarhi okungenza ukurhi aphumelelise izinhloso ezinkulu noshinrsho kubanru baseNingizimu Mrika. Lezi zikhungo zakhiwela ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme. Lakhu kwenzelwa ukurhi kusershenziswe amakhono asevele ekhona ikakhulukazi eMnyangweni Wezilimi. Lezi zikhungo zi~ikezwe iminyaka emirharhu kuphela. Impokophelo yoPhiko Lwezilimi kuZwelonke ukurhola ukurhi ngabe lezi zakhiwo ziyasiza yini ekwenzeni inqubomgomo yolimi kazwelonke isebenze. 
lzinhloso Zezikhungo Zocwaningo Nokuthuthukiswa Kwezilimi Lezi zikhungo zasungulelwa: 
* Ukuqinisekisa inrurhuko kanye nokusershenziswa kwezilimi ezisemrherhweni zomdabu zase-Mrika njengezilimi zomnorho, zepoliriki, zemfundo, zesayensi, zomrherho njll; 
* Ukugqugquzela nokweseka ucwaningo.lwezilimi oluhambisana nezidingo zabasebenzisa izilimi kanye nalabo abarharha izinqumo bese-ke kulondolozwa inqolobane yolwazi; 
* Ukuhlanganisa imisebenzi efanayo ukuvimbela ukuphindaphinda umsebenzi owodwa nokulahlwa kwezinsizakusebenza; 
* Ukweseka imizamo ebhekele ukurhurhukiswa kwamakhono okubhala ngezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika, lokhu kwenziwe ngokusebenzisana nezinhlangano zababhali, kwenziwe imihlangano yokucobelelana ngolwazi yababhali, njll.; 




* Ukweluleka ngezifundo ezingabenza abafundi beze bazofunda izilimi zomdabu, lokhu kwenziwe ngokukhombisa amathuba emisebenzi namathuba okuzilungiselela ukusebenza uma kunokwenzeka; 
* Ukubamba iqhaza ekuthuthukisweni kwamakhono olimi kwezinye izilimi zomhlaba ukuze abantu baseNingizimu Mtika bakwazi ukuthi babambe iqhaza ezinhlanganweni zezifunda nezamazwe ezifana ne SADC, AU, NEPAD, UNESCO nezinye. Lokhu kuzokwenziwa ngenxa yezivumelwano okungenwe kuzo. 
   Ekusebenzeni Kwezikhungo Zocwaningo Nokuthuthukiswa Kolimi kufanele zithintane nezinhlaka ezifana namakomidi olilIl.i-el'ifundazweni, amabhodi ezilimi kuzwelonke, izikhungo zezichazamagama kuzwelonke. Kungaba umqondo omuhle ukuthi lezi zikhungo zisebenzisane ukuze kungabibikho ukuphindaphinda imisebenzi kuma-projects ehlukene abanawo. Abaqondisi bezikhungo kufanele babikele iNkundla kaZwelonke yoLimi kanye nePanSALB ngomsebenzi abawenzayo. Okubalulekile okufanele kwenziwe yilezi zikhungo ukuze kuthuthuke izilimi zomdabu ukuqeqeshwa kotolika, abahumushi, abahleli bolimi ukuze umsebenzi wolimi owenziwayo kube ngowekhethelo futhi osezingeni eliphezulu. Kungumsebenzi walezi zikhungo ukuthola lawa makhono. 
  Ngesikhathi kuvunyelwana nezikhungo zemfundo ephakeme kwavunyelwana ukuthi okuyiyona mingxa okuzosetshenzelwa phezu kwayo yilena: 
* Ukukhuliswa kwezilimi nokuqanjwa by~atemu; 
* Ucwaningo nezizinda zemininingwane; 
* Ukuthuthukiswa kokufunda nokubhala ezilimini zomdabu zaseMrika; 
* Amagugu kanye nezigcina magugu zolimi; kanye 
* Nokufinyelela emphakathini noma ukusebenzisana nomphakathi. 
   Kulesi sahluko-ke ngizokhuluma ngezikhungo ezimbili zocwaningo nokuthuthukiswa kwezilimi, isikhungo seSepedi eNyuvesi yaseLimpompo kanye nesikhungo sesiZulu eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu, Ongoye.

8. IZINHLOBO ZOKUHLELWA KOLIMI 
Kulesi sahluko kuzokhulunywa kabanzi ngezinhlobo zokuhlelwa 
kolimi. Esahlukweni sokuqala lezi zinhlobo zichaziwe ngamafuphi ukuthi zikhuluma ngani. Ababhali abaningi balthetha ukwehlukanisa ukuhlelwa kolimi kabili okungukuhlela izinga lolimi nokuhlela ikhophasi. Ababhali abafana noCooper (1989) balthetha ukwehlukanisa ukuhlelwa kolimi kathathu. Kulesi sahluko ngizohambisana kakhulu nemibono kaCooper njengoba ngizokhuluma ngazo zontathu izinhlobo zokuhlelwa kolimi ngoba ngikholelwa ekutheni kumele zibe ntathu. 
Ukuhlelwa kwezinga lolimi (Status Planning) 
   Uma kukhulunywa ngokuhlelwa kwezinga lolimi kusuke kubhekwe kakhulu izinto ezifana nokukhethwa kwezilimi ezisemthethweni, kuhhekwa ukuthi yiluphi ulimi okufanele lusetshenziswe ukufundisa ezikoleni, nokufanele lusetshenziswe ezinkailtolo, kumabonisakude njl!. Uma kuhlelwa ulimi kufanele ukuthi umphakathi uthathe izinqumo ngolimi oluqokiwe, futhi ube nendlela yokuqoka ulimi ukuze lukwazi ukuthi lusatshalaliswe kubantu. Lena ngenye yezindlela eyenza ukuhlelwa kolimi kuphumelele. Ukuhlela izinga lolimi kunemigomo emibili ebalulekile: ukukhethwa noma ukuqokwa kolimi okwenza ulimi lusebenze. 
  Ukukhethwa kolimi kweyeme emthethweni wolimi. Ulimi lukhethwa ngumphakathi ngokusebenzisana nabaholi bezepolitiki. E-Mrika 
emazweni athola inkululeko ngeminyaka yowe-I960 kwadingeka 
ukuthi babe nolimi ababezolusebenzisa ukuxhumana. Isikhathi esiningi bekuba khona izilimi ezimbili, ezintathu noma eziningi. Ngaleyo 
ndlela, kudingeke ukuthi uhulumeni aqoke ulimi olulodwa oluzokuba ngolokuxhumana nolusemthethweni. ENamibia ngonyaka we-I 990 emva kokuthola inkululeko isiNgisi saba ulimi olusemthethweni, ezinye izilimi bezisetshenziswa nje. ENingizimu Afrika izilimi ezisemthethweni ziyishumi nanye. Ukukhetha ulimi olusemthethweni akuyona into elula ngoba kusuke kukhethwa ezilimini eziningi, eziqhudelanayo. Ukuhlela izinga lolimi ngokubhala kuka Webb (2002)) kubandakanya: 
* Ukuhlelwa kolimi 
* Ukuqoka ulimi lokufunda nokufundisa 
* Ulimi olusemthethweni 
* TTlimi lnL-llvhllm';ln~ T<:ihnnpln I1kllrhllthllki.li;w~ kwf'5:iHf'hhe:rlJ 
* Ukushintsha indlela ulimi olusebenza ngayo 
* Ukwenza ulimi lusebenze 
* Ukuhleleka kwezinsizakusebenza zolimi 
* Ukuhlola 
UStewart (1968) yena uthi ukuhlela izinga lolimi kubandakanya 
izimpawu ezilandelayo: 
1) Uphawu lokuba semthethweni 
2) Uphawu lwesifundazwe 
3) Uphawu lokuxhumana 
4) Uphawu Iwamazwe omhlaba 
5) Uphawu lomnotho 
6) Uphawu lweqembu 
7) Uphawu lwemfurttlo 
8) Uphawu lokuba isifundo esikoleni 
9) Uphawu lobuciko bokubhala 
10) Uphawu Iwenkolo . 
   Kubalulekile ukubheka ukuth\ lapha eNingizimu Mrika ngesikhathi kuhlelwa ulimi zabhekwa yini ezi;"ye zalezi zimpawu ezaphakanyiswa nguStewart (1968). Ngizoqala ngizibuke kabanzi lezi zimpawu okumele zibhekwe uma kuhlelwa izinga loliini bese nginikeza izibonelo. Ngizobe sengihlola ukuthi abanye abacwaningi abafana noKamwangamaiu (2000) bathini ngokuhlelwa kwezihga lolimi eNingizimu Mrika.

UStewart (1968) wasungula imisebenzi elishumi okumele ulimi 
luyenze njengomhlahlandlela wokuhlelwa kolimi kubhekwa isimo sezepolitiki, waqhubeka wanikeza Ie misebenzi izimpawu. Uphawu lokuqala u-O (Official) lapho ulimi luhlonzwa nguHulumeni njengolimi olusemthethweni, nokumele lusetshenziswe ePhaiamende nakwezinye izindawo zezwe. Uphawu Iwesibili uphawu u-P (Provincial), lapho uphawu olusemthethweni lungelona olukazwelonke kodwa kiingolwesifundazwe. Uphawu Iwesithathu uphawu olumele ukuxhumana okubanzi okungu-W (Wider Communication), lapho ulimi lubamba iqhaza kwezokuxhumana, kungalthathalekile noma ngolukazwelonke noma lungolwesifundazwe. Uphawu lwesine, nolusondelene nokuxhumana okubanzi ngu-I (International) omele izinga lamazwe omhlaba, lapho ulimi lusebenza njengethuluzi ekuxhumaniseni izalthamuzi zelinye izwe nezakwamanye amazwe. Uphawu Iwesihlanu oluphakanyiswe nguStewart wuphawu u-C, omele (Capital), lapho ulimi lugxile kalthulu kunhlokodolobha yezwe 




17. 
njengesizinda sokuxhumanisa amalungu eqembu elixhumana ngezamasiko nezobuhlanga, isibonelo nje isizwe. Umsebenzi wesikhombisa wolim~ umelwe wuphawu u-E, omele ezemfundo (Educational), nalapho ulimi lusuke lusebenza njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa emazingeni aphansi naphezulu ezemfundo, ezifundazweni nakuzwelonke. Umsebenzi wesishiyagalombili owenziwa wulimi umelwe wuphawu u-S, omele isifundo (School Subject), lapho ulimi lufundiswa njengesifundo emabangeni emfundo asethe thuthu nalawo aphakeme. Uphawu lwesishiyagalolunye wuphawu u-L, omele u (Literary), lapho ulimi lusetshenziswa kwezobuciko bokubhala. Umsebenzi weshumi nokungowokugcina owenziwa wulimi ngokuka-Stewart umelwe wuphawu u-R, omele inkolo (Religious), lapho ulimi lusetshenziswa ngokuxhumana namasiko kanye nezingu~o zenkolo ethile. Ngokwengeziwe kule misebenzi yolimi eyaphakanyiswa ngu- 
Stewart, uCooper (1989: 118), wabuye wengeza imisebenzi emibili eyenziwa wulimi, okungabengamele izindaba uelIlisebenzi yabanru, lapho izinhlclo zisetshenziswa nguHulumeni ukukhulisa nokucindezela izilimi ezikhethiwe, nalapho ulimi lusetshenziswa njengomgudu wokuxhumana emsebenzini. 
   UKamwangamalu uke wacubungula kabanzi inqubomgomo yobuliminingi eNingizimu Mrika, ikakhulukazi uma kubhekwa indlela okusetshenziswa ngayo izilimi ezikhungweni ezithile eNingizimu Mrika. Izindawo ayebheke kuzo kakhulu ngumabonisakude, kwezemfundo, kuHulumeni kanye nasendleleni okuqhutshwa ngayo kwezokwengamela izwe. Ngizobheka-ke injwayezi yezikhungo ezithile lapha eNingizimu Mrika yokulandelanisa izilimi ngokohlelo lokubaluleka kwazo, ngaphandle kokulandela umthetho, Ie njwayezi ibekwa ngohlelo oluyizitebhisi, lapho isiNgisi sithe chwa phezulu, kube yisiBhunu phakathi nendawo bese 
kuba yizilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika phansi. UKamw~ngamalu (2000:50) ugcizelela ukuthi kumele kubhekwe kabusha inqubomgomo yobuliminingi, ngomqondo wokuthatha inqubo evulelekile, nehlabahlosile yokubhekana nokuhlelwa kolimi kubhekwa isimo sezepolitiki. Lokho okungaqinisekisa ukuthi izwe liyophumelela emizamweni yalo yokuthuthukisa nokuphakamisa izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika. 
UCooper (1989) udingide kanzulu ngo-Stewart (1968) nombono 
wakhe wokuthi ulimi kumele Iwenze muphi umsebenzi ngaphambi kokuthi lubhekelelwe ohlelweni lokuhlelwa kolimi, ikakhulukazi isimo solimi ngakwezepolitiki. Ekudingideni kwakhe, uCooper uvumbulule iqiniso . lokuthi ulimi nolimi lunomsebenzi okumele luwenze, kusukela emkhakhem 
I". '1' T 
oluningi olwenziwe emazweni athile emhlabeni wonke jikelele luveza ukuthi izilimi zengcindezelo zisabhula amaphiko [isiDashi, isiNgisi, isiFulenrshi nesiPutukezi] njengezilimi ezixhumanisa izizwe ezikhuluma izilimi ezehlukene, kanye nezilimi zomnotho, ubudlelwano phakathi kwamazwe kanye nezepolitiki. Le nqubo engakaguquki izithwalisa kanzima izilimi zomdabu, ezijwayele ukubamba iqhaza elikhulu ekuxhumaniseni amasiko nezinhlanga ezehlukene, njengokophawu u-G, olumele iqoqo olwasungulwa ngu-Stewart (1968). Ngakho-ke izilimi zomdabu njengamanje eNingizimu Mrika ziyathuthukiswa ukuze nazo zigcine sezifinyelele esimweni; 
noma ezingeni lokuba yizilimi zokuxhumana ezingeni lomhlaba kanye nakwezamaphephandaba nasemisakazweni (Cooper, 1989; Stewart, 1968). 
   Uhlelo lokuhlelwa kolimi lungumsebenzi ongumshikashika nodinga isineke, ngenxa yokuthi izilimf zomdabu zase-Mrika bezinganakiwe 
futhi zicindezelwe phambilini, kanti futhi zaphucwa amandla yizilimi zabelumbi. Ngakho njengamanje angeke zivele zisukume zilingane ncamashi nezilimi zabelumbi. Yize noma kwamanye amazwe izilimi zomdabu zaseMrika seziphucwe amandla yizilimi zabelumbi njengezilimi zomnotho, ezepolitiki kanye nokuxhumana ngokobudlelwano, isibonelo isiSwahili 
e Tanzania, amazwe amaningi e-Mrika asalandela inqubomgomo evuna izilimi zabelumbi njengezilimi zokuxhumana kanye nezilimi zikazwelonke, isibonelo e-Namibia ulimi olusemthethweni yisiNgisi kuphela. Amanye amazwe asafunga, ngokusebenzisa izinqubomgomo ukunika izilimi zendabuko izinga elifanayo nalelo lezilimi zabehifubi, kodwa 10 mbhidlango ugcina ngokubhalwa phansi ungasetshenziswa ngokuphathekayo. Singeke sikushaye indiva ukuthi kwezinye izikhathi izilimi zabelumbi zisabamba iqhaza elibalulekile kwezokuxhumana, kodwa-ke hnhi umuntu akumele alibale imizamo eyenziwayo yokufukula izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika. Ngakho-ke uma kuhlelwa izinga lolimi kubhekwa ulimi ngakwezepolitiki, amaqiniso anjengalawa akumele ashaywe indiva, ngoba lokho kuyimbangela yokuthi isiNgisi silokhu sibhula amaphiko njengolimi olusemthethweni njengaseNamibia nakoZimbabwe. 
   UKamwangamalu (2000) ubheke ngeso elibanzi inqubomgomo yolimi eNingizimu-Mrika ebalula ukuthi zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni kumele zithole ukuhlonishwa okuzifanele kanye nokuphathwa ngendlela elinganayo. Ubeka umuzwa wokuthi inqubomgomo ayikabi yinto ephathekayo uma kubhekwa indlela izimo ezenzeka ngayo ezikhungweni zaseNingizimuAfrika, isibonelo komabonisakude bomphakathi, ezokusakaza, ezemfundo,

okungumshoshaphansi njengohlaka lokuthuthukisa izilimi zendabuko e-Afrika. UKamwangamalu akablonizi ikakhulukazi ngalesi siphakamiso sakhe senqubo-mgomo evuna umrhetho wobuliminingi obhekelela izimfuno zezilimi zomdabu eNingizimu-Afrika, ezinikwe izinga lokuhlonishwa elithi alilingane. ENingizimu-Mrika kuyiqiniso ukuthi uma kuqhathaniswa 
izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika nesiNgisi nesiBhunu kutholakala ukuthi azisershenziswa ngendlela elinganayo. Isizarhu salokhu phela ukuthi 
akumele sikulibale kalula nje ukuthi izilimi zomdabu kade zicindezelekile ngenxa yemiphumela yobandlululo. Ngesikharhi sobandlululo iNingizimu Mrika yakhipha inqubomogomo yobulimimbili, lapho isiNgisi nesiBhunu kwakuyizo kuphela izilimi ezazisemrherhweni, kufundiswa furhi kufundwa ngazo ezikoleni, zisershenziswa ePhalamende, kwezomnotho, }<wezepolitiki kanye nakwezezindaba kudluliswa imibiko. Ngaphezu kwalokho izilimi zomdabu zagqilazwa wuhlelo lomthetho wemfundo yabantu owenza 
kube yize ukusetshenziswa kwazo futhi zazivinjelwa ukuba zisetshenziswe kwezomnotho nakwezamandla ezepolitiki, Sookrajh (1990), Ndimande (2004). Lesi simo saze sa/lnyelela ekutheni ngisho amathuba emisebenzi ayevuleleke kuphela labo ababehlafuna isiNgisi nesiBhunu. Lesi simo sadlondlobala kakhulu ngesikhathi sikaHulumeni wobandlululo, kanti umthelela waso usabonakala namanje. 
  Ngenxa yemiphumela yobandlululo, ama-Afrika uqobo lwawo aba nomqondo wokubukela phansi izilimi zawo. Ngaphezu kwalokho azithatha njengezingabalulekile futhi ezingaliboni elidlalayo uma kuqhathaniswa nezilimi zabelumbi. Yingakho indlela u-Kamwangamalu aqhathanisa ngayo isiNgisi nesiBhunu nezilimi zendabuko emigudwini yokudlulisa imibiko noma izindaba njengomabonisakude, kwezemfund(), ezinkantolo kanye nezombutho wezokuvikela ingabhekelelwa nhlobo 'eminye imisebenzi okumele yenziwe wulimi, ikakhulukazi leyo ebalulwe ngu-Stewart kanye no-Cooper. Isibonelo imisebenzi emithathu okumele yenziwe wulimi ebalulwe ngu-Stewart, enjengokuxhumana okubanzi enophawu u- W; eyezinga lamazwe omhlaba u-I, kanye nophawu u-C, lapho izilimi zisetshenziswa njengemigudu yezokuxhumana ezingeni lenhlokodolobha, kanjalo nakwelikazwelonke, ayihambisani nesimo esiqhubekayo sendlela okuphethwe ngayo izilimi zomdabu eNingizimu-Mrika. Le misebenzi emithathu ebalulwa ngu-Stewart (1968), ikakhulukazi leyo emibili okungukuxhumana okubanzi (Wider Communication-W), kanye nezinga lomhlaba (International-I) ibheka isidingo solimi ezintweni ezifana

Uqhubeka aphawule ngokuthi uma ulimi lungolwangaphandle ngempela, isikole yiyona ndawo enhle yokuthi 1010 limi lufundwe. 
   Izilimi zomdabu zaseNingizimu Mrika okwamanje zisangena khaxa kweminye yemisebenzi ebalulwa ngu-Stewart, isibonelo sophawu 
Iweqoqo, sokuba isifundo sasesikoleni, zisetshenziswe emibhalweni kanye nakwezenkolo. Okuphawulwa ngu-Kamwangamalu ukuthi izilimi zomdabu zaseNingizimu-Mrika kumele zithole ukuhlonishwa njengesiNgisi. Isibonelo, kwezemfundo ubalula ukuthi ngaphandle komgomo womthetho-sisekelo othi 'wonke umuntu kumele athole imfundo ngolimi azikhethela lona uma lokho kungenzeka ngokwezinsiza ezikhona (Umthetho-sisekelo, isabluko 32 (c), ucashunwe nguKamwangamalu, 2000:55). Uqhubeka abalule ukuthi asikho isigameko esesike sabikwa sabafundi baseNingizimu Mrika abafuna ukufundiswa ngezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika. Konke lokho kushayela isipikili kulokho engike ngakubalula ukuthi umphumela wobandlululo usabonakala endleleni ezithathwa ngayo izilimi zendabuko eNingizimu-Afrika. 
Imiqondo yethu isasemaketangweni engcindezelo kanti kuzotharha isikhathi ngaphambi kokuthi sisamukele lesi simo bese senza okuthile. 
   Intando yabantu yaseNingizimu Mrika yayisakhasa ngesikhathi uKamwangamaiu eqhamuka nalezi ziphakamiso. UHulumeni waseNingizimu Mrika usukhiphe amangwevu ukuqinisekisa llkusimama kwentando yabantu. kakhulu abantu abansundu eNingizimu Mrika ngezilimi zabo. Imithetho eyayiphoqwa yaba nomthelela engqondweni nasendleleni abantu baseAfrika ababuka ngayo izilimi zabo uqobo. Ngisho namanje, uma ngingenza isibonelo abantu baseNingizimu-Mrika abansundu basadansela isigingci esishaywa yisiNgisi nesiBhunu njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa ezikoleni.   ENingizimu-Afrika, izilimi zase-Afrika sezenze imizamo ebonakalayo ikakhulukazi emva kokhetho lonyaka we-1994. Lokhu kubonakale 
ngeqhaza elibanjwe izikhungo ezifana nemithombo okudluliswa ngayo izindaba nemisakazo yomphakathi. Inhlangano Yokusakaza eNingizimuAfrika, (SABC) yasetshenziswa kakhulu nguHulumeni wobandlululo njengosomlomo wayo esikhundleni sokuthi ibe ngunogada wayo, okuyinto elindelekile kumsakazi womphakathi. Ngokuphambene nalowo muzwa i-SABC yayisekela isihluku sikaHulumeni wobandlululo, ezinhlelweni zayo zezindaba. Kodwa-ke, ukukhululwa kwamagagasi omoya kwaletha uguquko olusheshayo kusukela kuHulumeni wobandlululo kuya kuHulumeni wentando yebantu, eyeza noguquko olusemqoka kwa-SABC, futhi njengamanje kunezinhlelo ezisakazwa ngezilimi ezehlukene zase-Afrika. Okungumphumela osobala ngokwandiswa kwesikhathi esinikezwe izinhlelo zezindaba ezisebenzisa izilimi zendabuko, okuyisinyathelo esathamwa yisigungu sabaqondisi be-SABC esasiholwa nguDali M pofu. 
  Ngasemkhakheni wezemfundo, kusenenselelo enkulu uma kubhekwa indlela okusetshenziswa ngayo izilimi zase-Afrika. IsiNgisi yisona esisengungqo shishilizi, njengalokhu izifundo eziningi zesayensi nobueiko zisafundiswa ngesiNgisi. UKamwangamalu (2000: 55) ubalula ukuthi isidingo sokusebenzisa ulimi lwesiNgisi njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa kunolimi lwebele kumele ngakolunye uhlangothi siqonde ngokubhekisisa amandla esiNgisi kwezenhlalo nomnotho kanye nokumi isiNgisi siwulimi olusezingeni lomhlaba kanye nomthelela woMthetho_Wemfundo Yabantu. Kubalulekile ukuphawula futhi ukuthi othisha basahudula izinyawo ekutheni baqalise ukusebenzisa izilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika ezinhlelweni zokukufundisa ezikoleni. Isizathu esisemqoka salokhu kunqaba, wukuvumela umqondo wokuthi izilimi zase-Afrika zisezingeni eliphansi uma ziqhamanizwa nezilimi zabelumbi. Ngakho uphawu luka-Stewart u-E, omele ezemfundo, nobalula ukusebenza kolimi njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa emazingeni emfundo aphansi naphezulu lusahlangabezane nezinqinamba ezinkulu eNingizimu Afrika.

  Abahleli bolimi bangaqhamuka nohlaka olungeke Iwagculisa umphakathi wonke. Isibonelo, abahleli bolimi bangahlela indlela yokupela amagama alula/afundeka kalula, asebenziseka kalula, eyonga imali ishicilelwe ngenani elingabizi. Umphakathi ungakwemukela ukushintsha noma ungakwemukeli nhlobo. Ngesikhathi amaJuda esebenzisa isiHebheru njengolimi lokufundisa ezikoleni kwadingeka ukuthi bakhe amagama amasha othisha nabafundi ababengawasebenzisela ukuxoxa ngezifundo ezintsha ezazifundiswa ezikoleni. Ngonyaka we-I904 inyunyana yothisha yavuselela Umkhandlu wolimi IwesiHebheru owawufe izinyanga eziyisithupha emva kokuba wawusungulwe uBen Yehuda ngonyaka we- I 980, ukugcina izidingo zezikole. Emva kokuba I-Itish yaqokwa njengolimi olusemthethweni e-Ireland kwadingeka ukuthi kubhalwe kabusha ubhalomagama lwalo. 
  Ukuhlelwa kwekhophasi akudalwa ukuthi ulimi selwenza omunye umsebenzi, okunye futhi okubalulekile umsebenzi/ukusebenza yikona okuhamba phambili kulandelwa isakhiwo. Izibonelo ezingenhla zokuhlelwa kwekhophasi ziveza izinhlobo ezahlukene zokuhlela ikhophasi.

Ukulinganisa Ulimi (Graphization) 
   UFetguson (1968) uveza izindlela ezintathu ezingahlelekile ezingasetshenziswa ukuqhathanisa intu~u~? ~oli~i. Lo~u k~ng~nziwa 
ngumsebenzi wabantu abaningi ikakhulukazi amamishinari amaKr05tu okuyiwona abambe iqhaza elikhulu esikhathini sanamhlanje. Ekuhlelweni kwekhophasi kuyenzeka kuthathwe isinqumo sokuqamba indlela entsha yokubhala ulimi. 
Okufanele kuqashelwe ukuthi into okulula ukuthi uyifunde 
kungaba nzima ukuyidlulisela. Imibhalo eminingi yakhiwe ukuguqula ubhalomagama /ukulotshwa kwamagama. Ubhalomagama luyibhuloho lalabo abasuke bengakwazi ukubhala nokufunda ulimi 1010 esizweni 1050. Eqinisweni ukufunda ukubhala nokufunda kwenzeka ngolimi lomfundi lokuqala. Kunobufakazi obushayisanayo obugunyaza ukuthi ulimi lokubhala nokufunda lunikezelwe ngolimi lokuqala. Ekubeni injongo ekugcineni ukwazi ukubhala nokufunda ngolimi Iwesibili. Uma kusetshenziswa ulimi lokuqala ukufunda nokubhalailokhu kuyaye kumsize umntwana ngoba ulimi usuke elukhuluma kunokumfundisa ngolimi lwesibili. Kuyaye kube lula futhi ukudlulisela ukubhala nokufunda ukususa olimini lokuqala kuya kolwesibili uma izindlela zokubhala zifana noma futhi umfundi elwazi ulimi Iwesibili. Ubudlelwano phakathi kobhalomagama nezinguqukomsindo lubalulekile uma kudingeka ukuthi kuguqulwe ubhalomagama lolimi. 
Ubhalomagama lwezilimi luyaye luncike kakhulu kulolo limi lwababusi.

UHaugen uthi ulimi into eyenzeka engqondweni yomuntu ongeke uyiqhathanise namathuluzi abantu abawasebenzisayo ukuqonda abantu nendawo abahlala kuyo. 
   Ukuvanyiswa kubona bonke abantu kungukuzikhohlisa, yize noma ngabe kungenzeka kutholakale ulimi oluvanyiswe ngokuphelele, lungaba njani? Ulimi oluvanyisiwe yilolo limi olwamukelwe ukuthi lungasetshenziswa kunoma iziphi izimo, kuzokwenziwa uguquko oluncane nje kuphela. Umahluko esifundazweni, emphakathini, ekukhulunyweni nasekubhaleni mncane kakhulu. Izinkolelo zokuvamisa ulimi zihambisana oofQqondo wokuthi kukhona ukusebenzisa ulimi ngendlela elungile nokuthi kufanele abantu balandele leyo ndlela. Ulimi olukhulunywayo alunakwa kakhulu kodwa olubhalwa phansi oluba nokuhlonipheka kunalolo olukhulunywayo. Lokho kuyiqiniso ngoba: 
* Sikhulu isidingo sendlela eyodwa yokubhala ulimi kuneyokukhuluma 
* Kulula ukuyedlulisela ezikoleni 
   Isibonelo: Ngokwejwayelekile kunendlela eyodwa evamile yokubhala ulimi IwesiN gisi kumaZwe onke omhlaba asebenzisa isiN gisi, kodwa kunesiNgisi esahlukahlukene esikhulunywa esifundaZweni, kuzwelonke njll. Okuyiyona ndlela eba semthethweni ileyo ebhalwe phansi. 
   Ubulthona besiBhunu neNethetland eNingizimu Afrika. IsiBhunu saba uphawu lobuzwe bamaBhunu. Uma ukuvanyiswa kolimi kufeza izinjongo zamaqembu azisa ubuzwe bawo kanjalo futhi kufeza iziilhloso zabaningi emazweni omhIaba. U-Ansre (1971) uthi okuyibona bantu ababamba iqhaza ekumiseni izilimi eSub-Saharan Mrika ngabaseNtshonalanga neYurophu abenza imizarno yokuvamisa izilimi kwezokuphatha, ezemfundo nasenkolweni. 
Ukuhlelwa kwemithetho (Codification) 
Izindlela zokuvamisa ulimi zahlukaniswe uRubin (1977) kasithupha: 1.) Ukwahlukaniswa kohlelo/inkambiso 
2.) Ukuhlaziywa kohlelo/inkambiso 
3.) Ukuthakwa kohlelo/inkambiso kwenzelwa isimo esithile 4.) Ukwamukelwa 
   Okunguwona mgomo wako konke lokhu yikona ukuhlelwa kwemithetho. Lena imithetho ebhalwe phansi. Igama le-"codification" lisuselwa kwelesiLathini "codex" elisho okubhalwe phansi. Ukuvanyiswa kolimi kuyenzeka ngomlomo kodwa futhi nangokubhala phansi kuyenzeka. Ubukhona bezichazimagama, izincwadi zohlelo lolimi, ukupelwa kungukuvanyiswa kwezilimi ezibhalwe phansi. Uma ulimi lungabhaliwe phansi lokhu kuyenzeka ngomIomo njengoba kwenziwa uma kuxoxwa izinganekwane kusikompilo lama-Mrika bese umthetho lowo ugcina sewaziwa ngabantu bonke. 
   Isibonelo sokuhlelwa kwemithetho: Ukwakhiwa kwesichazimagama sokuqala sesiNgisi ngonyaka we-I775 lesi sichazimagama yisona esasiza ukuthi kuvanyiswe isiNgisi eNgilandi nguSamu'el Johnson. Ukuhlela ukufimdwa nokwamukelwa kolimi (Acquisition Planning) 
   Ukuhlela ukufunda nokwamukelwa kolimi kuchaza imizamo eqondene nokuthuthukisa izinga lokufundwa kolimi. Ziningi izibonelo ezikhona zemizamo yokufunda ulimi. ENyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali singakhuluma ngezifundo: zesiZulu, zesiNgisi, zesiFtentshi nezinye izilimi. Lesi sigatshana sokuhlelwa kolimi sibalulekile n"ezizathu ezimbili: 
izinga lokusetshenziswa kolimi lokho kungena ngaphansi kokuhlela izinga lolimi. Kodwa uma kubhekiswe ekutheni kwenyuswe inani labantu abasebenzisa ulimi, Iwababhali, lwabalandeli, Iwabafundi kudingeka esinye isigaba eceleni. 
2.) Ukushintsha kokusebenza nesakhiwo solimi okwenziwa ukuhlela izinga neKhophasi kukhinyabeza inani labantu abasebenzisa ulimi. Abasebenzisi bolimi abasha bangabehwa ukusebenza okusha kolimi isib. Uma ulimi luqala lusebenza Ilusabalala njenge 'Lingua Franca' uma senza isibonelo singathatha isiSwabili eTanzania nakwamanye amazwe angomakhelwane nesiHebheru ePalestine, ulimi luba 
usizo bese luheha abakhulumi abaningi, kungaba isiZulu, singakwenza yini lokhu lapha eNingizimu Afrika? Abakhulumi abasha bangaqhagmka nendIela entsha yokusebenzisa ulimi. Kukhona abanye 'abangabambisani nendlela yokuthi ukufundwa nokwamukelwa kolimi kungene ngaphansi kokuhlelwa kolimi. Lokhu kudala ukuthi kavele kukhona ukungaboni ngaso linye ngokufaka ukuhlelwa kolimi ngaphansi kwe- "Applied linguistics." 
   UCooper (1989) uthi lapha kulolu hlobo lokuhlela kusuke kukhulunywa ngemizamo ehlelekile yokuthuthukisa ukufundwa kolimi. Isibonelo kungathathwa izwe lakwa-Israel okuthe uma kufika izifikanamthwalo zasizakala lapha ngokuthi zifunde isiHebheru. Izindawo lapho zazifikela khona kwakuba nezifundo zesiHebheru, ezazithatha izinyanga eziyisithupha. Lokhu kwakwenzeka ngesikhathi besalungiselelwa izindawo zokuhlala, imisebenzi. Ezinye izifundo zenziswa ngomasipala kodwa kuyakhokhwa. AmaNyuvesi anezifundo zolimi zabafundi abafikayo abavela kwamanye amazwe. Uma abantwana bezifikanamthwalo bengena ezikoleni bafundiswa ngesiHebheru njengolimi lwesibili. Kunephephandaba eliphuma masonto wonke elishicilela ngaso belu isiHebheru. Kune~ndaba ezisakazwa nsuku zonke izinsuku ngesiHebheru naltumabonisaltude kukhona izinhlelo ezisakaza ngesiHebheru. Ukuthuthukisa ukufundwa kwesiNgisi, umkhandlu waseBrithani ugcina kukhona imitapo yolwazi emazweni omhlaba futhi uhambisa ongqondongqondo ukuze benze izinkuthazakwenza lapho beqwashisa khona ngezindlela zokufundisa. 9. UKUHLELWA KOLIMI E-AFRIKA 
  Ngaphambi kokuthi ukuhlelwa kolimi kube yingxenye yokufundwa kolimi lomphakathi, eqinisweni izingxoxo zokuqala zokuhlelwa kolimi eNingizimu Mrika zaba phakathi kwamaMishinari kanye nabafundi ababenomqondo wokuthi kube khona ubhalomagama ezilimini 
zesiXhosa nesiZulu. EMpumalanga Mrika benza isinqumo sokuthi izilimi zezigodi zaseZanzibar zeSwahili zibe ulimi lwesizwe kunokuba kube 
ulimi olukhulunywa eMombasa. Amamishinari aqhamuka nombono wokuthi kulula ukuphendula abantu ngenkolo besebenzisa izilimi zabo. Amamishinari nabefundisi yibona ababehlela ulimi e-Mrika. UBamgbose (1991: Ill) uthi amazwe afana neCongo, Ghana, Kenya, Nigeria, Senegal, Zambia, neSierra Leone ahluleka ukwenza inqubomgomo yolimi isebenze. EMpumalanga Mrika emazweni afananoKenya, Tanzania, no-Uganda ukuhlelwa kolimi bekuwucwaningo olunzulu eminyakeni eminingi edlule. Kulesi sahluko kuzobhekwa amazwe amane okuyiTanzania, iNamibia, iMalawi neZimbabwe ukuthi a1uhlele kanjani ulimi kanjalo nemithetho yolimi esebenza kulawa mazwe. 
Ukuhlelwa kolimi eTanzania 
  ITanzania izwe laseMpumalanga Mrika, umengameli wakhona nguBenjamin Mkapa kanti inhlokodolobha yakhona iDar Es Salaam. Izilimi ezisemthethweni: IsiSwahili nesiNgisi. Abelumbi beTanzania iBrithani. ITanzania ithole uzimelegeqe ngonyaka we-1961 ngaphansi kombusi wokuqala omnyama uDokoteia uJulius Nyerere. ITanganyika yahlangana neZanzibar kwabe sekuphuma iTanzania. ITanzania'yaziwa kakhulu ngegalelo layo ekuhlelweni kolimi emazweni ase-Mrika. UPillay (2007: 42) yena uthi leli lizwe lenza umlando ongeke wakhohlwa emhlabeni wonke jikelele. Kuthe ngokungena kukamengameli onsundu uJulius Nyerere kwaphenduka amatafula ngasemthethweni noma inqubomgomo yolimi, lokhu akubanga into elula nje. Inqubomgomo yolimi kanye nokuhlelwa kwalo akuyona into eyayenziwa ngabezepolitiki noma izazi zilimi njengoba kwenzeka manje. 
Inqubomgomo yokusebenza kolimi

Ukuhlelwa kolimi uma kwenziwa ucwaningo kuncike ekusetshenzisweni kwezilimi ezahlukene kanye nenhlalo emphakathini. Kwaba khona imibono eminingi mayelana nokuhlelwa kolimi olusetshenziswa ngamaqembu ezombusazwe, uhulumeni kanye nososayensi bezilimi ezahlukene. Lokhu abezombusazwe bakwenza ukuze baphikise imibono yabo esuke ingenayo ingqikithi noma isisekelo. 
   Kulokhu kuhlelwa kolimi kwaba khona uhlelo lokuhlaziya ulimi olwalubizwa nge-uJamoo. Sithola ukuthi leli lizwe liphinde labalulwa njengezwe lase-Mtika eli be nobunyoninco ukuba lingasebenzisi ulimi lwezwe elabe lilithumbile emva kokuthi selithole uzimelegeqe. Umengameli wokuqala waseTanzania uJilius Nyerere nguye owaba ngungqondongqondo ngokuthi athi lapho esegcotshwa ngokusemthethweni njengomengameli enze izifungo zakhe ngolimi l),VesiSwahili. lwabo kuzo zonke izimo zempilo kubantu. Lokhu kungumlando kanti futhi ukusatshalaliswa kolimi IwesiSwahili kwabe kungesiyo into ekhulumeka kalula futhi sithola ukuthi kwabe kungulimi olwabe lungaqondile 
kahle. Umbono owaphakanyiswa yilowo wokuba kulandelwe umgudu owawulandelwa yizingqalabutho kwezombusazwe ezifana noNkwame Nkrumah. Uhla lwemigomo yabo lwalubandakanya ukukhushulwa kwabantu mayelana nesimo senhlalo njengekusasa kanye nomlando wesiko le-Mrika. Uhla lwabo lwavumelana nenqubo yokuthuthukisa bonke abantu. Kulo mkhankaso wabo babelwela ukulingana phakathi kwezakhamuzi ze-Mrika. Leli qembu labe lisebenza ukuba liqinisekise ukuthi ulimi lusetshenziswe ngendlela eyamukelekile nesezingeni eliphezulu. 
   Kwaba khona olunye uhlangothi olwabe lukholelwa ekutheni kufanele kwenziwe izinguquko. Emva kokuba iZanzibar kanye neTanganyika 
bethole uzimelegeqe kwaba khona ubumbano nezinguquko zangonyaka we-1964. Ukuvukelwa kombuso kwangonyaka we-!.964 yiko okwabeka uhlangothi oluphikisayo ezinranjeni zombuso. ionke. Babekholelwa ukuthi ulimi lwesiSwahili lukhombisa ubuzwe bokuba ngum-Afrika phakami kwezizwe, lukhomba ubunye nobumbano kany~ nokulingana phakathi kwezakhamuzi. Babefuna ukuthi isiSwahili sisetshenziswe ukumola ulwazi bese kuthi ulimi IwesiN gisi lusetshenziswe ezizindeni zemfundo ephakeme kodwa isiN gisi sibe ulimi Iwesibili hhayi ukumi kube yiso esisetshenziswa njengolimi olwancelwa ebeleni. Lokhu kwabe kubuyisela isimo sezomnotho kanye nezombusazwe uma kungaphandle kwamanye amazwe. 
  Iqembu lesibili lona lalifuna ukuba ulimi lwesiSwahili lusetshenziswe njengokhiye kuzo zonke izindawo. Lokhu babekwenzela ukumi kubumbane isizwe sibe munye. Babefuna ukuba sisetshenziswe njengesikQJ~izwe. Lakhu babememba ukuthi kuzoletha inguquko emasikweni. Bona olwabo uhlelo lwabe kungelona lobulimimbili kodwa babefuna ukumi isiSwahili kube yiso kuphela ezweni laseTanzania esizoba ulimi olusemthethweni. Lakhu kwabe kusabandakanya ukusetshenziswa kwaso emfundweni ephakeme. Babefuna ukuba isiNgisi sisetshenziswe njengolimi Iwangaphandle olubalulekile 
hhayi ukuthi kube ngolwesibili. Nokuthi futhi ukufundiswa kwesiNgisi kungabukelwa phansi bese kuyalahlwa. Kuzona zombili izinhlangothi imibono yabo babevumelana ngokumi kufanele kuncikwe nakwezinye izilimi zangaphakami. Lokhu kwasekelwa nayisikhungo sezemfundo esiphakeme sase Dar es Salaam. Esimeni semfundo esemazingeni aphansi kwabe kungumdonsiswano phakami kwesiSwahili silwa nesiN gisi njengolimi lokuxhumana. 
  Esimeni somnotho nezombusazwe kanye nokuhlelwa kolimi, sithola ukuthi kwaba khona ukuphikisana phakathi kwamaqembu amabili okuchaza ngokusobala ngesimo sokuhambisana kwezlvumelwano kanye nokuguquka kulokho obekushiwo ngaphambili mayelana nokuhlelwa kolimi eTanzania. Womabili lama qembu avumelana ngokungabhaliwe phansi futhi okungacacile ukumi isiSwahili kanye nokuhlelwa kwezinye izilimi kumele kwenziwe ngendlela ezokwazi ukutholakala kuzo zonke izakhamuzi. Imithombo yolwazi kumele abantu bakwazi ukufinyelela kuyo. Lokhu kwaholela ocwaningweni olunzulu mayelana nendlela yokufundiswa kwesiSwahili. Yize noma kunjalo kwabonakala ukuthi abavumelani ngokuyingqalasizinda senjongo yabo yokuthi ngabe kumele yini ukumi iTanzania ibe yizwe elisebenzisa isiSwahili sodwa noma ibe yizwe elibulimimbili isebenzise isiSwahili kanye nesiNgisi noma ibe yizwe

wenze icala uma ushebanisile. UMnyango Wezemfundo kwakufanele wengamele imizamo eyenziwa ukurhuthukisa ukufundiswa kwesiSwahili kanjalo nokubhalwa kwezinsiza kufundisa. Abafundisi babambe iqhaza elikhulu ekwakhiweni kohlelo olusha lokufundisa. Amagama amasha esiSwahili kwadingeka ukurhi asarshalaliswe ngokushesha. UMnyango Wezemfundo wazinikela ekurheni usebenzisane noMnyango Wezokuhlolwa kwabafundi ukuze kube noshinrsho emaphepheni ashicilelwayo. Lezi zikhungo ziyahalaliselwa kanri ziyacelwa ukuba zishicilele imibhalo yazo ngesiSwahili ukuze isershenziswe ezikoleni.
