UKUHLELWA KOLIMI ENAMIBIA 
INamibia yarhola uzimele geqe ngoNdasa onyakeni we-1990. 
INamibia inezigaba zezilimi zomdabu eziyi-18 kanye nezinye ezinrarhu zesijalimane. Yileso naleso sigaba solimi sinezilimi zezigodi zakhona. 
lzilimi eziyisishiyagalolunye zalezo zomdabu ziyasershenziswa emfundweni (Zimmermann 1984: 27). Kutharhwa kalula nje ukuthi yilezi zilimi ezikhulunywayo furhi ezaziwayo kodwa akwanele ukurhi zingenziwa 
izilimi zesizwe noma izilimi ezisemrhethweni. Ngaphambi kwenkululeko iNamibia yayinezilimi ezimbili ezisemrherhweni. IsiBhunu nesiNgisi 
kodwa isiJalimane naso sasisershenziswa ezingeni eliphakarhi nendawo. IsiNgisi sasingasetshenziswa njalo. Ngesikharhi iNamibia irhola inkululeko kwaba khona imibuzo yokuthi baqhubeke yini nezilimi ezazisemrherhweni njengoba kwakuyizilimi zokufika zabelumbi. INamibia yazirhola isezinkingeni ezinkulu ezifana nalezo ezibhekene namanye amazwe amaningi anezilimi ezahlukene njengalezi: 
* Ukuqokwa kwezilimi ezisemrherhweni 
* Ukwakhiwa kwesizwe esibumbene esinezinhlanga 
* Ukwakhiwa nokuthurhukisa amarhuba alinganayo abo bonke 




24. 
   Ulimi olusemthethweni ulimi oluthathwa ngokomthetho njengolimi lukahulumeni ulimi lwemfundo. INamibia yayifuna ukuthi ibe izwe elizoba nolimi olulodwa kodwa oluvumela izilimi zendawo zibe khona eduz~ kwalo njengase Soviet Union. Uma izwe liqoka ukukhetha ulimi olulodwa lube semthethweni, lokho kusuke kunikeza abahleli bolimi amathuba amathathu: 
* Ukuqoka ulimi lwabelumbi njengolimi olusemthethweni. 
* Ukuqoka ulimi lomdabu njengolimi olusemthethweni 
* Inhlanganisela yezilimi ezimbili kanye nolimi lokuxhumana bese kuba khona ulimi lomdabu lwase-Mrika olusemthethweni. 
   UFasold (1984: 4-5) uthi yena ezweni elinezilimi eziningi indlela elula yokukhetha ulimi lukahulumeni olusha yileyo yokuqoka ulimi lwabelumbi obeluvele lukhona, ufukazelwa nguWardhaugh (1987: 163) kalo-mqondo. 
Lena yindlela esetshenziswe amazwe amaningi ase-Attika njengalawa: INigeria, iGhana, iKenya, i-Uganda, iSenegal, iZaire, iGabon, i-Ivory Coast kanye neZimbabwe. Iningi lalawa mazwe alenzanga kahle kulezi zinqubomgomo zawo. Isizathu abasibekayo ngesokuthi imibhalo eminingi kahulumeni kanye nezikhungo zakhona kungolimi 1010 obelusemthethweni. Kuyaye kube isinqumo esinzima kona ukusithatha. Isinqumo esinye ababengasithatha yileso sokuqoka ulimi lomdabu lube ngulimi olusemthethweni, oluzoba nalobu buhle: 
* Izilimi zomdabu zisetshenziswa kakhulu; 
* Kulula ukulwazi ulimi ngaleyo ndlela kwenza ukuthi lusabalale kalula, ukuxhumana phakathi kukahulumeni nabantu kuba lula; 
* Imfundo kungaba ngeyawo wonke umuntu; 
* Ungavumela abantu abaningi bakwazi~kuthi babambe iqhaza enkululekweni yezwe futhi kungavaleb lsikhala phakathi kwabampofu nabadla izambane kilapondo. 
   Okuyinkinga lapha ukuthi kungaba khona abantu abangavaleleka ngenxa yokungalwazi ulimi olusethethweni. 
Imithetho Yolimi eyake yaba khona eNamibia 
  Ngonyaka we-1884 kuya kowe-1918 iGerman yaba ulimi olusemthethweni, nanamuhla kunabantu abasakhuluma iGerman. N gonyaka we-1976 kwakhiwa i United Natiom Institute fOr Namibia (UN IN) yiyona eyabamba iqhaza elikhulu ekwalthiweni komthetho  ";l,,n'1 "limi 
Isimo sabantu baseNamibia ngesiBhunu 
   Isimo sabantu baseNamibia ngolimi IwesiBhunu besixega kusukela ekutheni singemukeleki ngaphansi kombuso wamaJalimane, kodwa ngokuhamba kwesikhathi samukeleka. Ubandlululo eNamibia Iwaphela ngonyaka we-1979. Ukuphoqelelwa kolimi IwesiBhunu eNingizimu 
Mrika kwenza ukuthi iNamibia ingabe isazixaka ngokuqoka isiBhunu njengolimi olusemthethweni, ezweni elikhululekile. Abahlali baseNamibia abaluthandanga ulimi lwesiBhunu ngoba Iwabenza baba ngabafokazana ezweni labo, ngendlela yokuthi kwaba yilo ulimi IwesiBhunu olwavimbela ukuba babe yizakhamizi ezweni labo. Udlame Iwangonyaka we-1976 eNingizimu Mrika olwenzeka eSoweto lapho abafundi abansundu benqaba ukufunda ngesiBhunu lwaba nomthelela omkhulu kalthulu esinyathelweni solimi eNamibia. Ukusukela ngawo 10 nyaka abantu baseNamibia babesibalekela isiBhunu. Lokhu kwaqala eNyakatho kwaya kwaze kwafika kwezinye izindawo eNamibia. ISWAPO yayithatha isiBhunu njengolimi lwengcindezelo kanti isiNgisi son:;: njengolimi lwenkululeko. Abazali abaningi baeela ukuthi izingane zabo zifundiswe ngesiN gisi. N gonyaka we-1981 isiNgisi saba ulimi lokufundisa e-Ovambo. Ngonyaka we- 
1988 iNyuvesi yaseNamibia yashintshela olimini lwesiNgisi njengolimi lokufundisa. Ngonyaka we-1980 kwadingeka ukuthi kutholakale ulimi olunye olwaluzoba semthethweni. Kwahlanganwa eLusaka ngamhla ziyisi5-8 kuMeyi ngonyaka we-1980 kudingidwa udaba IweNgisi njengolimi olusemthethweni. Umphumela walo mhlangano kwaba umqulu orhi: 
"Towards a language policy fOr Namibia" lapho inqubomgomo yolimi ivezwe khona ngokujulile. Inqubomgomo yabo yolimi ngeyokuhlanganisa bonke abantu baseNamibia ngale kwebala. Lapha kwalthethwa ulimi lwesiNgisi njengolimi lobumbano. INamibia yayizimisele ukuthuthukisa izilimi zomdabu ukuze inqubomgomo yabo yolimi kube ngeyobuliminingi 
njengoba sibona ezweni laseNingizimu Mrika. 	'. 
'., 
I-United Natiom Imtitute fOr Namibia (UNIN) (1981: 37-38) 
yaqhamuka nemigomo eyisishiyagalombili okufanele ibe khona olimini oluthathwa njengolusemthethweni: Ubumbano, ukwamukeleka, 
ukwaziwa, ukusebenza, isayensi nobuehwepheshe, iPan Aficanism, ulimi lokuxhumana nokuba ulimi Iwamazwe omhlaba. Emigomweni eyayibekiwe, isiN gisi asihlangabezani nemigomo emibili, wokwaziwa nowokuba ulimi olusetshenziswa ngabantu. Abantu abaningi base Namibia babengalwazi ulimi lwesiN gisi, kanti ukuqaliswa kwalo kwakuzodala izinkinga eziningi .  


Ubumbano 
   Kuyinkinga ukuthi ulimi olufana nesiNgisi eNamibia lwalungenza ukuthi abantu baziqhenye ngobuzwe babo. Inkinga ngomthetho of ana nalona seyibonakele emazweni amaningi, bancane abantu abayaye bazi isiNgisi ngendlela efanele futhi bakwazi ukuxhumana ngaso. Kuyaziwa ukuthi ulimi olusemthethweni alusabalele kahle emazweni amaningi aseMrika, ngaleyo ndlela kwakungeke kuze kube lula nakhona eNamibia. Akwaziwa noma ulimi IwesiNgisi luzokwazi yini ukuhlanganisa 
abantu baseNamibia. Isizathu sokufuna ukwenza isiNgisi sibe ulimi olusemthethweni yingoba isiNgisi ulimi lokuxhumana. IsiNgisi ulimi lomhlaba wonke kanti eNamibia lukhulunywa ngabantu abayi-50/0 kuphela. Ulimi IwesiNgisi luhle ngoba ulimi lokuxhumana lwamazw<; .. ngamazwe noluzokwenza abantu baseNamibia bath ole ulwazi lomhlaba futhi bakwazi ukubamba iqhaza ezindabeni zomhlaba ngaphandle kokusebenzisa abuhumushi. IsiNgisi eNamibia sibonakala siwulimi lwemfundo, 
kanjalo nololwazi. IsiNgisi sabonakala njengolimi olwaluzohlanganisa abantu baseNamibia. Inkinga engadalwa ukuqoka isiNgisi njengolimi olusemthethweni ukuthi nje okokuqala isiNgisi ulimi lokufika kubantu abaningi baseNamibia. Akufani naseKenya noma e-Uganda lapho isiNgisi kuwulimi olusemthethweni futhi ulimi lwenkululeko, ulimi lwezokuphatha nolwemfundo. Obunye ububi ukuthi kukhethwe lona lodwa. Yize noma isiNgisi sisemthethweni kodwa bayavuma ukuthi ulimi lokuqala lomdabu nalo lusebenze. Okunye okungaba yinkinga ukungasabalali kahle kolimi olusemthethweni. IsiNgisi eNamibia asinabo abakhulumi abangabanikazi bolimi okuyibona abazogqugquzela ukusetshenziswa kolimi IwesiNgisi.

IsiNgisi Kwezemjimdo 
   Izinqinamba abahlangabezana nazo kwezemfundo emva kokuqoka isiNgisi njengolimi olusemthethweni zibandakanya ukuqeqeshwa kothisha olimini IwesiN gisi. Ukuthengwa kwezincwadi zesiN gisi ngaphandle. Kunemibuzo emihlanu ebalulekile engaba luhlaka ekuhlelweni kolimi kwezemfundo (Rubin (I 971: 22): 
1.) Yikuliphi ibanga lapho ulimi lwasekhaya kufanele ulusebenzise 
khona?; 
2.) Yinini lapho ulimi IweSizwe kufanele lube ulimi lokufunda?; 
3.) Kungabe othisha banawo yini amakhono okufundisa ngesiNgisi?; 4.) Kungabe izincwadi zikhona yini ngolimi olusemthethweni?; 


UKUHLELWA KOLIMI EMALAWI 
   IMalawi ngelinye lamazwe aseMzansi ne-Mrika. Inhlokodolobha yeMalawi iLilongwe. Abantu bokuqala abahlala eMalawi amaThonga namaTumbuka (Davel, Engelbrecht no Rautenbach, 1987: 39). AmaTumbuka asabalala nezwe laseMalawi evela eFuba naseCongo, abe eseqala umbuso wamaMaravi, yilapho igama lezwe iMalawi lisuselwa 
khona. AmaMaravi umbuso owawuphethwe ngamaNyanja, amaChewa namaTsonga. Ulimi olusemthethweni eMalawi isiNgisi nesiChichewa. Ezinye izilimi ezikhona eMalawi iChewa, iYao, iChimpoka, iTonga, iTumbuka neNgoni. Ukuthola kwe-Mrika inkululeko noma uzimelegeqe ngeminyaka ephakathi kowe- 1950 kuya kowe-1970 kwenza ukuthi amazwe amaningi asale enomqansa wokuWela ulimi ukuze aphume nenqubomgomo 
yolimi. 	4 
Imithetho Yolimi Eyake Yabekwa Phambilini eMalawi 
   IsiNgisi nesiFrench yizona zilimi ebezisemthethweni phambilini. Ulimi olusemthethweni IweNWangano Yezizwe isiNgisi nesiFrench. INhlangano Yezizwe yanxusa ukuthi isiNgisi nesiFrench kushintshwe izilimi ezine zase-Mrika, ukwenzela isiko lobuzwe base-Mrika. Lezo zilimi isi-Arabhu, isiSwahili, IsiZulu, iShonaf Chich ewe neHausa. 
   IMalawi ibingaphansi kwamaNgisi ngonyaka we-1891 kwaze kwafika onyakeni we-1964, kanti inezilimi eziningi. Emva kwenkululeko 
ngonyaka we- 1964 iMalawi yaba nezilimi ezintathu ezisemthethweni: isiNgisi, iNyanja neThibuka. UBanda (Kamuzu) umholi waseMalawi wakubeka kwacaca ukuthi kwakufanele kusetshenziswe ulimi olulodwa olwaluzohlabahlosa bakwazi ukurhi bathuthuke kwezomnotho, ezolimo, imfundo njll. Kwagcina kuvunyelwene ngokuthi isiNgisi nesiChichewa kube izilimi ezisemthethweni. IsiChichewa saba ulimi lwemfundo 
iminyaka emithathu yokuqala. ENyuvesi singulimi o(tikhethwayo ukuthi ulwenze aluphoqiwe. IMalawi yayaziwa ngokuthi iNyasaiand ngenkathi isaphethwe iBrithani. Kuthe ngonyaka we-1964 ziyisi-6 enyangeni kaNrulikazi yakhululeka yathola ukuzimela, yaphuma ngaphansi kombuso wamaNgisi. Yabe isiguqula igama layo seyibizwa ngokuthi iMalawi. 
Umholi wokuqala waseMalawi yentando yabanru kwaba ngumengameli uKamuzu Hastings Banda. Ngemuva kukaBanda owaye sezinike isikhundla sokuba ngumengameli impilo yakhe yonke eMalawi, kwayiwa okhethweni wehlulwa nl':UBakili Muluzi. Kwathi ngonyaka wezi-2002 uMuluzi 




okuyiZambia ngaseNtshonaianga, iTanzania ngaseNyakatho bese ihlangana neMozambique ngaseMpumaianga naseNingizimu Ntshonalanga. 
   Inhlokodolobha yaseMalawi iLilongwe, nokho-ke iLilongwe incane ngoba ibonakala iBlantyre inkulu kunayo. Kwaba lula ukuthi iLiiongwe ibe inhloko dolobha ngoba iyona ecishe ibe phakathi neMalawi, kanti iBlantyre iceze kakhulu ngoba ingaseNingizimu Ntshonalanga yeMalawi. Abantu base Malawi babalelwa ezigidini eziyishumi (l0 million) kodwa ziyakhula izibalo unyaka nonyaka ngamaphesenti amabili (2%) ngokusho kwehhovisi lokubalwa kwabantu (National Statistical Office: 1998). Cishe amaphesenti angamashumi amahlanu (50%) wabantu baseMalawi izingane ezingaphansi kweminyaka eyishumi nanhlanu. 
  Izwe laseMalawi linoHulumeni osebenzisa ubuliminingi; .futhi uHulumeni wakhona uthathwa ngokuthi uHulumeni oqhuba intando yabantu. Izwe laseMalawi linezilimi ezingaphezulu kweshumi nesithupha. Lokhu akusho ukuthi zonke lezi zilimi zisebenza ngokulingana uma kufundwa noma kufundiswa ezikoleni. Izilimi okuyizona ezikhulunywa kakhulu eMalawi futhi ezibonakala zisemqoka zimbili, isiN gisi kanye nesiChichewa. Zikhona-ke nezinye izilimi ezikhulunywayo furhi baningi abantu abazisebenzisayo. Ukuzibala nje singabalula: isiChichewa, isiChinyawo, isiLomwe, isiNkhonde, is iN goni, isiNyakyusa, isiLambya, isiSenga, isiNgisi, isiPurukezi, isiLumbuka nesiLonga. ENingizimu ne-Mrika uma ubuka izinga lemfundo uthola ukuthi iMalawi isezingeni eliphansi kakhulu ngoba amaphesenti angamashumi amahlanu nesishiyagalombili nje kuphela abanru abafundile (UNICEF: 1993). 
	Ezemfundo eMalawi 	.... ~ 
   Ngokwemfundo yamabanga aphansi, imvamisa izingane ziqala imfundo yazo zineminyaka eyisithupha. Zithatha iminyaka eyisishiyagalombili kusukela ebangeni lokuqala (std 1) kuya ebangeni lesishiyagalombili (std 8). Ekupheleni konyaka wesishiyagalombili ingane ibhala ukuhlolwa okubizwa ngokuthi iPrimary School Leaving Cirtificate Examination. Lokho kuhlolwa kuqashelwa kakhulu futhi kubhekwe uNgqongqoshe weZemfundo neMalawi National Examinarion Board (MANEB). Emfundweni yasemazingeni aphakame umfundi uthatha iminyaka emine. Umfundi uvumelekile ukuzikhethela ukuthi uzofunda emazingeni aphakeme esikole sika Hulumeni noma esangasese. Emfundweni yasemazingeni aphakame umfundi uhlolwa kabili. Okokuoala ifunior Certificate Examination 
ibihlolelwa okubizwa ngeMalawi School Certificate Examination (MSCE). Yomibili Ie mikhakha ibihlelwa i MANEB ngokuhlanganyela nehhovisi likaN gqongqoshe Wezemfundo. Kuqhubeke isikhathi kwatholakala ukuthi lapha ekuhlolweni sekunomkhonyovu. Le mikhonyovu yokuhlolwa yaze yagcina ngokuthi uHulumeni aqede ukuhlolwa kwezingane ngonyaka 
wezi- 2000. Futhi ngawo 10 nyaka kwaxoshwa oyinhloko yeMANEB ngoba esoleka ngomkhonyovu. Umfundi ubethi uma eseqedile emfundweni yasemazingeni aphakeme bese kukhethwa labo bafundi abaphase kahle ukuthi baye emaNyuvesi nasema Theknikhoni. Umfundi wayekhetha phakathi kwamakolishi okuqeqeshela amakhono, iNyuvesi yaseMalawi neNyuvesi yaseMzuzu. 
   Okudabukisayo nje eMalawi ukuthi amaNyuvesi akhona mabili nje kuphela. Ileyo ebizwa ngeNyuvesi yaseMalawi kanye naleyo okuthiwa nguMzuzu. INyuvesi yaseMalawi yavulwa ngonyaka we- I 965. Kuthe ngemuva konyaka-nje kwavulwa i~yuvesi uMzuzu. 
lnqubomgomo yolimi ezikoleni zaseMalawi 
   Sengizobheka inqubomgomo yolimi ezikoleni zaseMalawi. Ngiphinde futhi ngibheke ukuthi Ie nqubomgomo babeyenza kanjani ukuthi isebenze. Bese ngibheka ukuthi ikuphi abakuzuza nalokho okungahambanga kahle ngale nqubomgomo yabo. Ukubona ukuthi iyasebenza inqubomgomo ababezimisele ngayo, babe sebekhetha izikole ezithile ukuze bacwaninge ngazo. 
  Lolu cwaningo engizokhuluma ngalo Iwenziwa ngonyaka we-1999 ezikoleni ezingamashumi ayisithupha nanhlanu (65) ezindaweni ezimbili, iMangochi kanye neBaiaka okuyizindawo eziseNingizimu yeMalawi. Le nqubo uma uyibuka ngeso eliphindela emumva kuHulumeni wengcindezelo wamaBrithani uyayibona. ArnaBrithani ayeqikelela u~uthi ingane uma isaqala isikole ifunde ngolimi Iwayo iminyaka emine ingenile esikoleni.

UKUHLELWA KOLIMI EZIMBABWE 
   IZimbabwe izwe laseNingizimu ne-Afrika, uMengimeli wakhona uRobert Mugabe kanti inhlokodolobha yakhona iHarare. Izilimi ti.khona ezisemthethweni isiShona, isiNdebele kanye nesiNgisi. IZimbabwe ithole uzimele geqe ngonyaka we-I 980. Abelumbi beZimbabwe iBrithani. URobert Mugabe uyena owaba umengameli waseZimbabwe kusukela ngonyaka we- 1980. Kanti Inkolo eyabe kuyiyona eyabe ihamba phambili eZimbabwe kwabe kungeyamaRoma. Ziyisishiyagalombili izifundazwe zaseZimbabwe kanye namadolobh'!!<azi akhona amabili. UBulawayo, eHarare, kuzophawulwa ngawo ngaphansi kwenqubomgomo yolimi ezweni laseZimbabwe. Ukuhlelwa kolimi uma kwenziwa ucwaningo kuncike ekusetshenzisweni kwezilimi ezahlukene kanye nenhlalo emphakathini. Ulimi olusemthethweni ngokomthetho ulimi oluthathwa njengolimi lukaHulumeni njengolimi lwemfundo. 
   Umphakathi waseZimbabwe uhlukaniseke izizwana ezimbili. AmaShona kanye namaNdebele. AmaShona nawo ahlukaniseke kanje kukhona angamaTavara, amaKorekore naManyika, labo ngokwesiko babekwa ngokuthi inkolo yabo kanye nezigodi zabo amaShona. Kahle kahle wona amaShona isona sizwe esiningi ngoba sithatha ingxenye engamashumi ayisikhombisa nanye kumaphesenti 71 % bese kuthi amaNdebele athathe ingxenye yamaphesenti ayishumi nesithupha (16%) yomphakathi, bona bakhuluma u1imi oluzwakala njengesiZulu. Bese kuba yilaba abanye ababuya emazweni akhelene neZimbabwe njengeMozambique. IsiNgisi eZimbabwe sithathwa njengolimi olusemthethweni futhi olusetshenziswa uhulumeni nanjengolimi lwemfundo. Abanye noma idlanzana lezakhamizi zakhona eZimbabwe ezingabantu abamhlophe, amaBhunu, akhuluma isiBhunu. Izwe laseZimbabwe linabantu abalinganiselwa ezigidini eziyishumi nantathu, okuyinhlanganisela yabantu base-Afrika nabantu baseYurophu. Kukhona nezingxenyana zabantu ababuya e-Asia. Ngaleyo ndlela izwe laseZimbabwe izwe eliliminingi futhi elinamasiko amaningi. Kunezilimi ezintathu ezithathwa njengezilimi ezibalulekile eZimbabwe. 




isiHwesa, isiShangani, isiBarne, isiSurhu, isiVenda, isiChiiokunda, isiXhosa, isiTshwano, nesiTswana. 
   UChiwome benoThondhlana (1990) uthi iZimbabwe njengamazwe amaningi ase-Mrika yakhetha ukusebenzisa ulimi IwesiNgisi njengolimi olusemthethweni okwabe kuwulimi Iwencindezelo. Ilona limi oluthathwa njengolimi lokuhweba, izindaba, olusetshenziswa ezimbonini kanye nakwezemfundo. IsiNdebele kanye nesiShona noma ngabe sibalulekile kodwa sisithola kuphela sivumeleka ukurhi sisebenze njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa ezikoleni kuphela emazingeni emfundo aphansi bese kuthi lapho umntwana esenyukele emazingeni athe ukuphakama lapho-ke sekudingeka ukurhi afunde ngolimi IwesiNgisi. 
Ukuhle!4 ukufunda nokwamukelwa kolimi 
   Laba abanye bomphakathi waseZimbabwe ngaphandle kwalezi zilimi ezintathu kuyabakhalisa ukurhi izilimi zabo zithathwe njengezilimi ezingekho ekubeni abanikazi bazo beyingxenye yomphakathi. Bathi ulimi Iwabo luyingxenye yempilo yabo, kodwa nokho selibonakala luya ngokuya lufa ngenxa yokurhi uhulumeni engaziniki zonke izilimi amathuba okuthi zingasetshenziswa. Eminyangweni kahulumeni kubonakala kuyilezi zilimi ezintamu kuphela ezisetshenziswayo. Imibhalo kahulumeni, nokusakwazwa komabonisakude eZimbabwe kusetshenziswa isiN gisi, isiShona kanye nesiNdebele. Ephepheni lango May 17,2004 elibizwa nge The Herald lapho kwakhalaza abanikazi bezilimi ezincane ngokuthi babona sengathi uhulumeni ukhombisa ukuthuthukisa izilimi ezintathu kuphela ezinye ezincane zikhishwa inyumbazane bese kuvikwa ngenkinga yokushoda kwezimali.    Iminyakazo seyikhona yokumi inqubomgomo yolomi kwezemfundo yenze isiqiniseko sokuthi zisetshenziswe zonke izilimi. UN gqongqoshe Wezemfundo wakhipha izimali zokuthi kukhishwe izincwadi zalezi zilimi futhi kuphindwe kurhengwe nomshini ozosiza ukurhi kugaywe izincwadi. Umfutho weZimbabwe noma ngabe ubonakala umncane kodwa bakurholile ukutuswa uma kukhulunywa ngezilimi. Izazi zolimi zithi ukusetshenziswa kolimi nsuku zonke yiyona ndlela eqinisekisa ukuthi.)uyaqhubeka 
lukhule. Emhlabeni wonke jikelele, izilimi ezincane ziyasatshiswa nsuku zonke ngezinkulu nokuyizona ezivelele namasiko azo. Osolwazi bezilimi balinganisela ukurhi ekupheleni kweminyaka eyikhulu, amaphesenti angamashumi amahlanu 50% ezilimi zomhlaba zizonyamalala noma zizophela. E-Austtalia uLo Bianco (2003) uthi izilimi zakhona zomphakathi ezmgamaphesenti angama-95 azisafundwa abantwana ezikoleni nenani labakhulumi bazo liya ngokuya liyancipha.

Le nhlangano ngonyaka we-1999 yabe isaqhubeka ukuhlanganisa amaNyuvesi aseZimbabwe ebandakanya neGotebong ngenhloso yokuthi bakhiphe ikhophasi yobulimimbili ngokubhekela izichazimagama =ilimi zaseZimbabwe. Lapha babebhekele ukuthuthukiswa kwezichazimagama, ukuqanjwa kwamatemu ezilimi ezahlukene zakhona eZimbabwe. Nokho okwamanje inqubekela phambili esabonakele ukwakheka kwesichazimagama esilimilunye solimi IwesiShona, esibizwa ngokuthi i-Duramazwi Rechishona. Lesi sichazimagama sakhishwa ngonyaka we-1996.    Le nhlangano ye-ALLEX ungayifanisa neBhodi Yezilimi Zonke ZaseNingizimu Mrika (PanSALB). Ukuba khona kwe-PanSALB eNingizimu Mrika kuwukurhi ibhekele ukurhurhukiswa kwezilimi zabomdabu ebezicindezelwe phambilini nokuvikela amalungelo ezilimi zabomdabu. 
Ukuhlelwa kwekhophasi 
   Ulimi IwesiShona lwaphinda lwathola amandla emiphakathini yaseZimbabwe. IsiShona sesibe yilona limi lokuxhumana eZimbabwe. Ikakhulukazi ezindaweni zikahulumeni kwezomburho, ezikoleni, emaphoyiseni nakuzona zonke ezinye izikhungo zikaHulumeni. 
Inhlangano ebizwa ngokurhi i-National ZTV yenze umsebenzi omkhulu ekurhurhukiseni ulimi IwesiShona eZimbabwe. Phela iZimbabwe isizwe samaShona. Okunye okufanele sikukhumbule ukurhi inturhuko enjenga 
Ie yokudlondlobala kolimi isho ukuvuleka kwamathuba emisebenzi, kusekhona nesidingo sokurhi kusatshalaliswe ulimi. Ngokusabalalisa ulimi kungaba ukurhi kufanele kuhunyushwe izincwadi, nanoma yiziphi ezinye izinto ezibhalwe ph ansi ngolimi lwabacindezeli. Lapho-ke kudingeka abantu abazoqashwa ukwenza lowo msebenzi. Manje abaIltu abakhuluma isiShona sebegcwele wonke amakhona ezwe laseZimbabwe. Ngisho abanrwana abangamaNdebele sebeqala ukubona ukurhi ukwe~za- sengathi ababoni ukurhi isiShona sidla lubi sebeyaqala manje ukubona ukurhi akuzukubasiza lokho. Lokhu kudala ukurhi kancane kancane isiShona siyemukelwa njengolimi lokuxhumana. Awusemkhulu umsebenzi owenziwa abantu abangamaNdebele ngaphandle kokuhumusha, bahlole amaphephamvume kanye namaphephandaba. Amashumi ayisishiyagalolunye nanhlanu yamaphesenti (95%) yemisebenzi kahulumeni ezweni laseMatebeleni ikhulu lamaphesenti (100%) wesizwe sonke ukhuluma isiShona. Izinkampani ezinkulu zokusebenza sezinikezelwe ezandleni zamaShona. Lokhu kubavulela amathuba emisebenzi engcono. Amakolishi orhisha, amaNyuvesi, nazo zonke lezi zikhungo zemfundo ephakeme zenganyelwe amaShona 

Uma kuwukuthi kuvela izikhala wkufundisa wthisha akungatshazw.a ukurhi leso sikhala siwthathwa ngumShona, phela basuke beqeqeshl'~ve. Ngisho ezindaweni \apho kukhome\wa khona sengisho emas~ntwem, 
\0 moya uyafakwa wokurhi uma kushunyaye\wa noma kwemlwa noma yini esontweni u\imi okufande \usetshemiswe \apho isiShona. Nanoma kusabonakala sengathi kukhona abaBhishobhi bona ubiw \wabo enkosini bagcotshwa ngesiNdebele kodwa masinyane bazongena ngaphansi kwaso isiShona. 
Inkinga yezilimi 
   Ulimi yiyona ndlela ewuphawu lomphakathi ukurhi uxhumane, nokukwazi ukukhuluma ngento ofuna ukuyisho. Lokho kwenza isizwe siqhakaze, ngamasiko kanye nezinkolelo zaso futhi isizwe sikwazi ukugcina izimfihlo zaso. Umthetho wokuhlanganisa umhlaba ngokurhi kukhuliswe lezi zilimi ezinjengesiNgisi, isiFrentshi, isiPutukezi, isiPenishi kanye 
nezinye izilimi zase Yuropu endaweni yezilimi zomdabu, kudale ukurhi izilimi zomdabu zilahlekelwe amagugu nezimfihlo zobuzwe bazo. Lezi 
zilimi zokufika ngempela zintsha e-Mrika njengoba ziyizilimi zokugqilaza okuyinto esidlulelwe yisikhathi. Lezi zilimi bezisetshenziswa uma kuxhunyanwa ngezomnorho, futhi abantu abebezisebenzisa bengaphansi kwamaphesenti angamashumi amabili abanru bezilimi zomdabu. Kunamazwe amaningi ase-Mrika abuliminingi futhi anezilimi ezincane eziningi kufakwa nezilimi zezigodi. Izwe laseDemocratic Republic o/Congo (DRC) linezilimi ezingaphezu kwamakhulu amabili, elase Tanzaniya linezilimi eziyikhulu namashumi amabili, i-Angola inamashumi ayisithupha ezilimi, iMozambique inezilimi ezingamashumi amabili nanhlanu, ekubeni iBotswana neZimbabwe banezilimi ezibalelwa emashumini amabili 
isizwe ngasinye. Kunjalo amazwe aseNingizimu ne-Mrika awakayibeki inqubomgomo yokuthi ivikele futhi ithurhukise izilimi ezincane. 
   INingizimu Mrika ngelinye lamazwe elathatha inqubomgomo yobuliminingi ngonyaka we-l 996. IZimbabwe yona yenza inqubomgomo yolimi kwezemfundo yokurhi iminyaka emithathu yokuqala kwezemfundo ingane kufanele isebenzise ulimi lwayo lomdabu njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa. Ngaleso sikhathi kube kwethulwa isiNgisi. Izilimi eziyisikhombisa eZimbabwe ezisetshenziswayo kule minyaka emithathu isiShona, isiN debele, isiKalanga, isiThonga, isiVenda, isiShangane kanye neNambya, bayakujabulela lokhu kuhlelwa. 
Ububi obuvela ngaleli lizwe indlela yokukhethwa kukahulumeni. Lapha

Uma kuziwa ngasemnothweni e-Algeri~;lnzuzo kuleliya 
zwe itholakala kakhulu ngokudayiswa kwe-hydrocarbon, kanti abalingani abaqavile lelizwe elihwebelana nabo yi-France, yiNtaliyane kanye neMelika. Ezimpahleni eziyiswa kwamanye amazwe i-Algeria yethembele kakhulu ezweni laseFrance (20%), ilandelwe yi-Melika (ngo-9.80/0) 
kanye neNtaliyane (ngo-9.6%). Kodwa-ke, impahla abahwebelana ngayo nesimamisa umnotho wase-Algeria yi-hydro-carbon, kanti ngonyaka wezi2003 ingxenye yesamba sobugugu bezimpahla eziphumela ngaphandle kuleliya lizwe ingamaphesenti asukela ema-95 kuya ema-97 (Kuthathwe ku-Algeria Interface, 2004; CIA, World Fact Book, 2005; Martin, 2003: 39, icashunwe ku-Benrabah, 2005: 388). 
baMaFulentshi, ukugxambukela enqubeni yokuphatha eyandulela isikhathi sokulunjwa ngokusebenzisa amakhosi ama-Musilemu. US tone (1997) uphakamisa ukuthi ngaphandle kwezinsalela zemiphakathi yamaKrestu kanye namaJuda e-Algiers namanye amadolobhakazi, cishe bonke abantu base-Algeria bangama-Musilemu. Emva kwenkululeko, i-Islam njengenkolo yabamba iqhaza elibonakalayo emizamweni yokuthuthukisa inqubomgomo yolimi eyayibizwa phecelezi ngokuthi yi-Arabisation. Lokhu kwenzeka ikakhulukazi ngesikhathi sokubusa komengameli abanjengo-Ahmed 
Ben Bella, u- Houari Boumedienne kanye noChadli Bendjedid. Abantu bokudabuka e-Algeria bafunda isi-Arabhu ngencwadi engcwele yesi-Islam ebizwa nge-Koran. U-Gellner (1973), ecashunwe ngu-Benrabah (2005: 392) ubeka uvo lokuthi kusukela ekuqaleni yile ndlela eyenza ukuthi isi-Arabhu sithathwe njengolimi olusonpelene kakhulu ne-Islam eNyakatho ne-Afrika. 
   UWebb (2002) ubheka izigaba ezintathu eziqikekelwayo uma kuhlelwa ulimi njengezingxenye zokuthuthukiswa kolimi, okungukuhlela izinga lolimi (Status planning), ukuhlela ikho.phasi (Corpus planning) kanye nokufunda nokwamukela kolimi (Acquisition planning). Uma kubhekwa ukufunda nokwamukela ulimi, u Webb ubeka ukuthi lesi sigaba sokuthuthukiswa kolimi siphathelene nokufundwa kolimi njengolimi lokuqala (Ll), kanye nokufundwa kolimi njengolimi lwesibili (L2) noma ulimi lwangaphandle (2002: 277). E-Algeria isi-Arabhu safundwa njengolimi lokuqala, kwathi isi-Fulentshi safundwa njengolimi lwesibili (L2) noma ulimi lwangaphandle. Uma-ke ngizobuyela enkolweni, e-Algeria nase-Afrika jikelele inkolo yabamba iqhaza elikhulu ekufundweni kwezilimi zangaphandle. E-Afrika, inkolo seyibe yingxenye enkulu yokufundwa kolimi. Kusukela ezikoleni zamaMishinari, kuya ekuhunyushweni kwamabhayibheli, ulimi lokudumisa, umkhuleko njalo njalo, ulimi nenkolo sekube yinto engahlukaniseki uma kubhekwa ukufundwa kolimi. I-Islam yaba nomthelela omkhulu emazweni aseNyakatho ne-Aftika, isibonelo i-Algeria, yi-Liby.a kanye ne-Egypt. UNkrumah (1964: 22), ecashunwe ku-Mazrui (2004: 105), ubeka kanje ngobuhlobo phakathi kwe-Afrika nenkolo: 
   Ngenxa yenkululeko, uzwano kumele lukhuthazwe, uzwano oluzovumela ubukhona obubumbene bomdabu base-Afrika, i-Afrika ye-Islam kanye ne-Afrika yobuKrestu base- Yurophu, ukuze lobu bukhona buhambisane nezinqubo eziyizo zobuntu ezisibekele imiphakathi yase-Afrika. 
   Emva kwenkululeko e-Algeria, isibalo sabantu abafundile sakhula kangangokuthi ngisho ezindaweni zasemakhaya abantu bathola

esimeme kanye nezimo zempilo ezisezingeni eligculisayo. Yingakho uStone (1997: 2), ebalula ukurhi kusukela ekubeni yichweba elinewoza woza kubeLumbi ngonyaka we-1962, i-Algiers isithurhuke yaze yaba yidolobhakazi eselinwebeke laba nesiminyaminya ngendlela exakile. Ukulunjwa ngamaFulentshi kwashiya i-Algeria inabantu abangafundile, ngaphezu kwalokho izilimi zabo zenziwa zaba ezokukhulunywa kuphela. Umphakarhi wase-Algeria wendabuko wagcwalisa izindawo ezigudle 
ugu ukuze uhwebelane kalula nozakwabo baseYurophu, ikakhulukazi i-France. NgokukaBenrabah (2005: 394), ngesikhathi senkululeko kwakunabantu base-Algeria abayizigidi eziyishumi, kanti ikota yabo yayihlala emadolobheni. Ikota yabantu ababehlala emadolobheni kwakungumphakathi wama-Fulentshi ongafundile, owasabal.alisa isiFuientshi ngokushesha. Ingxenye eningi yabantu, ikakhuluka~i amaBhabha, ama Vandali, amaBhazantani angamaRoma (Romanised Byzantines), kanye nama-Arabhu ayengafundile ngenxa yokuswelakala kwethuba lokuya esikoleni. UBenrabah (2005: 394) uphonsa itshe esivivaneni ngovo lwakhe lokuthi e-Algeria izinga lokungafundi lahamba laze lafinyelela kumaphesenti angama-90, nokwakuyilapho amaphesenti ayi-5 nje kuphela abantu ababefundile, futhi nakhona befunde kuphela i-Literary Arabic (abantu abalinganiselwa emakhulwini angama-300). 
   Ngesikhathi i-Algeria ithola inkululeko ngamhla zi-5 kuNtulikazi ngonyaka we-1962, emva kweminyaka eyikhulu namashumi amathathti nambili ngaphansi kokulunjwa yiFrance, ubuholi base-Algeria baqalisa ukusebenzisa izinqubomgomo ezinqala, ikakhulukazi uma kuziwa olimini kanye nokuzazi kwabanru ngobuzwe babo. Ngaph:,mbi kokuzimela i-Algeria yayilunjwe ngamaFulentshi, ngakho isiFulentshi sodwa saphoqelelwa njengolimi olusemrherhweni kwezemfundo, ephalamende, kwezomnorho, kwezobuchwepheshe kanye nasemithonjeni edlulisa izindaba. Kodwa-ke kusukela esigabeni sonyaka we-I 962 kuya onyakeni we-I 970, i-Algeria yasungula inqubomgomo yobulimimbili lapho isi-Arabhu esijwayelekile noma esifundwayo (Standard/Literary Arabic) sajoyinwa yisi-Fulentshi njengolimi olusemrherhweni, yize noma makharhaleni isi-Arabhu sodwa saba wulimi olusemrhethweni. Lolu shintsho olunobuhlakani lwaba yimpumelelo ngenxa yemizamo eyenziwa ngu-Ahmed Ben Bella, owaba ngumengameli wokuqala wase-Algeria emva kwenkululeko, lwabe seluqhutshwa nguHouari Boumedienne, uChadli Bendjedid, uZeroual

Kusukela ngonyaka we-1962 kuqhubeka, izinhlangano ezifana neFront Des Forces Socialites (FSS), kanye ne-Front Islamique de Salut (FIS) zibe ngundaba mlonyeni ezweni lase-Algeria. Lezi zinhlangano zazaziwa ngokungaboni ngaso linye kwezepolitiki, ezenkolo kanye nobuhlanga, kusukela enhlanganweni ebizwa nge-Social Democratic and Liberal (FSS), yi-conservative kanye ne-traditional FrS kuya kwi-nationalist ~NL. Lol.u. qhekeko lwabuye lwabhebherhekiswa yizinqubomgomo ezazmgahlomz, zokuguqulwa kwe-Algeria irharha inqubo yesi-Arahhu eyaytqhutshwa yi-Islam. emva kwempi eyayishoshozelwa yimbumba ye-FNL, kwaba nokwehlukana kwezepolitiki. Emva kancane kokukhululwa kuka-Ahmed Ben Bella . nayeboshwe nabo, i-FNL yabhekana nezinxushunxushu ezishubile zangaphakathi okwathatha isikhathi esincane emlandweni. UBen Bella owayeyigagu lokukhuluma wayengabuseki ubuholi bokubambisana, futhi njengeshoshozela lezokuvukelwa kombuso wahlaba wahlikiza umbo no wokubusa ngokubambisana owawuqhutshwa yi-GPRA. Igxathu lokuqala elalibheke ku-!lrabisation lathathwa ngu-Ahmed Ben Bella owaba ngumengameli wokuqala wase-A1geria emva kwenkululeko. Njengengxenye yegxathu lokuqala ukuqinisekisa ukufundwa kwesi-Arabhu ezikoleni, ezazifundisa ngolimi IwesiFulentshi esikhathini esiyiminyaka eyikhulu namashumi amathathu nambili, umbuso ka-Ben Bella wangenisa ezweni omisha ababeqhamuka eMpumalanga ye-Arab, ikalthulukazCEgibhithe, 
Iraq naseSyria (Stone, 1997: 19). Ngesikhathi sokulunjwa kwamazwe aseMrika, lapho yonke into yayiphethwe ngamaFulentshi, iningi labantu base-Algeria babengafundile, ngenxa yomphumela wokungafinyeleli ezikhungweni zokufunda. Kodwa emva kancane kwenkululeko abantu abaningi base-Algeria, ikakhulukazi ama-Arabhu namaBhabha bathola imfundo eyisisekelo. Ngisho ngaphambi kokushintshwa kwezinto zithathe inqubo yesi-Arabhu, umengameli u-Ahmed Ben Bella wakubeka kwacaca enkulumweni ayenza mhla lu-1 kuNovemba ngonyaka we-1962, emva kwenyanga i-Algeria ithole uzimele geqe ukuthi 'Ulimi lwethu lukazwelonke lwesi-Arabhu luzothatha indawo elufanele'(Veremen, 2004: 143, ecashunwe ku Benrabah, 2005: 418). 
  Abanye babantu ababamba iqhaza elibalulekile ekuhlelweni kolimi e-Algeria yilabo ababeqhoqhobele izintambo zomb~so, labo ngosopolitiki noma amalungu ephalamende. Njengalokhu ukuhlelwa kolimi kuhlukaniswe izigaba ezintathu, izigaba.ezimbili emva kwezinga lolimi 
ngeke kufinyelelwe kuzo ngaphandle komthetho obekiwe ophathelene nesimo solimi kwezepolitiki. Yingaltho nase-Algeria kwalthishwa umthethosisekelo wokuqala mhla ziyi-l 0 ku-September ngonyaka we-I963, owachaza kabanzi izwe lase-Algeria njengengxenye ebalulekile yama-Arab Maghreb, asemhlabeni wama-Arab kanye ne-Mrika (Benrabah, 2005). Umthethosisekelo wase-Algeria wakubeka kwacaca esandulelweni ukuthi 'i-Algeria kumele ibethele isipikili sokuthi isi-Arabhu wulimi lukazwelonke nolusemthethweni futhi luthola amandla kwezikamoya ku-Islam' (Benrabah, 2005: 418-419).    Njengoba sekuke kwaphawuleka, i-Algeria yayilunjwe yi-France kusukela ngonyaka we-1930 kuya kowe-1962. Ngenxa yomphumela walokho i-France yaphoqelela indlela yase Yurophu, isiko kanye nengqalasizinda, ezomnomo, ezemfundo, ezezimboni kanye nezikhungo zikaHulumeni e-Algeria (www.arab.net). Indlela eyayiqhuba ngayo iFrance ukulumba i-Algeria yaguqula amatafula kuleliya lizwe fumi isizwe samaMusilemu sasithathwa njengesincane, kanti lesi senzo sabangela ukusungulwa kwamaqembu avukela umbuso ekudingisweni njenge-National Liberation Front (FNLO, eyasungulwa wu-Ahmed Ben Bella ngonyaka we-1950. 1950 abelumbi kanye nezikh~u zombumo wempi yaseFtance bafuna ngo 
dli ukubuya kuka-General De Gaulle ukuhola iFrance iye ekunqobeni. 
N gesikhathi sehlandla lalthe lokubusa uDe Gaule wavulela izwe ukuthi likheme phakathi kokubuswa wumbuso wama-Fulentshi noma ukuzimela qelekeqe, kanti abantu balthetha ukuzimela geqe. Lesi senzo sika- De Gaulle sathamwa wuHulumeni wamaFulentshi njengokudayiswa kombuso wamaFulentshi, kodwa-ke lesi sinyamelo asikwazanga ukuvimba i-Algeria ukuba ithole uzimele geqe ngonyaka we-I962, owabangela ukumi u-Ahmed Ben Bella abe ngumengameli wokuqala wase-A1geria. 
   Selokhu yathola uzimele geqe, i-Algeria beyilokhu ikhungethwe yizinkinga ngenxa yezinxushunxushu zangaphakathi ku-National Liberation Front (FNL). Ngesikhathi u-Ahmed Ben Bella ethatha izintambo njengomengameli wokuqala wase-Algeria emva kwenkululeko, waqalisa izinqubomgomo ezintsha, nezabangela ukuthi i-Algeria ibe yisizwe esiqhoqhobelwe yinhlangano eyodwa, lapho inhlangano eyayibizwa ngeNational Liberation Front (FNL) kwabe kuyiyiyona yodwa inhlangano esemrherhweni kuHulumeni noma ePhalamende.    Ukulangazelela amandla kwadala ubuphekula okwavuka ngaphakathi e-Algeria kangangokuthi kwafinyelela esikhathini lapho i-Algeria yacwaswa ngamazwe omhlaba. Ukwanda kobuphekula kwadala ukubulawa kuhleliwe kukamengameli uMohammed Boudiaff ngenyanga kaNhlangulana 
1992, nowalandelwa wu-Ali Kafi ngokushesha. Kusukela ngonyaka we1962, i-Algeria isibe nomengameli abayisithupha izikhathi zilandelana ngaphambi kukamengameli u-Abdelaziz Bouteflika osaqhoqhobele izinrambo njangamanje. Labo mengameli ngo-Ahmed Bell ~ella, u-Houari Boumedienne, u-Chadli Bendjedid, u-Mohamed Boudiaff, u~Ali Kafi kanye noLiamine Zeroual owakhethwa njengebamba likamengameli ngonyaka we1994. Lesi kwakuyisimo sepolitiki e-Algeria. 
   Uma sibuyela ezintweni ezithinra ulimi e-Algeria, kuyaphawuleka ukuthi esikhathini samanje ezweni lonke ulimi lwesi-Arabu lusabhula amaphiko, njengoba lukhulunywa ngamaphesenri angamashumi ayisishiyagalombili abanru. Ingxenye esele yabanru ikhuluma izilimi zesiBhabha ezehlukene, ezibuye zibizwe ngezinhlotshana ze- Tamazight, isibonelo iKabhayile (Kabyle), iMuzabu (Mzab), iShawia (Shawia), iShenowuwa (Chenoua), neTamasheki (Tamasheki). Ngesikhathi i-Algeria ithola uzimele geqe, kwaba nokuguquka kwamatafula endleleni okwakusetshenziswa 
ngayo ulimi ezikoleni zamabanga aphansi, ezikhungweni eziphakeme zemfundo, ephalamende kanye nasemithonjeni.Y0kudluliswa kwezindaba. Indawo yesiFulenrshi yathathwa yisi-Atabhu ngokushesha, lokho 
okwaba ngumphumela wokuqaliswa kokusetshen~lswa komthetho 
onqala kaHulumeni. NgokukaWebb (2002: 39), ukuthuthukiswa kwenqubomgomo yolimi kufanele kuqala kuhambisane nombono izwe elizibekele wona, lokho kusho ukuthi, izinto izwe elifuna ukufinyelela kuzo neziyizinjongo zikaHulumeni ophethe. Ngesikhathi ethatha izinrambo umengameli Ahmed Ben Bella wakubeka kwacaea kunqubomgomo ukuthi umbono we-Algeria njengezwe kwakuwukubona izwe lonke liguquka lithatha inqubo yesi-Arabhu. Yingakho yonke imithetho eyayishaywa nguHulumeni yayiqhakambisa ukuguqulwa kwe-Algeria ithathe inqubo yesi-Arabhu. Ngemva kokuba i-Algeria ithole uzimele geqe, kwakunenhloso enqala eyayivuna ukusetshenziswa kolimi lukazwelonke kwezemfundo: 

   Kubanru noma emiphakathini yase-Algeria eyayincishiwe ithuba lokuthola imfundo, izinqubomgomo zika-Ben Bella zazisho ukusuka kwenkungu ezimpilweni zabo, lokho kwadala ukuba kwande imiphakathi yama-Arabie-Berber ezikoleni. U- Webb uyaqhubeka nokuvumbulula iqiniso lokuthi; 
   Impumelelo yokuhlelwa kolimi ilele ekwesekweni ngabaholi bezombusazwe, izinqubomgomo eziphumelelayo kanye namabhodi kaHulumeni. Izinqubomgomo zidinga ukuba zigeinwe njengomthetho ophasile (njengezahluko zemithetho, izimiso kanye neziehibiyelo), noma zishaywe njengemibandela, izindlela okumele zilandelwe, ukulawulwa ngokuphatha kanye nezinqubo zezinkantolo zomthetho (2002: 41). 
   Umbono walabo abake baba omengali base-Algeria kusukela kuAhmed Ben Bella kuya ku-Ali Kafi kwakuwukuthuthukisa isi-Arabhu njengolimi kuze kube seqophelweni lokuthi lonke izwe liguqukele kusiAtabhu. Ukuthuthukiswa kwesi-Arabhu kwakuhambisana neamashi nokuthuthukiswa kwenkolo yama-Muslim. Lo mqondo uqoqwe kafushane kuleli binzana lamagama aeashunwe kuCollot noHenry, (1978: 66, becashunwe ku-Benrabah, 2005: 415) 
   Ulimi lwesi-Atabhu kuma-Musilemu luyilokho eliyiko ibandla enkolweni yamaKhatholika. Ngeke luphile ngaphandle kwawo. Inkolo yomuMusilemu ongafundile ifana nenkoleloze. Kithina i-Mosque ayilutho. Ukufundwa kwencwadi engcwele kuyikho konke. Kuma njengosemende wokukholwa kwethu. Ngakho kudingekile ukuba simemezele ukuzibophezela kwethu ukufundisa ulimi Iwesi-Atabhu, okuyisisekelo sokukholwa kwethu. 
   Ukuhlelwa kolimi kwesinye isikhathi kuhambisana nalokho abakholelwa kukho abasebuholini, yingakho u-Antonio Gramsei waqhamuka 
negama Ie-Hegemony, elisho ukuthi amandla a1okho okukholelwa kukho atholakala kakhulu ngokuvumelana kunokusetsheriziswa kwamandla. Labo abasemandleni basebenzisa izinsiza nezinro abafinyelela kuzo, kubandakanya ulimi abalukhulumayo ukusebenzisa noma kwesinye isikhathi ukusebenzisa ngokungafanele amandla abanawo. ulimi abalusebenzisayo luba ngu ngqo shishilizi kukho konke abakwenzayo, yilokho-ke uGramsci akubiza nge-Hegemony njengoba kukhulunywe ngayo

e-Algeria esikhamini esiyiminyaka eyikhulu namashumi amathathu nambili. lapho umbuso wamaFulentshi waqhoqhobala wonke amandla ngesikhathi 

30. 
   Ukufundwa nokwamukelwa kolimi kuyisigaba esimqoka ekuhlelweni kolimi noma isu lokuhlelwa kolimi. Kubandakanya amasu okuqinis~kisa ukuthi ulimi luyakhulunywa kusetshenziswa amasu noma izindlela ezahlukene. Ukuguqulwa ngokugcwele kwe-Algeria ithatha inqubo yesiArabhu, emva kokuthola uzimele geqe kwakuhambisana nokwakhiwa okunqala kwenqubomgomo kanye nokuqaliswa kokusetshenziswa kwayo ngokucophelela. Isigaba sokuqala sokuguquka kwe-Algeria ithatha inqubo yama-Arabu kwaqala njengenkolelo yesi-Islam, ngakho ukuguqulwa kwe-Algeria ithatha inqubo yama-Arabu kanye nesi-Islam kwaba yizinto ezingehlukaniseki, ikakhulukazi emva kokuthola uzimele geqe kwe-Algeria. Inkolo yamaMusilemu yabuya yaphendula imiphakathi yamaBhabha, agcina esephila ngenqubo ye-Islam, ngakho ingxenye yokusetshenziswa kwesiArabhu wumphakathi wokudabuka e-Algeria yenzeka yaba Iufa- ngolwazi olwalutholwa ngokufunda i-Koran nokulalela imiyalezo yabashumayeli bevangeli. Iminyakazo eminingi yokusebenzisa isi-Islam e-Algeria yaqala ungakaphushwa nokuphushwa uzimele geqe e-Algeria, kodwa-ke isikhathi esalandela uzimele geqe sasihambisana nokufudulwa kwabantu base- 
Algeria abakhuluma isiFulentshi. U- Veremen, (2004: 320), ecashunwe kuBenrabah, (2005: 381) ubalula iqiniso lokuthi izinkulungwane zama-Algeria althuluma isiFulentshi aqeqeshwe kabanzi ngokwamakhono nalungele umsebenzi ayephoqelelwa ukuba aye ekudingisweni, iningi labo laze layobhaca eFrance. Isimo solimi e-Algeria emva kokuthola kwezwe uzimele geqe sasingasimeme, ikakhulukazi ngesikhathi ulimi olubizwa nge-Standard/ Literay Arabic luthola ithuba lokuhlonzwa njengolimi olusemthethweni, ngakho umthetho wobulimimbili waqaliswa emva nje kancane kokuba izwe lithole uzimele geqe, yize noma wawuzoshintsha tnakhathaleni. 
  Ngesikhathi kuqhubeka isikhathi i-Standard Arabic sathatha indawo yesiFulentshi njengolimi olusemthethweni e-Algeria, kanti isiFulentshi saba wulimi lwangaphandle. 
  UBenrabah (2005: 381) uyibeka obala indlela i-Algeria eyashintsha ngayo isuka emthethweni wobuliminingi kuya kowolimilunye, lapho ethi: 
   fzinto i-Algeria eyahlangabezana nazo ngokokuhlelwa kolimi kwezemfundo zisondelene nezigaba ezimbili eziqavile: esokuqala sisukela onyakeni we-I962 kuya kowe-1970, esibonakala ngokusetshenziswa kwenqubomgomo yobulimimbili, lapho kwakusetshenziswa khona isiFulentshi kanye ne-Standard/Literary Arabic, esesibili sasinomthetho wolimi lunye, lapho i-Standard Arabic njengolimi yayikhulunywa yiningi 
emva kokuthola uzimele geqe kwe-Algeria, ake ngigawule ngigijime ngokubalula ukuthi akusibo bonke omengameli base-~geria ab~qhubeka. nenqubomgomo evuna isi-Arabhu, ngoba umengameh AbdelazIz Bouteflika wayishaya indiva yonke leyo nqubo. Ngisho namanje u-Bouteflika usebenzisa isiFulentshi ezinkulumweni zakhe azenza ephalamende nalezo azenza emphakathini. U-Bouteflika wayenomuzwa wokut~i uma izwe .laseAlgeria liqhubeka nokuguqula yonke into iqhu~sh".'e ngesl-A~a~~u nglsho kwezemfundo laliyobe lizivalela ekhoneni, kant! lal!yobe futh! IlZlvaiela iminyango yobuhlobo namazwe omhlaba. Kumanje u-Bouteflika uthatha isiFulentshi njengengxenye yesiko nomlando wase-Algeria. UBenrabah. (2005: 382-383) ubalula iqiniso lokuthi ngonyaka we-1999 [u-Boutefl!ka] wakubeka kwacaca kumabonakude ukuthi: 
  Akwazeke namhlanje ukufhi i-Algeria iyingxenye yomhlaba fu:hi. . kumele ingazikhiphi inyumbazane emazweni omhlaba, nanokuthl uhml lwesi-Arabhu luwulimi lukazwelonke nolusemthethweni. Ngokusho 
lokho, akwazeke futhi ukuthi ukungafaki imigoqo ebuhlotsheni nezinye izilimi, okungenani lezo ezingaphansi kwenhlangano Yezizwe akuy~na ingxenye yobuxoki. Kuleli qophelo asiwona ama-Arabhu ngokweq,le ~oma sihlakaniphe ngokweqile kunabanye ozakwethu base-Morocco, e-TunlSla, e-Gibhithe, E-Jolidani, e-Siriya, E-Libanoni, e-Palestine nakwezinye izingxenye zomhlaba. Ukuze zithathe igxathu eliya phambili kumele saphule lokhu okubizwa ngemitheshwana esingazi yashaywa nguba~i. Lena yinkokhelo okumele siyikhokhe ukuze siphucule izwe lethu nobuthma njengama-Algeria. Ukuzibona njengezihlakaniphi (Chauvinism) kanye nokuzibandIulula kuphelile, akusenamsebenzi. 
   Le ngxenyana yenkulumo ikhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi u-Ab~elaziz Bouteflika wayemelene nomqondo wokuthi i-Algeria iphendulwe Izwe lama-Arabhu ngoba lokho kwakuthiya izwe ukuba lizibandakanye kubuhlobo namanye amazwe, kodwa-ke konke 10\910 kwakuphambene nenqubo yabomengameli abendulela uBouteflika. UBouteflika wayekusho esidlangalaleni ukuthi ufuna ukubuyisa kabusha ulimi lwesi-Fulentshi ukuba lube wulimi olusemthethweni, kangangokuthi wenza umbhidlango wokuphucula izikhungo zase-Algeria, isibonelo inqubo yezemfundo eyayithathwa ngabanye njengehlathi. Ngakho-ke ngesikhathi uBouteflika eqhoqhobala izintambo kwaba nengwijikhwebll nokllgllqllka kwamat~fula endleleni okllsetshenziswa ngayo 1I1imi e-Algeria kanye nasemlandwem wezwe jikelele. Umthetho wolimilunye (lapho isi-Arabhu sasithathwa 


  Kusukela ngesikhathi senkululeko, abatshali bezimali bamaFulenrshi bahoxa ukufaka izimali zabo e-Algeria, futhi ngaphezu kwalokho abanru bokudabuka eFrance ababeyizakhamizi e-Algeria balibalekela izwe ngesikhathi sokubusa kuka-Ahmed Ben Bella. NgoNhlangulana onyakeni wezi-2000, ungqongqoshe oqavile wezomnotho wabhala isiqeshana sombhalo kujeneli ephuma masonro onke lapho wayenxenxa khona abatshali bezimali bama-Fulenrshi ukuba bafake izimali zabo e-Algetia. Wabuye wakuvuma futhi ukuthi isi-Fulenrshi njengolimi singaba yithuluzi lokufinyelela kwe-Algetia ezingeni lomhlaba lomnotho nanokuthi ibe yingxenye yeNhlangano Yomhlabuhlangene (UNESCO) ngokusho kukaBenrabah (2005: 384). Manje ngizoke ngibuyele futhi kumagxathu aqavile athathwa ngoHulumeni base-Algeria ngaphambi kwehlandla lokubusa kukaBouteflika. 
Kusukela ngesikhathi sikazimele-geqe, oHulumeni base=Algeria 
sebenze lukhulu ukuthuthukisa isi-Arabhu ukuba sibe wulimi 
lokuxhumana (emigudwini yokudlulisa izindaba), siphinde sibe wulimi lokufundisa ezikoleni, sisetshenziswe ezikhungweni zikaHulumeni kanye nakwezobuchwepheshe. Kungakapholi maseko nje, u-Ahmed Ben Bela eqhoqhobele izinrambo e-Algeria wasungula umthetho owawubizwa phecelezi nge-Arabisation, nokwakuwumthetho owawuzoqhutshwa ababezomlandela esihlalweni sombuso njengo-Boumedienne, Bendjedid, Zeroual, Kafi kanye noBoudiaff. UBen Bella akakuhlonizanga ukuthi uzothuthukisa ulimi lwesi-Arabhu, kanri lelo gxathu lalibekwe lacaca kumthethosisekelo owaphasiswa mhla zi-l 0 kuMandulo ngonyaka we-I 963, nowawuchaza i-Algeria njengengxenye ebalulekile ye-Arabhu Maghreb emazweni esi-Arabhu kanye nase-Mrika' (Benrabah, 2005: 418). Ziningi izinro ezenziwa e-Algeria njengamagxathu okuthuthukisa nokukhuthaza uhlelo lokuguqulwa kwe-Algeria ithathe inqubo yesj-Arabhu ngeminyaka yawo-1970. Isibonelo, unyaka we-1971 wamenyezelwa ngokusemthethweni njengonyaka wokuguqula i-Algeria ithathe inqubo yesi-Arabhu, lokho okwadala ukuthi kwakhiwe ngokushesha izikhungo zokuhlolisisa uhlelo lokuhlelwa kolimi e-Algeria njengeKomidi lezemfundo ephakeme kanye neKhomishana likaZwelonke lokwenziwa kwesi-Arabhu sibe semthethweni. 
   UChadli Bendjedid, owalandela uHouari Boumedienne njengomengameli wase-Algeria waqhamuka nezinqubomgomo ezazishubile zokuguqulwa kwe-Algetia ithathe inqubo yesi-Arabhu. Kusukela mhla ziyi-12 kuya mhla zingama-20 kuZibandlela ngonyaka we-1973, i-Algeria yabamba ukhukhulela ngoqo womhlangano kazwelonke owawubizwa ngePnn Arnh ron""ess. nowaohakamisa ukusungulwa kwamaRama asetshenziswa 
2005). Makhathaleni ngonyaka we-1970, nasekuqaleni konyaka we- 
1980 uhlelo lwe-Arabisation e-Algeria lwasabalala kangangokuthi lwaze lwafinyelela nakunqubo yezobulungiswa kanye nasezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme. Isibonelo, ekuqaleni konyaka we-1980 ngesikhathi uBendjedid esaqhoqhobele izinrambo iziphathimandla zase-Algeria zathatha isinqumo sokuguqula inqubo yezobulungiswa e-Algetia ithathe inqubo yesi-Arabhu, kanri leli gxathu ladala amathuba omsebenzi amaningi (Ruedy, 1992: 228, ecashunwe kuBenrabah, 2005: 424). U-fusous (1985: 137), ecashunwe kuBenrabah (2005: 424) ubalula iqiniso lokuthi mhla ziyi-14 ku-Agasti ngonyaka we-1980, uMnyango Wezemfundo Ephakeme waphakamisa ukuthi iMinyango ye-Social Sciences ne-Humanities ezikhungweni eziphakeme e-Algeria iqhutshwe ngesi-Arabhu, kwathi futhi mhla ziyi-II kuNovember ngonyaka owodwa kwakhiwa iKhomishani yokuguqula zonke izinro e-Algeria zithathe inqubo yesi-Arabhu. Ngokushesha iNyuvesi yaseAlgiers yasungula ingxenye yesi-Arabhu eMnyangweni Wezomthetho kwathi izifundo zama-Bachelor kwezomlando zafundiswa ngesi-Arabhu (Benrabah, 2005: 443). 
  Ngesikhathi esasukela onyakeni we-1970 kuya kowe-1970, i-Arabisation ikakhulukazi kwezemfundo yadlondlobala. Lokhu kwaba yinruthuko ebalulekile ngoba imfundo idlala indima ebalulekile ekufundweni 
kolimi. E-Algetia kwenzeka isimo esingajwayelekile kwezemfundo 
ngesikhathi sehlandla lokubusa kuka- Houari Boumedienne. UMnyango Wezemfundo wahlukaniswa ngokushesha waba yiminyangwana emithathu, okwakuwuMnyango Wezemfundo yamabanga aphansi kanye nalawo 
asethe thuthu, uMnyango Wezemfundo Ephakeme (Ministry of Higher Education) kanye noMnyango wezemfundo yama-Islam (Ministry of Islamic Education). Leli gxathu kwaba elibaluleke kakhulu ekufundweni kolimi lwesiArabhu, kauti uMnyango Wemfundo yama-Islam wawubhekelele kuphela ukuthuthukiswa nokusabalalisa ukusetshenziswa kolimi lwesi-Arabhu ezikoleni. Ngokuka-Rueddy (1992: 228), ecashunwe kuBenrabah (2005: 446-447), ngonyaka we-1985, amanani abafundi abakhuluma isi-Arabhu emabangeni asethe thuthu nasemabangeni emfundo ephakeme ayemi kanje: amaphesenti angama-65 abafundi abejwayelekile basemazingeni asethethe thuthu ezemfundo, amaphesenri angama- 28 abafundi abasezingeni eli the thuthu nasemazingeni aphakeme ezemfundo, amaphesenti angu-32.5 abafundi abangakazithwali iziqu emfundweni esemazingeni aphakeme emfundo, kauti labo asebemnkanrshubomvu babengamaphesenri angama-20.

Lona-ke belugxile esifUndazweni saKwaZulu-Nataii kuphela. Ngalesi sikhathi isi-Fulentshi sathatha isimo sokuba wulimi lwangaphandle. UGordon (1978: 153), ecashunwe kuBentabah (2005: 443) ubalula iqiniso lokuthi ngonyaka we-1971 uHulumeni wathatha inqubo eyayibizwa ngokuthi yi 'punctual system', neyayibandakanya ukuguqulwa kwazo zonke izifundo zifundiswe ngesi-Arabhu ezingeni elibekiwe, esikhundleni sokuguqulwa endaweni yonke (Isibonelo, ukuguqulwa kwezifundo zifundiswe ngesi-Arabhu ezikoleni ezithile zasemakhaya nasezindaweni ezinogwadule), noma ukuguqulwa okubizwa nge-'Vertical' Arabisation, lapho kwakuguqulwa isifUndo ngesifundo sifUndiswe ngesi-Arabhu. Inqubo yezemfu~do e-Algeria yayikhomba izimpawu zobandlululo, ngenxa yalokho emva kwenkululeko, ngoMandulo onyakeni we-1976, kwaba noguquko kwezemfUndo. Kusukela ngonyaka we-1976, uHulumeni waqalisa ukusebenzisa inqubo eyayihlolwa ngaleso sikhathi neyayibizwa ngokuthi yi-Fundamental School, okwakungukuhlanganiswa kwamabanga emfUndo aphansi namaphakathi, lapho zonke izifUndo zazifUndiswa ngesi-Arabhu ngaphandle kwezilimi zangaphandle (Benrabah, 2005: 444). Ngokuka-Benrabah (2005: 444), ngaphambi konyaka we[1976], inqubo nokuhlelwa kwezemfUndo kwakunezinkomba zenkathi yokulunjwa, kanti kwezemfundo izikole zazihlukaniswe izigaba ezintathu: 
Izikole zamabanga aphansi (ezazinesikalo seminyaka emihlanu), lzikole zasemazingeni amaphakathi (ezazinesikalo seminy:l/.<a emine), kanye nezikole ezisemazingeni aphezulu. Emazingeni amabili okugcina kwakubhalwa ukuhlolwa njengendlela yokuhlolela abafundi ukuthi bakulungele yini ukuyofunda ezikoleni zemfUndo ephakeme, phecelezi (Six Form or Examen de Six ieme) , noma phecelezi (Baccalaureate Examination). Zonke lezi zinguquko zaziyimiphumela yokuqaliswa ukusebenza kwenqubo yokuguqulwa kwayo yonke into ibe yisi-Arabhu e-Algeria. 
   Ukwenza inqubomgomo isebenze e-Algeria kwafinyelela ngisho eminyangweni eyahlukene kahulumeni, bheka nje ngoba amaphepha aqukethe imininingwane yezakhamizi (njengamarekhodi okuzalwa, ukushada nokufa kwabantu), kanjalo nezakhiwo noma izinsiza P7i'Pt.,hpn7.iswa kakhulu wumphakathi (njengamahholo amadolobhakazi, 




uMnyango Wezomisebenzi yomphakathi, uMnyango Wamasiko kanye noMnyango Wezemidlalo), konke lokho kwashintshwa kwaqhutshwa ngesiArabhu. Ngokuka-Grandguillaume (1983: 190), ecashunwe ku-Benrabah (2005: 454), ekupheleni kukaZibandlela wonyaka we-1976, uMnyango Wezangaphakathi waqasha amaphoyisa abesifazane abangamashumi amahlanu ababekhuluma fUthi beqhuba ngenqubo yesi-Arabhu. 
U-Benrabah (2005: 254) ubalula iqiniso lokuthi mhla lulunye ku-Mashi ngonyaka we-1976 zonke izimpawu ezazisasemigwaqeni ewuthelawayekwa, izitolo kanye nezakhiwo ezilawula izinqubo zezwe njalo njalo), kanye nezincwadi zokushayela zashintshwa zaqhutshwa fUthi zabhalwa ngesiArabhu. Ngalesi sikhathi kwakucaeele noma wubani ukuthi iziphathimandla ezazikuHulumeni wase-Algeria zazifUna ukubona yonke into ishintshiwe yenziwa ngesi-Arabhu. U-Imaeha (1989), ecashunwe kuBenrabah (2005: 424) wenaba ngokubalula iqiniso lokuthi ngisho emahhovisi okubhaliswa kwemininingwane yabanru, ainagama emindeni ahunyushwa abhalwa ngesi-Arabhu, kwathi izingane ezisanda kuzalwa zanikwa amagama okuqala ngesi-Arabhu kanti abazali banqatshelwa ukunika izingane zabo amagama esiBhabha. 
   Ukwenza inqubomgomo yesi-Arabhu isebenze kwafinyelela kuvuthondaba ngesikhathi kubandakanya nemboni yokushieilelwa kwemibhalo, kanti kwathi ngonyaka we-I966, iziphathimandla zase- 
Algeria zasungula indlu kazwelonke yokushicicelwa kwemibhalo eyayibizwa ngokuthi yi-Societe Nationale dEdition et de Fusion (SNED). Inhloso enkulu yaleli gxathu kwakungukuvumela ababhali abambalwa abasafUfusa besiArabhu ukuba bashieilele imisebenzi yabo e-Algeria kunokuba bathembele emazweni ama-Arabhu aseMpumaianga Emaphakathi (Middle East) (Benrabah, 2005). Ekugeineni Ie nqubo yafinyelela nasembonini yokugaywa kwamaphepha. Emva kweminyaka eminingi kuphethe uHulumeni wabelumbi, imigudu yokudluliswa kwemibiko yayilawulwa wuHulumeni wama-Fulentshi, kodwa emva kwenkululeko, iziphathimandla zase-Algeria zathatha izintambo zokulawula, fUthi baletha uguquko 01 usheshayo ngoba makhathaleni imigudu yokudluliswa kwemibiko, yaguqulwa yaqhutshwa ngesi-Arabhu. 
   Ekugeineni, umunru kumele avume ukuthi i-Algeria seyenze lukhulu ukuthuthukisa nokuphakamisa ulimi lwesi-Arabhu, emikhakheni nasemazingeni ehlukene, kusukela kwezemfUndo, izikhungo zikaHulumeni, ezobulungiswa kanye nezezindaba, ikakhulukazi uma sizobheka ukuthi akudlali ukuqhoqhobalwa abelumbi iminyaka eyikhulu namashumi amathathu nambili. 11. IMIZAMO YOKUHLELA UKUFUNDWA NOKWAMUKELWA KOLIMI ENYUVESI YAKWAZULU- NATALI 
  Umrherhosisekelo onikeza igunya lokuba zonke izilimi ezisetshenziswa abanru baseNingizimu Afrika zisershenziswe ngokukhuIuleka nangokuthanda kwalowo muntu okhuluma 1010 limi, washicilelwa ngonya1<a we- 1996 uHulumeni kaZwelonke kanye nesigungu sakhe esengamele yonke imirhetho eshicilelwayo. Lokhu kufakazelwa isigaba samashumi amarharhu somthethosisekelo (Act no2, section 30, 1996) lapho uthi: 
  Wonke umuntu unelungelo lokusebenzisa ulimi alukherhayo furhi abambe iqhaza empilweni yamasiko ayikhethayo, kodwa akekho o~nyelwe ukusebenzisa la malungelo ngendlela engahambisani nanoma yisiphi isimiso soMqulu wamalungelo. 
Inqubomngomo yolimi kaZwelonke emfundweni ephakeme yashicilelwa 
. ngonyaka wezi- 2002, iNingizi~u-Afrika yabe seyamukelwa kuzona 
zonke izikhungo zemfundo ephakeme. Lokhu kwaveza inselelo enkulu emfundweni ephakeme ukuqinisekisa ukuthi iyalandelwa. Ngonyaka 
wezi- 2003, iKomidl likaNgqongqoshe Wezemfundo lasungulwa ukuze ligqugquzele furhi libe isisombululo ekukhuliseni zonke izilimi zabansundu ngoba yizona ebezikade zingenayo inkululeko, ngakho Iesi sigungu sasungulwa ukuze sibhekelele lezi zilimi ukuthi zisershenziswe njengolimi lokuxhumana ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme. Iziphakamiso ezenziwe yileli Komidi embikweni walo (2005: 22) uthi: 
  Yileso naleso sikhungo seinfundo ephakeme ku,:nele sibe nolimi labomdabu oluzosetshenziswa njengolimi lokuxhumana, uma kungakenziwa lokho kumele kube nemizamo eyenziwayo ewuhlelo lokuthurhukisa ulimi eminyakeni emibili noma emithathu ezayo. 
Esinye isiphakamiso siveza ukuthi yileso naleso sikhungo 
sezemfundo ephakeme kumele sikwazi ukuthola ulimi lomdabo oluzoba ngolukhululekile ekutheni umuntu azikhethele lona alusebenzise ngaphandle kwemibandela. Kungalezi zizarhu ngikhethe ukuveza imizamo eseyenziwe isikhungo sezemfundo ephakeme iNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Naraii ukuhlela ukufunda nokwamukelwa kolimi. Kuzovezwa izingqinamba isikhungo esihlangabezana nazo ekwenzeni lokhu ukuze inqubomgomo yolimi isebenze nokuthi yimaphi amathuba abawavezayo ekuthuthukiseni ulimi IwesiZulu njengolimi lokuxhumana esikhungweni semfundo ephakeme.

Isikhungo sesibili esibizwa ngeHoward College eyaziwa ngokuthi kuse Thusini ngenxa yewashi lethusi eliphezu kwebhilidi. Lesi sikhungo siqeqesha abafundi emkhakheni wezifundo zobuntu, zobunjiniyela, eziphathelene nokusebenza kwengqondo neminye imikhakha njengowobuhlengikazi. Isikhungo sesithathu iNeison Mandela esiqeqesha odokotela bamakhambi. Isikhungo sesine i-Edgewood, yona iqeqesha abafundisi bezikole zamazinga ahlukene. Isikhungo sesihlanu uMgungundlovu, sona-ke siqeqesha amakhono amaningi atholakala eThusini, nase-Edgewood ngoba sona sithe Iikuqhela eThekwini. Inyuvesi yonke yenganyelwe nguSolwazi uMakgoba. 
   Sizogxila-ke emizamweni eyenziwa yile Nyuvesi ukuhlela ulimi, siveze namaqiniso ngolimi, izinhlelo zolimi ezihlelelwe ukuthuthukisa ulimi eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali, inqubomgomo yolimi lweNyuvesi kanye nokunye okuyizidingo zokuthuthukisa ulimi kule Nyuvesi. Uma sikhuluma ngokuhlelwa kolimi kumele sibheke nazi izinto ezintathu ezingumsuka wolimi: ukuthola amaqiniso, ukuvela kwezinjongo ngokuzokwenziwa 
kanye nezindlela zokuhlola okuzokwenziwa. Sekuxoxiwe ngenqubomgomo yolimi yeNyuvesi esahlukweni sesithathu evuna ubulimimbili 
okuyisiNgisi nesiZulu. Le nqubomgomo yakhishwa kulandelwa Uhlaka Lwenqubomgomo Yolimi Yezikhungo Zemfundo Ephakame (2002). Ukuthuthukiswa kwezilimi kuyingxenye yenhlosongqangi kahulumeni waseNingizimu Afrika wentando yabantu. Ungqongqoshe Wezemfundo Kuzwelonke, uNkosikazi Naledi Pandot wahlangana nomphathi weNyuvesi baxoxisana ngenqubomgomo yolimi ngoba wakuthokozela okwenziwa isikhungo ngokuphumela obaJa ngesinqumo saso sokweseka ubulimimbili ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme. Akugcinanga uPandor yedwa ekuvuneni inqubomgomo yobuliminingi ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme kanjaJo noNdunankulu wesifundazwe saKwaZulu-Natali kanye nekomidi lakhe bahlangana nabaphathi bezemfundo ephakeme babonisana ngokubaJuleka kokuba kugqugquzelwe ubuliminingi kunobulimimbili emaNyuvesi. UNksz. Pandor wathi inhlosongqangi yenqubomgomo yolimi ukuba kuthuthukiswe zonke izilimi ezikhulunywayo ukuze zingagcini nje ngokuba zikhulunywe 
lokhu kuyodingeka ukuba kuvuselelwe ukufundiswa kwezilimi emaNyuvesi ukuze kwande isibaJo sabafundi abazoqeqeshelwa izilimi, kwande nabafundisi abanolwazi oludingekile oluzosiza ekufundiseni ulimi. 
   Uma sibheka kwezemfundo kumele sizibuze umbuzo wokuthi ngabe izilimi zabomdabu ziyasetshenziswa yini njengokusho komthethosisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika ogqugquzela ukusetshenziswa kobuliminingi? UWollf (2000: 129) uthi imibuzo ngezilimi zabomdabu zase-Afrika kwezemfundo ingachazwa njenganezinye izinkinga ezihambisana nokusershenziswa 
kolimi kanye nokungathuthuki kolimi ngokujwayelekile kwezemfundo e-Afrika. Ngokubheka konke lokhu iNyuvesi yaKwaZtilu-Nataii yaphumela obaJa njengesikhungo sezemfundo ephakeme yabamba iqhaza ekutheni ithuthukise ulimi. 
  Ulimi yilona oluchaza ukuthi umuntu ukhululekile ngoba uma ukuxhumana ukwenza ngolimi lwakho yilapho ukwazi ukusho yonke imizwa yakho kanye nokuqondisa kahle inkulumo yakho ngendlela 
of una ukuyibeka ngayo. Kuyamangaza ukuthi noma sithi sikhululekile kodwa kunabantu ikakhulukazi abakhuluma izilimi zabomdabu ababona kuyihlazo ukusebenzisa ulimi lwabo njengolimi lokuxhumana sikuyekeke ukulusebenzisa ukufundisa. Uma sithi sikhululekile kodwa sisabona kuyihlazo ukukhuluma ulimi lwethu okusho ukuthi sisazicindezelile 
thina uqobo. Sidinga ukwenia lokhu uWathiong'o (l9S6) akubiza ngokukhuculula inkuna egcwele engqondweni yethu. UKamwangamala (1997: 237) uyakuvuma lokhu uthi abakhulumi bolimi abaluncele ebeleni ulimi lwabo baqoka ukukhtiluma isiNgisi kunokukhuluma olwabo ulimi. Lokhu ukubiza ngokuthi ukucwaswa kwezilimi. 
   1mizamo esiyenziwe iNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Nataii ukusimamisa ulimi ibandakanya ukwakhiwa kweBhodi Lolimi leNyuvesi. Leli Bhodi seliqaJile ukwenza uhla lwezinhlelo okubhekeleke ukuba zithuthukise ulimi.   Okwesibili ukuthi iNyuvesi izimisele ngokuba ulimi IwesiZulu nesiNgisi lusetshenziswe ngokuseqophelweni eliphezulu. INyuvesi iyokwenza

ulimi abaqalayo ukulufunda, lokhu sekusabalale kwaze kwaheha amazwe omhlaba ikakhulukazi izwe laseMelika. Izikhungo eziningi zemfundo ezifana no- Wisconsin-Madison, Albany, Illionois Urbana-Champaign, Pennsylvania, Califonia, Yale, Temple, Georgia nezinye eziningi zifundisa isiZulu njengolimi Iwesibili. Phezu kwalokho lezi zikhungo ziletha abafundi babo eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Nataii ukuze bazoqeqeshwa futhi olimini nasemasikweni esiZulu, bathole nethuba lokuhlala nemindeni ekhuluma isiZulu. 
  INyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Nataii yabheka ulimi njengesikhali sokusebenza kwezemfundo ephakeme, lokhu yakwenza ngokuba igqugquzelwa inqubomgomo yolimi kwezemfundo yonyaka we-1997 kanye nohlaka Iwenqubomgomo yolimi ezikhungweni zeMfundo Ephakeme (2002). INyuvesi ikhiphe inqubomgomo yolimi ukubheka isidingo esikhona sokuba kusungulwe futhi kuphakanyiswe noma kuqhakanjisWe;zilimi ezisemthethweni ngokusezingeni lokuthi abazisebenzisayo bakwazi ukulukhuluma nokulubhala 1010 limi, ikakhulukazi ulimi lwesiZulu nesiNgisi. 
  Ukusimamisa ulimi IwesiZulu nakho kuyosiza kakhulu ekwakheni isizwe ngoba kuyokwenza kubelula ukuxhumana nabantu bonke besifundazwe saKwaZulu- Natali ngoba abantu abangamaphesenti angama- 84 abakhele lesi sifundazwe bakhulilma isiZulu ngakho kuyoba lula ukuxhumana nabo ngolimi Iwabo. Inqubomgomo yale Nyuvesi ukwenza iNingizimu-Mrika ibe ubuliminingi ngokwangempela, ngakho inqubomgomo yayo ikubeke kwasobala ukuthi kunesidingo esikhulu sokuba kugqugquzelwe futhi kuhlonishwe zonke izilimi ezisemthethweni. Ngokusho komthethosisekelo waseNingizimu-Mrika kubandakanye izilimi ezisetshenziselwa imigubho zisimamise umnotho ngokwamasiko, kwezesayensi'kanye nakwezomnotho 
ukuze zihlale zenza ubumbano. 	. .:-, 
  Le nqubomgomo yale Nyuvesi ithi ukuqwashisa ngobuliminingi. kungenzeka ngokuthi kwaziswe izilimi ezisemthethweni esifundazweni saKwaZulu-Natali, lezi zilimi okuyisiZulu, isiNgisi, isiXhosa kanye nesiBhunu. Ithi kunesidingo sokuba kuthuthukiswe isiZulu kulesi 
sikhungo ngenxa yesifundazwe esikuso. Lokhu kuyothuthukisa izidingo zezinsizakusebenza ukuthi zenyuse izinga lokusebenza kwesiZulu njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa kanye nokwengamela. Kanjalo nesidingo sokuba kwenziwe ucwaningo ekuhlelweni kolimi kanye nasekulusunguleni. Lokhu okushiwo inqubomgomo ngohlaka Iwayo olusezinhleni zayo akusho ikuthi isiNgisi sona siyobe sesingasasetshenziswa, kodwa iNyuvesi iyoqhubeka

kwaso njengolimi lokwengeza ekuxhumaneni nasekufundiseni kuhlanganiswa izinsizakusebenza ezingeni eliphezulu kanye nasesimweni esijwayelekile. Lokhu kuyokwenza ukusetshenziswa kolimi kwamukeleke kuyo yonke imikhakha yesikhungo. 
Inqubomgomo yeNyuvesi ibheke isibalo sabafundi abakhona 
ekwenzeni lolu hlaka lokusimamisa ulimi. Umsebenzi omkhulu weNyuvesi ukusabalalisa ulwazi ngokuba ibheke izinga eliphezulu kuzwelonke futhi yengeze ukuze igcine ulwazi ngokucwaninga kanye nokuxhumana nabafundi ezweni lonke kanye nangaphandle kwe-Mrika. Le Nyuvesi isesifundazweni saKwaZulu-Natali, lokhu kwenza abafundi abakhuluma isiZulu emakhaya abo babe iqembu elikhulu uma uqhathanisa nabafundi abakhuluma 
ezinye izilimi. Kungalesi sizathu iNyuvesi ibone kungumsebenzi wayo 
ukuba inikeze uhlelo lolimi kanye namasiko azolungela bonke abafundi. Ukubhekelela izinga leNyuvesi ekusabalaliseni nasekufakeni ulwazi ngokocwaningo elwenzile kanye nokusebenza kwayo kwangaphandle kuncike kakhulu ekugqugquzeleni nasekubumbeni isiZulu ngokugcwele. IsiZulu siwulimi olusemthethweni lapha eNingizimu-Mrika njengoba sibhaliwe kumthethosisekelo, ukusebenza kwaso kanye nezinga laso kunomlando ojulile, ngakho-ke iNyuvesi ngokulandela umthethosisekelo ibophezekile ekutheni yenze okuhle nokubalulekile ekutheni ithathe izinqumo ezijulile ekusimamiseni izinga lolimi kanye nokuthuthukisa ukusetshenziswa kolimi lwesiZulu. 
  INyuvesi iyasazisa isikhundla solimi lwesiNgisi njengolimi olusetshenziswa kakhulu eNyuvesi njengolimi lokufundisa, ngakho ayisho ukuthi asingabi sezingeni esikuso isiNgisi kodwa ithi akuthuthukiswe isiZulu ukuze sisebenze ezingeni elilinganayo nesiNgisi. Ngakho-ke iNyuvesi izimisele ukusithuthukisa isiZulu ukuze sibe ulimi lokufunda nokufundisa eNyuvesi. Ukusimamisa ulimi IwesiZulu eNyuvesi, kuyodingeka ukuba isungule izichazimazwi nezinye izinsiza zokufunda nokufundisa. N genxa yalokhu iNyuvesi kumele yakhe uhlelo lolimi olunezinhlelo abazosebenzela phezu kwazo zibe nesikhathi esihleliwe kanye nezindleko eziyosetshenziswa. Ukuphumelela kukho konke lokhu okusohlelweni iNyuvesi kumele isebenzisane ngokusondelene nenhlangano eyengamele ulimi kuzwelonke iPanSALB, uNgqongqoshe Wezemfundo kanye noMnyango Wezamasiko. Ukusimamisa konke lokhu iNyuvesi kumele inikeze izinsizakusebenza eziyosiza ekutheni zithuthukise ulwazi IwesiZulu nesiNgisi. 
  Wonke 10 msebenzi uhlelwa iBhodi Lolimi elengamele ukuthuthukiswa kolimi eNyuvesi 'yaKwaZulu-Nataii okufanele ukuthi ngabe luqalile ukusebenza ngonyaka wezi-2008. Ukubuyekezwa kwenqubomgomo yolimi 




wesigaba sokuqala. Inqubomgomo yolimi ezikbungweni zemfundo ephakeme (2002) yiyona enikeza Ie Nyuvesi ugqozi lokuba ibambe iqhaza ekuthuthukiseni ulimi. Le nqubo ibheka lokbu: Izilimi zokufundisa, ikusasa lezilimi zaseNingizimu-Mrika njengezifundo zokufunda nokucwaninga, ukufundwa kwezilimi zakwamanye amazwe kanye nokuthuthukiswa kobuliminingi emithethweni yezikbungo zemfundo ephakeme. 
  Nakuba kulesi sikbathi esiphila kuso abanrwana abasebenzisa izilimi zabomdabu bebona sengathi kungukungaphucuzeki ukusebenzisa ulimi lwakbo, babukela izilimi zabo phansi babone ukuthi uma ukbuluma 
ulimi IwesiNgisi ubonakala njengomuntu ongcono nophezulu. Imbongi uMzwakbe Mbuli (1994) iNingizimu Mrika ithola inkululeko wahaya inkondlo yakbe eyayiphawula ngokubaluleka kolimi lapho athi 'ukufa kolimi ukufa kwengqondo, ukufa kwengqondo ukufa komuntu' ngamafuphi uma umuntu ekuncisha ilungelo lokukbuluma ngolimi lwakbo usuke ekubulala. Kodwa esikbathini samanje abantu abawazi amalungelo abo ngolimi bancama impilo yabo kunokuba balwele amalungelo olimi lwabo. Inkinga enkulu esibhekene nayo lapha e-Mrika ukuthi sisabuswa umqondo wokucindezeleka ohambisana namasiko ahlukene akbinyabeza umuntu. Konke lokbu kungumphumela ongemuhle endleleni esibuka ngayo izilimi zabomdabu zase-Mrika. Abaholi base-Mrika babona isiN gisi kungulimi oluphakathi nendawo olungasetshenziswa ukuvikela izimo zobuhlanga phakathi kwama-Mrika ewonke (Mateene, 1999: 171). Lesi sihloko kuzokbulunywa ngaso kabanzi esahlukweni esilandelayo. 
  Ekucindezeleni izilimi zabomdabu babona ukuthi umnotho ngeke wasimama uma kungasetshenziswa ulimi olungakathuthuki kwezemfundo. Uma sibheka lokbu osekuphawuliwe maqondana nolimi emkbakbeni wezemfundo kusinika isithombe sokuthi phezu kwemizamo emingaka

iNyuvesi esiyihlelile kungenzeka ingaphumeleli ngokohlelo lwesikbathi 
abasinqumile uma kusenohlobo lwabantu ababukela phansi ulimi lwabo. Imizamo yokufundisa ulimi ibandakanya ukufundisa ulimi ezikoleni, ukwenziwa kwezinsizakufunda lapho umfundi engazifundela ngokwakbe kanye nokukbiqizwa kobuciko bokubhala, amaphephandaba, izinhlelo ezilula zomabonisakude kanye nemisakazo. Kungenziwa isibonelo ngezwe lakwa-Israel nolimi lwakbona isiHebheru. Ukuqinisekisa ukuthi abantu bayalufunda yini ulimi kuyaye kwenziwe imigomo ephoqa ukusetshenziswa kolimi. Sibuka kbona belu ezweni lakwa- Israellapho abanrwana bakbona bephoqwa ukuba bafunde isiNgisi ukuze baphase umatikuletsheni wabo. kusuke phezulu kuHulumeni kwehle njalo kuze kubantu. UHulumeni ubambe iqhaza elikbulu ekutheni akbe izidingo zokuthi kufundwe izilimi ezithile ikakbulukazi izilimi zabomdabu lezo obekuyizona ebezinganakiwe ngesikbathi sikaHulumeni wobandlululo. Ukuphumelelisa uhla IweNyuvesi maqondana nokwenza imizamo yokwamukela ulimi, iNyuvesi ibheka 
ulimi njengethuluzi lentuthuko kwezemfundo. Kuyinto ebalulekile ukuthi kuhlolwe amakbono olimi adingekayo kanye nokuthuthukisa ulwazi, ukuqonda kanye namakbono abafundi. Lokbu kudinga ubudlelwano obukbona phakathi kolimi kanye nokuqonda, okuzosetshenziswa 
uma sekukbulunywa empikiswaneni ngolimi lokufun'da nokufundisa. Kunamaphuzu ayisithupha abalulekile obudlelwano phakathi kolimi nokuqonda okufundwayo.

2.) Ukwazi ukucabanga:bgokwezibalo, ngokomlando, ngokolimi njll. 3.) Umfundi kumele akwazi ukuthi athule imiqondo ephikisayo noma egxekayo ngendlela eyamukelekile, akwazi ukubona amagama anobudlelwano bemibuzo esebenzisa amagama afanayo isb.xoxa, chaza, qhathanisa, gxeka, nikeza njl!. 
4.) Abafundi kumele bakwazi ukufunda izincwadi ngokuqonda isithombe salokbuabakufundayo, babone amaphuzu asemqoka kanye nalawo alekelelayo. 
5.) Abafundi kufanele bakwazi ukuxhumana ngesikbathi kufundwa. 6.) Ulimi luyigugu, yilona esethula ngalo imizwa yethu, isiko lobuzwe bomuntu njl!.

12. IM/BUZO NGEZ/LIM/ ZOMDABU KWEZEMFUNDO E-AFRIKA 
   Imibuzo ngezilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika kwezemfundo ngokuka Wolff (2000: 129) ingachazwa njenganezinye zezinkinga ezihambisana nokusetshenziswa kolimi kanye nokungathuthuki kolimi ngokujwayelekile ikakhulukazi kwezemfundo e-Afrika. Lapha-ke u Wolff ubheke umbuzo wolimi lomdabu Iwase-Afrika kwezemfundo. Uthi kulona lolu daba kukhona neqhaza Iolimi lomdabu njengolimi lokufundisa okuhambisana nombiko Wekomidi likaNgqongqoshe Wezemfundo eNingizimu Afrika (2005). Uthi udaba lwezilimi zomdabu angeke lusonjululwe ngaphandle kokuthi kuqale kucaciswe iqhaza lezilimi zomdabu njengezilimi ; zokufundisa. Lokhu akusho ukuthi akuyekwe isiNgisi, isiFulenrshi noma jsiPur~kezj nezinye izilimi ekufundiseni kwezemfundo. Lezi zilimi zidinga ukurhl zlbekwe endaweni yazo kwezemfundo emazweni ase-Afrika Ak

esmgazlqo a njengezilimi zokufundisa ezinhlelweni zemfundo e-Afrika.

Kuncane okwenziwayo ukuthurhukisa lezi zilimi. Umbuzo wezilimi zomdabu ubandakanya amaqiniso arhi ama-Afrika arshelwa amanga ngezilimi zawo, futhi nawo akholwe amanga lawo afana nalawa:

kwezemfundo. Akwenzekanga ngokwezifiso zabo ngoba isimo sehluke kakhulu e-Afrika yonkana. Izilimi zomdabu zenziwa isifundo kuphela. Azicarshangwa kwanhlobo ekutheni kufundiswe ngazo. kokwabela izimali ezilimini ezimbili noma ezinrarhu okufundiswa ngazo.
