Ingasonjululwa kanjani inkinga yolimi lomdabu kwezemjundo? Ngokwemvelo umbuzo wolimi lomdabu ungaphendulwa kodwa 
lokhu kungenzeka uma bona abantu abangama-Afrika beyixazulula. Isixazululo singukuthi ulimi aluqale lusetshenziswe. Isixazululo 
sibonakala silula ngenjulalwazi kodwa uma sekufanele kwenziwe kuba nezihibe; ngokomlando, ngokomqondo; ngokwesiko; ngokwepolitiki nangokomnotho. Njengoba sakwazi ukumelana nobugqila, ukulunjwa, ukubandlululwa njIl, impi manje esibhekene nayo yileyo yokukhulula izingqondo zethu naleyo futhi yamasiko sizikhulule kuyona njengoba ihambisana nokuqwebuka kwe-Afrika. Impumelelo yakho konke lokhu isekutheni kufanele laziwe iqhaza lolimi lomdabu kwezemfundo. Lesi siphakamiso solimi lokufundisa sibuyela emuva eziphakamisweni ezibekwe i-UNESCO ngesikhathi kuhlangenwe eParis ngo~yaka we-1951 lapho 
khona yathi: 	. ':', 
  Ngokwemfundo, siphakamisa ukuthi ukusetshenziswa kolimi lokuqala lomntwanalulimi Iwebele kwelulwe. Izingane mazifundiswe ngolimi Iwazo ngoba ziluzwa kahle, futhi ukuqala ngalo esikoleni kuzovala igebe phakathi kwekhaya nesikole (UNESCO 1953: 47-8). 
  Amazwe afana no-Asia, Zambia, Nigeria ayesebenzisa is iN gisi ekuqaleni nje ngesikhathi umntwana engena esikoleni. Sebekushinrshile lokho manje, sebeqalisa imfundo ngolimi lomdabu iminyaka emithathu kuphela bese kungena isiNgisi. IGhana neSierra Leone nayo seyiqalise ukulandela lolu hlelo. Izingane ziyashesha ukubamba ezikufundiswayo uma zifunda ngolimi Iwazo. Iqhaza lolimi kwezemfundo kufanele luxoxwe luhambisane nale 
* Ulimi nokuthuthuka kokuqonda kwengane. 
* Izindlela zokusebenzisa ulimi olulodwa noma eziningi. 
* Ubuqorho borhisha nezinsizakufundisa. 
* Ulimi nokubaluleka kwemfundo emphakathini. 
Ulimi nokuthuthuka kokuqonda kwengane 
  Kwenziwa ucwaningo emazweni afana noNigeria (1970), iMali (1985), iNingizimu Afrika (1990) kwatholakala ukuthi uma kusetsheziswa ulimi lomntwana ekuqaleni emfundweni kuba nomphumela omuhle. Lapho kwasebenza khona ulimi okungelona olwebele kubantwana kwaba nezinkinga. Okuyiyonanro ebonakala ingaba isixazululo kwezemfundo ubuliminingi. Umbiko ovela ku South African Threshhold Project uthi izingane azikwazanga ukuchaza ngesiNgisi ukuthi yini ezabe ziyifunda ngolimi Iwazo; azikwazanga fu,thi ukuchaza ngolimi Iwazo ukuthi yini ezabe ziyifundile ngesiNgisi (Luckett 1994: kucashunwe kuDAE 1996: 11). Lolu cwaningo Iwenziwa naseTanzania. Izingane ezazi isiSwahili njengolimi 
Iwazo lokuqala zazibuzwa imibuzo ngeSwahili ziphendule kahle, kodwa 
uma zibuzwa umbuzo of ana yo ngesiNgisi kwakuba yinkinga ukuphendula. E-Afrika yonke kutholakala ukuthi akekho uthisha oyaye angabuyeli olimini lwabantwana uma ebona ukuthi umbuzo awubuzayo ngesiNgisi awuzwakali. Ngenye indlela inro eyosiza emfundweni e-Afrika ubuliminingi. Abantwana kumele bafunde ngezilimi ezahlukene ukuze kuvaleke igebe eliba khona uma besebenzisa ulimi olulodwa. 
Ubuqotho bothisha kanye nezinsizakujundisa 
Kuba yinkinga ukuthatha abantwana uvele ubaqalise olimini 
IwesiNgisi kungelona ulimi Iwabo. Okutholakayo ukuthi othisha abaningi abafundisa ezikoleni ezisemazingeni aphansi emfundo abasazi kahle isiNgisi: Ukusikhuluma nokusibhala. Ngesikhathi bedlulisela ulwazi lwabo ngesiNgisi esisezingeni elingelihle kwezinye i~ifundo, kuba khona umphumela om ubi emfundweni. Othisha bagcina sebesolana bebodwa ukuthi ongaphambilini akafundisanga kahle njl!. Bamgbose (2000: 79) 
   Nakho ukufundisa ngolimi lomdabu iminyaka emithathu yokuqala kunazo izinkinga ezidalwa izilimi zezigodi ikakhulukazi uma abafundi bekhuluma ulimi Iwesigodi olungafani nolimi okufundiswa ngalo. Ukwazi ulimi akusho ukuthi wena uzoba nguthisha oqotho walolo limi. Bonke othisha abafundisa ulimi, okungaba isiN gisi noma izilimi zomdabu kufanele bazazi izindlela zokufundisa ulimi ngokujwayelekile noma zokufundisa 1010  




Ulimi nokufimeleka kwezemjundo 
   Kuyabonakala ukuthi iqhaza lolimi emfundweni into ebinganakiwe isikhathi eside phambilini e-Aftika. Iqiniso-ke ukuthi abahlaziyi bezomnotho/nabahlaziyi bezepolitiki baluyekelele lolu daba ngesizathu sokufuna ukuthi baluxoxe bodwa udaba Iwentuthuko. UBamgbose (2000) uqhamuke nemiphumela emithathu yenqubomgomo yolimi e-Afrika. 
I.) Ukuthow izinjongo zezemjundo: Imfundo yamazinga aphansi yandisa ulwazi lwabafundi. Izikole nothisha babalulekile emphakathini ukwenza lokhu. 
2.) Ulimi nentuthuko: Ulimi lomdabu lubalulekile emfundweni ukuze abantu bathuthuke. 
3.) Amalungelo Dlimi: Ilungelo lokuthola imfundo ngolimi Iwakho. 
Uma uncisha umntwana ilungelo lokufunda ngolirni lwakhe, ulwa nobuzwe besiko lakhe, kanjalo namagugu omntwana. 
Lolu daba lungena kakhulu ngaphansi kwamalungelo esintu. 
Umthethosisekelo wezwe laseNingizimu Afrika unikeza izakhamizi ilungelo lokuthola imfundo ngolimi lwazo. UPerry (2004) wenza ucwaningo olunzulu ngamalungelo olimi kanye nepolitiki yobuhlanga. Kulolu cwaningo lwakhe, ugxeka kakhulu iBhodi Yezilimi Zonke ZaseNingizimu Afrika. 
Ukuthuthukiswa kwezilimi kanye nokusetshenziswa kwazo 
  Ulimi oluthuthukile yilolo oluba nobhalomagama olubhalwe phansi, lusetshenziswe kwezemfundo, lusakazwe, lushicilelwe emaphephandabeni. Ulimi olungathuthukile a1unalo uhlelo lobhalomagama olwanele, (ngaleyo ndlela lolu limi luhle lukhunywa nje kuphela), ukungabi khona kwamagama anele (lokhu kudala isimo lapho ulimi kuthiwe alukillungele ukuba ngelokufunda nokufundisa), olungenazo izinsizakufunda. Izibonelo zezilimi ezinjena imvamisa kuba izilimi zezigodi. Ulimi olungeke lukwazi ukuthi luthuthuke uma lusetshenziswa ezindaweni ezincane, angeke futhi lube namagama, lunothe, lube nemibhalo uma lungathuthukiswa. Okudinga ukuthi kwenzeke ukusetshenziswa kwezilimi zomdabu kuzona zonke izinto okukhulunywa ngazo nakuzona zonke izindawo, ngaphandle kwalokhu ngeke kuphumelele lutho. Ulimi ludinga ukusetshenziswa ukuze luthuthuke (UNESCO working document, 1997: 13) 
lzinkinga zolimi eNingizimu Afrika 
zabantu bomdabu ezingakulungele ukusetshenziswa ezikhungweni ezahlukene zemfundo, ubunzima bokwenza ubuliminingi bungabi inganekwane, iqhaza lepolitiki ezilimini kanye nendlala yabasebenzi bolimi. Uma sibuka ukukhonya kwesiNgisi, sona sigcizelelwa kakhulu njengoba phela besivele siwulimi olusemthethweni eNingizimu Afrika isikhathi 
eside. Kwezemfundo nje yisona esibhula amaphiko ngoba izincwadi 
eziningi zibhalwe ngaso. Lokhu kwenza isimo sokuthi labo abangasazi isiNgisi bavimbeleke ekufundeni ulwazi oluthile. Lokhu akugcini kuphela kwezemfundo kodwa kuze kufike ngisho emathubeni ezomnotho. Yingakho kubalulekile ukuthi izilimi zomdabu zithuthukiswe ukuze zibe izilimi zomnotho. Umthelela wokukhonya kwesiNgisi ugcina sewenza ukuthi abantu abaningi bangakwazi ukubamba iqhaza kwezepolitiki bese-ke bekhishwa inyumbazane futhi basetshenziselwe izinhloso zabanye. 
Uma kubhekwa isimo sezili'mi zabantu bomdabu eNingizimu Afrika, 
u Webb (2002) uthi azikulungele ukusetshenziswa ezikhungweni ezahlukene zemfundo. Lesi simo siyalungiswa manje yizikhungo ezahlukene zemfundo ephakeme. UMnyango wezeMfundo eNingizimu Afrika ubambisene nezwe laseNorway bakhiphe uxhaso lwezimali banikeza izikhungo zemfundo ephakeme ukuthi mazithuthukise izilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme ukuze ngokuhamba kwesikhathi ziqale zisetshenziswe njengezilimi zokufunda nokufundisa. Enye yezinhloso ngalolu xhaso ukuthuthukisa abanye othisha abazofundisa izilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika njengolimi lwesibili. Akugcini lapho kuphela kodwa kuhloswe ukuthi kwakhiwe amatemu kuzona lezi zilimi emikhakheni enhlobonhlobo ukuze abafundi abayokhiqizwa ngaphansi kwalolu hlelo lwe-project ngamaNyuvesi ahlukene, bakwazi ukuba bulimimbili basebenzise ulimi lomdabu nesiN gisi uma bexhumana nabantu abazosebenza ngabo. Ezikhungweni ezinikezwe lolu xhaso singabala iNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali, iRhodes kanye neNyuvesi yaseKapa, Ndimande-Hlongwa (2008). Lezi zikhungo zontathu sezenze umsebenzi omkhulu wokwakha amatemu emikhakh"ni eyahlukene. Ukwenza nje isibonelo, eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali ukusukela ngenyanga kaMbasa onyakeni wezi-2009, Isikole Sezifundo zeNgqondo sizobe siqalisa ukufundisa izifundo ezimbili kumathathi ngesiNgisi nesiZulu. Lokhu kuzoba ingqophamlando ngoba kuzobe kuqala ukuthi kwenzeke kulo mkhakha eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali. Esikoleni sezoBuhlengikazi khona maningi amatemu akhiwe phakathi konyaka wezi-2007 nowezi-2009 azokwenza kube lula ukuhunyushwa kwemibhalo iyiswa olimini IwesiZulu. Okuhle ngalo msebenzi ukuthi uhambisana kakhulu nezinhloso zeArATAl\T 




)okuba izilimi zomnotho, okungumphumela kahulumeni wobandlululo. '\banikazi bazo lezi zilimi abakholelwa ekutheni kungafundwa ngazo dbuye zisetshenziswe kwezomnotho njl!. Izizathu ebezibekwa phambili kakhulu ngezokuthi awekho amagama anele. Lesi sizathu siphelelwa ' risikhathi manje njengoba asekhona manje amagama noma amatemu 
futhi uyaqhubeka umkhankaso wokuwakha. Esikhathini esiphambili bekuthiwa zilungele ukusetshenziswa emakhaya, noma uma kunemigubho yamasiko nasesontweni kuphela. Kuningi kakhulu okumele kushintshe noma kubuyekezwe, ukwenza nje isibonelo, sidinga ukubuyekeza ukufundiswa kwesiZulu njengolimi lokuqala. Kungagcini lapho kodwa futhi kubuyekezwe izinsizakufunda nezinsizakufundisa, Uhulumeni ubeke izinhlaka ezahlukene ukuze zikwazi ukuthi zithuthukise ubuliminingi bungabi nje inganekwane, Kuxoxiwe-ke ngalezi zikhungo esahlukweni sesikhombisa. Kwesinye isikhathi lezi zikhungo ziba manqikiiiqika ukwamukela amalungelo ezilimi ezahlukene. Kwezemfundo isiNgisi umakhonya njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa. Amaphephandaba amaningi asebenzisa isiNgisi. Kufanele samukele ubuliminingi sihloniphe ezinye izilimi sibe nolwazi lwazo. 
Ulimi Kwezemfundo 
Elinye lamaphephandaba aseNingizimu Mrika (iRapport ngo 27 
February 2000) labika ukuthi isimo semfundo sibi kakhulu ngoba amaphesenti ama- 5% kuphela abafundi abaphumelela umatekuletsheni ngamalengiso. Ngonyaka we-1999 kubafundi abayizi- 20 000 abaphumelela ezifundweni zesayensi bayizi- 3000 kuphela ababensundu. Isimo esifana nalesi sibangwa yimithetho yoMnyango Wezemfundo encike ekutheni othisha banikezwe izamba zemali yabo kuthiwe abasriye uma bengasathandi ukufundisa baziyele komathandanhliziyo. Lesi sinq~mo sokushiya sathathwa ngothisha abanamakhono abaziyo ukuthi bangathola imisebenzi kalula kwezinye izindawo. Abaningi basusiwe ezikoleni ababefundisa kuzona ngoba beshaywa umthetho we (PPN). 
  Imithetho yolimi eyakhishwa ngesikhathi sobandlululo nayo yaba nomthelela entuthukweni kwezemfundo. Kungenziwa isibonelo ngomthetho wemfundo yabantu. 
Imfihlo entsha ngemfundo 
Uma kubhekwa imfundo ngokohlelo lwemfundo-mphumela (OBE)  
   Imfundo-mphumela ihlelwe ngendlela yokuthi kube khona imiphumela ethile yalokho okufundwayo. I-SAQA iqhamuke nale miphumela eyisikhombisa ebalulekile: 
1.) Ukuthola nokusombulula izinkinga nokuthatha izinqumo 
    usebenzisa amasu okugxeka nawokucabanga ngokwakha. 2.) Ukwazi ukusebenza nabanye njengelungu leqembu. 
3.) Ukuhlela nokuphatha kahle ngesikhathi kwenziwa umsebenzi. 4.) Ukuqoqa, uhlaziye, uhlele ulwazi ngokwakha. 
5.) Ukuxhumana ngokusebenzisa izimpawu, amakhono olimi ezimweni ezahlukene. 
6.) Ukusebenzisa isayensi kanye nobuchwepheshe ngokuyikho. 7.) Ukukhombisa ukuqonda umhlaba. 
Ulimi njengethuluzi lentut!;uko kwezemfundo 
   Kuyinto ebalulekile ukuthi 'kuWolwe amakhono olimi adingekayo kanye nokuthuthukisa ulwazi, ukuqonda kanye namakhono abafundi. Lokhu kudinga ubudlelwano obukhona phakathi kolimi kanye nokuqonda, okuzosetshenziswa uma sekukhulunywa empikiswaneni ngolimi lokufunda nokufundisa. Kunamaphuzu ayisithupha abalulekile obudlelwano phakathi kolimi nokuqonda okufundwayo. 
I.) Ukwazi izincazelo zamagama okungumongo wokufunda nokwazi ukusebenzisa igama lela ezindaweni ezahlukene. 
2,) Ukwazi ukucabanga: ngokwezibalo, ngokomlando, ngokolimi njl!. 3.) Urn fundi kufanele akwazi ukuthi ethule imiqondo ephikisayo noma egxekayo ngendlela eyamukelekile. Akwazi ukubona ubudlelwano bemibuzo esebenzisa amagama afana nalawa: chaza, xoxa, qhathanisa, gxeka, nikeza njl!. 
4.) Abafundi kufanele bakwazi ukufunda incwadi ngokuqonda bakhe isithombe salokho abakufundayo, babone amaphuzu asemqoka 
	kanye nalawo alekelelayo, njl!. 	..~ 
5.) Abafundi kufanele bakwazi ukuxhumana ngesikhathi kufundwa. 6.) Ulimi luyigugu, yilona esethula ngalo imizwa yethu, isiko lobuzwe bomuntu njl!.

Umbuzo obalulekile ngowokurhi kungani kuthandwa/kuqokwe isiNgisi lapha eNingizimu Mrika njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa? 
* Ukurhola umsebenzi. 
* Yilona limi lomsebenzi. 
* Is iN gisi ulimi lomhlaba. 
* Sinamandla . 
* Uyahlonipheka uma usikhuluma.

* Lukuvulela amathuba amaningi nokwazi ukufinyelela olwazini 
oluphathelene namalungelo. 
* Kufanele kwenyuswe izinga lolwazi IwesiN gisi. 
* Izilimi zomdabu azinabo ubugugu bokuba izilimi zomnotho. 
* Azinakho konke lokhu okubalwe ngenhla. 
* Izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika zizokhurhaza ukwahluJana kwezinhlanga okuyinto ephikisana nohulumeni wentando yeningi lapha eNingizimu Mrika. 
  Abafundi abansundu balwazi kangakanani ulimi IwesiN gisi? Bangakwazi yini ukubhekana nezinselelo zemfundo-mphumela? Kutholalrala ukurhi abafundi abaningi banenkinga ngolimi lwesiN gisi, abakwazi ukubamba iqhaza ngendlela efanelekile ezingxoxweni ezindlini zokufundela. Ngizokwenza isibonelo esicashunwe encwadini kaWebb (2002) lapho esenzele khona isibonelo somfundi osesikhungweni semfundo ephakeme futhi enguthisha wesiNgisi esikoleni esisezabelweni. Lo mfundi wayephendula umbuzo othi: Yiliphi iqhaza elibanjwa ukukhumbula ekufundiseni ulimi Iwesibili? 
Uma kuhlazinywa impendulo yomfundi kwatholakala ukurhi 
umfundi wayesebenzisa amagama esiNgisi ngendlela engeyona. Lokhu okwadala ukuthi kulahleke impendulo yombuzo ayil?hala. Ekugcineni umbuzo obuziwe awuphendulekanga. UWebb (2002) noMazrui (2002) banomqondo wokuthi imithetho yolimi emazweni aseSub-Saharan Mrika idala ingcindezi entuthukweni yolimi e-Mrika. Lapha eNingizimu Mrika ukungasazi kahle is iN gisi kube nemiphumela enqala kwezemfundo: 
* Ukushiya isikole kwabafundi. 
* Ukuphumelela ngamazinga aphansi kubafundi 
njengokwejwayelekile: 
* Ukungaphumeleli kahle emfundweni ephakeme. 
* Ukungakwazi ukuqhubekela phambili. 
* Ukungazethembi. 
* Ukushayisana kwamasiko. 
   Kungabe ukusershenziswa kwezilimi zomdabu njengezilimi zokufunda nokufundisa akusilona yini isu elihle? 
* Izilimi zomdabu yizona ezibaluleke kalthulu emfundweni uma ubheka amaphuzu asebekiwe ngezinkinga zokungaqokwa kolimi IwesiNgisi. 
* Izizathu zokuqoka izilimi zomdabu zinqala ngoba abafundi bomdabu bangabe bezazi futhi beziqonda kahle .. 
* Imfundomphumela (OBE) nayo ingasebenza kahle . 
* Abazali bangakwazi ukurhi bazibandakanye emfundweni 
	yabantwana babo. 	, 
* Kungaba khona ukuzwana nokuqonda ngokwamasiko. 
* Kunemibuzo ekhona-ke ngeqhaza lolimi lomdabu kwezomnotho, kunemibuzo ehlala ibuzwa mayelana nesinsizakufunda/isa ezanele amagama njl!. Lokho akuyona inkinga ngoba uma uhulumeni ezimisele ngokurhuthukisa nokusebenzisa ulimi olurhile angeke ayeke ukukhipha uxhaso lwemali ukwenza lokho. 
* Emfundweni yamakliono, ukuqonda kanye nolwazi akuncikile olimini. Uma sewuwafundile ungakwazi ukuwadlulisela kwabanye nganoma yiluphi ulimi. 
* Okubi nje ukurhi abazali abazi kahle ngeqhaza lolimi emfundweni nezimpikiswano ezikhona ngolimi. 
* Okufanele ukuthi kuqondwe ukurhi ukusetshenziswa kolimi lomdabu akusho ukuthi ukwamukelwa noma ukufundwa kwesiN gisi akuphele. 
   Kunezihibe ezintathu ezikhona ekusebenziseni izilimi zomdabu njengezilimi zokufunda nokufundisa: 
1.) Izinga lezilimi zomdabu emphakathini. 
2.) Ukuxhumana kwezilimi zomdabu nemithetho yolimi yobandlululo. 
3.) Ulimi lomdabu uma lwenziwa ulimi lokufnnda nokufundisa lokho kusho ukurhi kubukelwa phansi abantu abansundu eNingizimu Mrika.

Ziningi-ke izinto okufanele ziqashelwe uma kuthathwe isinqumo sokusebenzisa izilimi zomdabu njengezilimi zokufunda nokufundisa: Isimo sasekhaya, izinga lemfundo labazali, isimo saselokishini nesasemakhaya, ukugqugquzelwa kwabafundi, ubuqotho bothisha k'anye nokubaluleka kwezilimi emphakathini. Izindlela ezingalandelwa ekuqokeni ulimi olufanele njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa. UFasold (1984) simcaphuna ku Webb (2002: 193) uphakamise imibuzo emithathu yokuqala, Ion a wesine ufakwe ngu Webb ngoba ewubona ubalulekile futhi ufanele ukubuzwa uma kuqokwa ulimi lokufunda nokufundisa: 
I.) Kungabe ulimi 1010 luzokwazi yini ukwenza umsebenzi? Lubhaliwe yini phansi, seluyaziwa yini, akhona amagama obuchwepheshe, izincwadi zokufundisa nezinye nje izinsizakusebenza zikhona yini? 2.) Kungabe inqubomgomo yolimi 1010 lokufunda nokufundisa izokwenziwa isebenze ngempela? Bakhona othish:i-aoazofundisa? 
3.) Kungabe inqubomgomo yolimi iyahambisana yini nezidingo zomphakathi? Abafundi bazovuma yini ukuthi kusetshenziswe 1010 limi, ulimi 1010 lwamukelekile yini, izinga lolimi yini, ulimi luzobahlanganisa yini abantu? 
4.) Kungabe umfundi ulwazi kahle yini 1010 limi, angakwazi ukuthi asebenzise ikhono lakhe kulolo limi? 
  Kunesidingo esikhulu socwaningo mayelana nolimi lokufunda nokufundisa eNingizimu Aftika. Kufanele kuqwashiswe abafundi, othisha, izingane kanjalo namalungu amakomidi ezikole ngokubaluleka kolimi emfundweni.

thi ezihlanganele wodwa nje kodwa uzwe ekhala emuka ngolimi lukaJoji. 
  UMamphela Ramphele (2009) uhlaba ikhwelo lapha ekhuluma khona igokuthi ekugcineni abantwana bethu sebehola umvuzo wokuyekelelwa :wezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika. Ukhala kakhulu ngokuthi izilimi zomdabu ase-Mrika ziyekelelwa kakhulu futhi zibukelwa phansi enkululekweni 'aseNingizimu Mrika. Ubuza ukuthi siyaye sizibuze yini ukuthi kungani baholi bamaShayina namaJaphani beqikelela ekutheni basebenzise izilimi .abo? Isikhathi esiningi bayatolikelwa, yize noma besazi isiNgisi. Uthi lokhu ,akwenziswa ukuthi bageina ubugugu bezilimi zabo nokwazisa amazwe abo, ,ho kwakhala nyonini kithina sizwe esinsundu? Uyaqhubeka ngokukhala Igokungasetshenziswa kahle kwentando yabantu ekwenzeni inqubomgomo 'olimi isebenze. Ukhala ngesinqumo esathathwa sokuthi abazali abangazi utho ngezinqubo zolimi kuthiwe yibona okumele bathathe isinqumo 19o1imi okumele kufundiswe ngalo ezikoleni. Ihlazo lamahlaio ngoba phela aba bazali basuke bengatshelwanga wonke amaqiniso, bona-nje bazibonela lbantu abenza imisebenzi emihle kuyilabo abakhuluma isiNgisi noma .siBhunu okunye abakwazi. 
  Ezinye zezinto ezibulala ulimi ngabazali abafundile abenza imisebenzi ~semazingeni aphezulu abajabulayo uma abantwana babo bengakwazi ukukhuluma izilimi zomdabu, aze alikhiphe umzali athi phela usibanibani lliakwazi ukukhuluma isiZulu. Lokhu-ke kuyizibonelo zokubulala ulimi lugeine ngempela selushabalele. 
Kuphinde kuveze e1inye ieala ebelinganakiwe ngeqhaza lomeulo ekuqwashiseni ngezimo ezibalulekile zempilo ikakhulukazi zolimi. Kuningi okumele kwenziwe ukuze kuliwe nalesi sihlava esingenisile kubantu bakithi. 
  INhlangano Yezizwe Ezihlangene yenza isiphakamiso sokuthi kwakhiwe Isikhungo Sase-Mrika Sezilimi (African Academy of Languages) enqanyulelwa ngokuthi i-ACALAN. Ngenyanga kaNtulikazi onyakeni wezi-2001 bahlangana eLusaka, eZambia nokuyikhona lapho lesi sikhungo samukelwa ngokusemthethweni (Alexander 2008: 8). INhlangano Yomhlab'uhlangene vakueaeisa-ke ukubaluleka kwezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika njengamathuluzi 


Ezinye zezinhlosongqangi ze-ACALAN (2002) njengoba zibalulwe emthethweni wayo, ukuthuthukisa izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika ngokuqinisa ubudlelwano phakathi kwamazwe ase-Mrika; Ukuthuthukisa izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika ezikhungweni zonke zemfundo nasezingeni lomhlaba. Okunye futhi okuhloswe i-ACALAN ukumuthukisa izinhlangano zezilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika ezwenikazi i-Mrika. Umsebenzi wayo-ke ubanzi impela ngoba ubandakanya ukuqhuba ucwaningo ngezilimi zomdabu zaseAfrika kusetshenziswana nezikhungo zocwaningo ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme. Yiyona futhi ebhekele ukusatshalaliswa kwemiphumela yocwaningo ngesayensi yezilimi; inikeze usizo ngokuqeqeshwa kwabacwaningi; iphucule amathuluzi asetshenziswayo ekuthuthukiseni ubuehwepheshe bezilimi ukuze kuvalwe igebe l!,buehwepheshe bamakhompyutha; ukuthumukiswa kwezilimi zomdabu zase-Afrika njengezilimi zokufunda nokufundisa kuwona wonke amazinga emfundo. Kungeminye yemisebenzi ye-ACALAN ukunikeza imiklomelo izikhungo kanye nabantu ababambe iqhaza ekuthuthukisweni kwezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika. I-ACALAN isebenza ngezinhlaka ezinhlanu ezilandelayo: 
a.) Ingqungquthela Yomhlab'uhlangene yoNgqongqoshe bamasiko; b.) Ibhodi e1ilawulayo nelikhipha inqubomgomo; 
c.) Ibhodi elelulekayo ngokwesayensi; 
d.) Izigele eziqhamuka ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme; e.) Abaphathi be-ACALAN . 
Ngonyaka wezi-2002 kwathumukiswa ukufundiswa ngobuliminingi. 
Ngonyaka olandelayo kwakhuthazwa intuthuko yezilimi zonkana. 
Ngonyaka wezi-2004 kwakubhekwa ukufundiswa kolimi kubantwana abasebaneane. Ngonyaka wezi-2005 kwabhekelwa ukubhalwa kwezilimi ngohlobo lwebraille kanye nolimi oluhunyushwa ngezimpawu. UNdimande-Hlongwa (2006) evula umgubho wesibili wamasiko eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali ophikweni oluseMgungundlovu, waveza ukuthi unyaka wezi-2006 wabekwa ngokusemthethweni yiNhlangano Yezizwe Ezihlangene eyaziwa ngokuthi Umhlaba'uhlangene njengonyaka.wezilimi zomdabu zaseMrika. Ukwenziwa kube semthethweni konyaka wezi- 2006 njengonyaka wezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika kwakhishwa ngamhla zingama-23 enyangeni kaMasingana 2006 e-Khartoum, eSudan. U-Alexander (2008: 9) uthi ngenxa yokubambezeleka okuthile ekusebenzeni kahle ngonyaka wezi-2006 kwabe sekululwa isikhathi ukuze nangawo unyaka wezi-2007 kuqhutshekwe nomkhankaso wokubungaza izilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika. Ezinye zezinto ezenziwa ukubungaza unyaka wezi-2006 njengonyaka wezilimi zomdabu zase-Mrika, zibandakanya ukwethulwa ngokusemthweni kwemisebenzi

ingqungquthela yamazwe omhlaba nokunye okuningi. 
  Izili~i wmda~u zase-Afrika zibaluleke kakhulu uma kukhulunywa ngamaslko, UbUClko, umculo, kanye namagugu. INyuvesi yaKwaZuluNat~i yamukela ngokusemthethweni inqubomgomo yayo yolimi kanye neqhmga lokuqhuba umsebenzi ngamhla zi-2 enyangeni kaNcwaba onyakeni wezi- 2006 ngawo 10 nyaka, okwaba yinto enhle ngoba lona kwabe kungunyaka lapho kwakubungazwa khona izilimi wmdabu zaseMtik~ ~~wenikazi i-Mrika nasemhlabeni wonke. INyuvesi yaKwaZuluNatal! lz!bophezele ekuthuthukiseni nasekusebenziseni isiZulu njengolimi lokufunda nokufundisa, kanjalo nokuphatha. 
  Ephawula ngohlelo lolimi Iwase-Mrika u-A1exander (2008: 9) wathi kunohlelo Iweziqu zeMA kanye newBudokotela okunguhlelo oluhlose ukunikeza usiw Iwezimali kubafundi basezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme ukuze kwandiswe abacwaningi bezilimi wmdabu ezwenikazit-Mrika. Lolu hlelo-ke lwenganyelwe yiNyuvesi yaseYounde eCameroon kanti luqale ngonyaka wezi-2008 e-Addis Ababa kanye naseKapa. Waphinda wabalula ukuthi i-ACALAN inohlelo lokwakhiwa kwamatemu olwenganyelwe Isikhungo Socwaningo sesiSwahili eDar es Salaam. Olunye uhlelo olukhona olokuhumusha, lona-ke Iwenganyelwe i-ACALAN eBamako. Inhloso enkulu ngeyokuthi kube khona isizinda lapho imibhalo ehunyushiwe iwgcinwa khona. Igcizelela kakhulu nokuhunyushwa kwemibhalo yobuciko. Lapho singabala iminxa efana namanoveli, izindaba ezimfushane kanye nemidlalo. Ngesikhathi kubhalwa Ie ncwadi lolu hlelo belunenkinga ngasezimalini. Olunye uhlelo olwenganyelwe i-PRAESA eNyuvesi yaseKapa yilolo 
olubizwa nge The Stories Across Africa (StAM). Inhlosonqangi yalolu hlelo ukubhala izincwadi ezintathu ngezindaba zase-Mrika bese zihunyushelwa ezilimini ezahlukene wmdabu zase-Mrika. Lezi zincwadi kuhloswe ngazo ukuthi zifundwe emazingeni aphansi ezemfundo. Se~,!setshenziwe impela kulolu hlelo ngokusho kuka-A1exander (2008: 10). Izinhlelo ezimbili ze-ACALAN zisingethwe nguMphathi uqobo we-ACALAN u-Adama Samassekou. 
  Unyaka wezi-2008 yiwona owahlonzwa Yindlu Yezigele Yenhlangano Yomhlaba'uhlangene njengonyaka Wezilimi Emhlabeni Wonke. UNgubane (2009) wathi 10 mbono wavezwa isehlakalo sokubulawa kwabafundi baseNyuvesi yaseBangladesh ngonyaka we-1952 eDhaka ngenxa yokulwela ulimi IweBengal ukuthi Iwamukelwe njengolimi olusemthethweni nguhulumeni wasePakistani. Uhulumeni wasePakistani wawumemezele ulimi lwesi-Urdu njengolimi olusemthethweni. 
Kllhollliekile ukuthi sazi ukuthi singobani thina futhi siqhamukaphi, 
luyithi uqobo. Uma singalwazi ulimi Iwethu, silubukela phansi, lokho akwehlukile nokuzibukela phansi thina. Kuyathokozisa ukuthi isiZulu sifundwa ezikhungweni eziningi zemfundo ephakeme emazweni aphesheya kwezilwandle njengakulezi zikhungo ezilandelayo: Pennsylvania, Yale, 
Emory, Florida, Georgia, Illinois, Indiana, Michigan State, Ohio, Wisconsin-Madison naseCalifornia. Lokhu kuyinkomba yokuthi ulimi IwesiZulu ungasebenza ngalo ngisho sewungaphandle kwaseNingizimu Mrika, alugcini nje eNingizimu Mrika noma emazweni angcimakhelwane kodwa luwela izilwandle. Ngaphezu kwalokhu, inhlangano yothisha bezilimi wmdabu zase-Afrika eMelika eyaziwa ngokuthi i-African Language Teachers Association (ALTA) yenze umsebenzi omangalisayo ngaphansi kobuholi bukaSekela Mengameli wenhlangano uDokotela uNonhlanhla Mbeje. Yathatha isinqumo ngonyaka wezi-2007 sokuthi engqungqutheleni yayo yaminyaka yonke ivumele ukuthi kube khona amaphepha ethulwa ngezilimi wmdabu zase-Mrika. Lokhu kuqhubekile ngonyaka wezi-2008. Nakuwo 
10 nyaka wezi- 2009 kusawki-enzeka. N gaphezu kwalokho, la maphepha abhalwe ngezilimi wmdabu azoshicilelwa kujenali yenhlangano ebizwa ngokuthi i-JALTA.
